 śrīmat veṅkaṭa nātha deśika maṇi prajñā sarit taraṅga paramparā pariṇāma bhūtam nyāya pariśuddhi abhidhānam prabandha ratnam idam jayati jīvitam iva nyāya vistarasya vidyā sthānasya śrī bhagavat rāma anuja muni vara kṣuṇṇa vartmanaḥ  brahma mī māṃsā śāstrasya ca anupajīvya ca idam vidyā sthānam kaḥ  vibhavaḥ sa panditum api śeṣasya vidyā sthāna jātasya sarvam eva hi loke śrutam saṃśaya viparyayābhyām āhita pāriplavam vātyāspṛṣṭam iva tṛṇa śakalam na kathañcid api pratitiṣṭhati pramāṇa parīkṣayā tu yathāvat upapāditayā dṛṣadā iva vyapoḍha vikṣobham niṣkampam avatiṣṭhate pramāṇa parīkṣā eva ca prathama avatāra padavī nyāya vistarasya pada vākya pramāṇa bhedena hi tredhā vibhajanti śāstram śāstra vidaḥ tatra tad am nāma śabda anuśāsanam pāṇini ādi praṇītam vākyam cavicāra pūrvaka śrauta vākya artha nirṇaya rūpam karma brahma ātmaka viṣaya vibhāga vibhaktam ubhayam mīmāsā śāstram pramāṇam tukvacid api artheṣu anavagāḍha avaṣṭambhām sva ātmani api anupajāta visrambhām ḍolāyamānām buddhim kareṇum iva tarka śṛṅkhalābhiḥ ālānayat manana vyapadeśam śāstram yasya saṃjñā antaram nyāya vistaraḥ tarka śāstram ityādi tad etad pramāṇa pradhānam api pramāṇa gateḥ prameya svarūpa vivecana paryavasāna tayā prameyepi nyasta padam pravṛttam itaretara visaṃvāda saṃrabdha uddhuraiḥ āstikaiḥ nāstikaiḥ ca bahudhā vādibhiḥ sva sva  chanda anurodhena anyathā ca anyathā ca prameyam pratipadyamānaiḥ itas tatas  parikṛṣyamāṇāni pramāṇāni api parāvṛtta rūpa tayā lakṣaṇataḥ  durgrahāṇi abhūvan māna ābhāsa vyāmiśrāṇi hi mānāni na sukarāṇi vivektum tad evam śāstram eva paṅkilīkṛtam cakṣuḥ iva timira upasṛṣṭam vigalita artha grahaṇa apāṭava saṃvṛttam aviparyasta lakṣaṇam pramāṇa vargam parigṛhṇādbhiḥ api saugata arhataka apila cārvāka jaiminīya ādibhiḥ aṅgeṣu avāntara bhedeṣu canyūna atirekam āsthitaiḥ anekadhā upayogāt anekāntī kṛta matayaḥ kṛta matayā upi sva sva upadeśa pāramparī pratyayāt ekatamam pakṣam abhimanyamānāḥ sparigraha avasāda kātara tayā pakṣa antareṣu sa abhyasūyāḥ cirāya api garu kuleṣu pariśramya alabdha buddhi prasādā vibhrāmyanta eva anubhūyante atas  sarva upayogāya doṣa guṇa hāna upādānābhyām śikṣaṇīyasya asya nyāya vistarasya pṛthak prasthānam nyāya darśanam nāma sūtra jātam gautamena muninā prathamam praṇītam yatra pramāṇa apramāṇa ādi vivecanayā tattva nirṇaya upāyāḥ tatra ca saṃbhavantaḥ  guṇa doṣāḥ kathāsu ca grāhyā parihārya vibhāgāḥ sa viśeṣam pradarśitāḥ tad ca nyāya darśanam prathamam pramāṇa prameya ādi sūtreṇa ṣoḍaśadhā padārthān vibhajya tad parīkṣaṇena caritārtham tatra prameya tvasya kevala anvayinaḥ sarva padārtha sādhāraṇa tayā vibhājaka tvam anupapadyamānam manyamānena kaṇā ādena muninā kṛtsnam eva prameya jātam dravya ādi sapta padārtha parisaṃkhyānena asaṃkīrṇam vibhaktam tatra ca sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya abhāvān vitatham eva apadārthān padārthayatā tathāvidham eva ca anyat anyat ālapatā grāhyam agṛhṇatā tyājyam ca atyajatā kaṇabhakṣeṇa dūram apathīkṛtaḥ śāstra patha iti brahmasūtra kāra ādibhiḥ pratikṣiptaḥ  vaiśeṣikaḥ pakṣaḥ nyāya pakṣaḥ tu śaṅkyamāna upasarga upi kathañcid vyākhyāna ādheya saṃskāra tayā na atyartha parivarjanīyaḥ iti manyamānāḥ katipaya saṃskāra saṃskṛtam imam pakṣam parigṛhya nibandhān nibabandhuḥ pūrve kecid ācāryāḥ te ca nibandhā eṣu divaseṣu nāmnā eva kevalam avaśiṣyantaḥ tad yathā aśrīmat nātha m uni miśra praṇītam nyāya tattvam śrīmat parāśara bhaṭṭāraka kṛtiḥ tattva ratna ākaraḥ śrī bhagavat yāmunā ācāryāṇām ācāryaiḥ śrīmat nātha muni caraṇa āśrayāṇām śrī puṇḍarīkākṣāṇām śiṣyaiḥ ca śrī rāma miśra gurubhiḥ viracitam vivaraṇam ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepaḥ ca iti grantha dvayam avidita prabandhṛ vyapadeśam nyāya sudarśanam prajñā paritrāṇām ca iti prabandha yugalam śrīmat nārāyaṇa muni viracita tvena ācārya upāttam nāmnā ca anuddiṣṭam kim api prabandha ratnam asya eva ca nyāya pariśuddhi praṇetuḥ ācāryasya ācāryeṇa mātulena ca vādi haṃsa ambuvāhaḥ iti praśasti nāma aṅkitena ātreya rāma anuja ācāryeṇa kṛtam sva pratibhā draviṇa nikṣepāyamāṇam nyāya kuliśa abhidhānam ca iti ete nibandhāḥ nyāya pariśuddhi kṛtā eva ācāryeṇa tatra tatra bhūyiṣṭham udāhriyante yad eva yāvat eva ca ācāryeṇa kvacid  kvacid udāhṛtam vākyam vākya khaṇḍam vā tad atiriktam kiyat api ṭīkā kṛtām api dṛṣṭi viṣayībhūtam na upalabhyate ayam atra hetuḥ pratibhāti ācārya saṃnihita kāleṣu api anatisaṃkṣepa vistara ramaṇīyāni prasphuṭa arthāni nitya prakāśāni ācārya śrī sūkti ratnāni avamṛśya rasa āsvāda vādi vijaya śiṣya pravacana adri pravaṇeṣu upari upari vyākhyāna ādi praṇaya naiḥ avistṛtya śāstram vitatham eva atipātita kāleṣu śiṣya praśiṣya vargeṣu kumāra vedānta ācārya ādiṣu atīte ca gaṇarātre kaiścid arva acīnaiḥ āvirbhūtaiḥ grantha kṛdbhiḥ ajñāta pūrva vṛttāntaiḥ yathā kathañcit vyākhyānena kaścid upakāraḥ kṛta iti hanta   niḥśeṣa kṣālita akhila kalaṅkasya api asya śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya idam ekam śocanīyam vaiśasam yad  tāvat ācārya pada abhiṣiktaiḥ api arvācīnaiḥ budha varaiḥ kāṇāda gautamīya ādi sāmānya śāstra pariśrameṇa vyayitavayobhiḥ antime vayasi kathañcid upajāta vedānta tṛṣṇaiḥ śiṣya saṃgrahaṇa kṛta kṣaṇaiḥ avaśya upādeya upadeśa śrībhāṣya ādi katipaya grantha grahaṇa carita arthaiḥ anādṛtāḥ prācām ācāryāṇām vāc vistarā etarhi śrotum api durlabha tām gamita arḥ idṛśoyam vidyā vadhaḥ kasya vā vidyā vyasaninaḥ na dūnoti mānasam athavā kṛtam prācām prabandha praṇāśa cintanena asya eva ācāryasya vāc madhu niṣyandaḥ  mudhā eva kiyān na visraṃsitaḥ sarva tantra svatantrāṇām ācārya caraṇānām śata adhikāḥ prabandhā hāra vimalāḥ prasiddhāḥ saṃskṛta prākṛta drāviḍa bhāṣā abhistra rauśikāni kāvya nāṭaka stotrāṇi lokaśāstra vyavahāra nirūḍha saṃskṛta vyatikīrṇa drāviḍa bhāṣā mayāni ca caturtha rāśi niviṣṭā nilaukikānām api anugrāhakāni parīkṣakāṇām api sugraha sāṃpradāyika tattva hita puruṣa arthāni ādarśa vimalāni maṇi pravāla śabditāni niyata śrāvya tayā rahasya saṃjñitāni siddhānta niṣkarṣaṇa īdaṃparāṇi loka śreyase jātāni grantha jātāni tatra vedānte tāvat  tad tvaṭīkā nāma śrī bhagavat rāma anuja muni vara viracitasya śārīrakamī māṃsa ābhāṣyasya vivṛtiḥ apūrva artha viśeṣa vinyāsa paribhūṣitā traikālya saṃbhāvanīyānām aśeṣa ākṣepāṇām acala niścayān parihāra anupadarśayantī gaṅgena gaurī guroḥ etasmāt ācārya varyāt āvirbhūtā sā ca prathama sūtra mātram api yāvat asamagra upalabdha pracārā vedānta vidyā vicāra kāṅkṣiṇām cintā vyasanāya eva khaṇḍa bhūtā paridṛśyate vicitra āyodhanā kuṇṭha śaktau tejasvini svām śakti samagram adarśayitvā eva niyati yaiyātyena akasmāt uparatam yodha ratne taṭastha dṛṣṭe kasya vā vīra dharmam anutiṣṭhataḥ  hṛdayam na dūyeta soyam asya nibandha ratnasya lope dṛṣṭāntaḥ kecid manyeran ācāryaiḥ eva na samāpūrita ayam grantha iti tad etad sva upamānena sarvatra śakti paricchedam kalayatām pralapitam atra na kramate trividhāḥ khalu loke prabandha kṛtaḥ kecid guru kula cira pariśramaiḥ anekaśas  śrutān yathāśrutam arthān patreṣu viniveśya prakāśayantaḥ  lokam anugṛhṇanti atha itare ye punar jātyā eva sphaṭika avadāta buddhayaḥ sattva viśeṣa āvirbhāva nistuṣa āśayāḥ svatas  svānta mukura tala sphuṭa saṃkrānta sarva artha praticchandā api saṃpradāya parirakṣaṇa śraddhalu tayā guru upadeśa darśitām pada vīm avarjayantaḥ citta ghaṇṭā patheṣu sama samaya saṃcarat akhila pramāṇa tarka guru upadeśa saṃpradāya viśeṣā eka helayā bhūyasā ūrthān ayatnena grahītum praṇetum api arhanti anye tu nirantara bhajana kṛta prasadanena bhagavatā sarva īśvareṇa dūra pratyūḍha pratyūha vipruṣaḥ  niḥśreyasa avadhīni kuśala jātāni anubhavitum nija caraṇa śaraṇān api anubhāvayitum cākuṇṭha śaktayaḥ tṛtīya kakṣyā niviṣṭāḥ ta ete vyāsa parāśara vālmīki pramukhaiḥ mahā ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ api gaṇanīya anubhāvā vilakṣaṇāḥ prabandha kṛtaḥ yeṣām eka pratibhā sūtra syūtāni prameya ratnāni punar  punar  pariśīlitāni api nava navāni iva prajñāvatām hṛdayeṣu kam api camatkāram āvahanti na ca kadācid  purāṇa citravat  vicchāyāni bhavanti nyāpariśuddhi kṛt ācāryaḥ tu dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ ubhayoḥ apri kakṣyayoḥ hāra āvalyoḥ iva nāyaka maṇiḥ prakāśata iti tattva vidām aparokṣam prakṛti siddham ca prakrāntasya anta gamanam śaktimatām loka anugraha mātraphalā yeṣām sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ tādṛśānām ayatna nirvartanīye loka upakāra arthe samārambhe cikīrṣita vicchedaḥ katham upapadyate evaṅguṇena ca ācārya cūḍāmaṇi pavanā śiṣya buddhim prasādayitum ārabdhā kṛtirasam āpya madhye apaviddhā bhavati iti kaḥ  nukhalu prabhāva vedī pratipattum arhati api ca nikhila nigama śreṇī cūḍā pariṣkṛti rūpiṇī nipuṇa manasām āśā saudha sthalīṣu nibadhyate yati pati bhuvaḥ  bhāṣyasya asau yathāśrata acintita pravacana vidhau  aṣṭāviṃśe jayadhvaja paṭṭikā iti sva kṛtasya bhāṣya pravacanasya aṣṭāviṃśya āmāvṛttau tattvaṭī kā nibandha praṇayanam ācāryaḥ tattvaṭīkā prārambhe svayam eva spaṣṭam āha saṃkalpa sūrya udaya prastāvanāyām ca viṃśati abde viśruta nānāvidha vidya striṃśat vāram śrāvita śārīraka bhāṣyaḥ śreyaḥ śrīmān veṅkaṭa nāthaḥ śruti pathyam nātha prītyai nāṭakam arthyam vyadhita etad  iti sūtra dhāravācā śārīraka bhāṣya pravacanam saṃkalpa sūrya udaya nirmāṇa kāle triṃśat vāra kṛtam prathayati tadānīm eva triṃśat vāram śārīraka bhāṣya pravacanam āsīt yadi tatas  paścāt  pravacana āvṛttayaḥ tatopi hi bhūyasyaḥ  bhavitum arhanti kṛṣṇa miśra samāgama kālaḥ  hi saṃkalpa sūrya udaya nirmāṇa samayaḥ tatas ca aṣṭāviṃśya āmā vṛttau tattvaṭīkā nirmāṇam kṛṣṇa miśra samāgamāt  pūrvataram bhavati śata dūṣaṇyāḥ samanantaram tad tvaṭīkā kṛtā iti ca pratīyate uktam hi svayam eva ācāryaiḥ tattvaṭīkām prakramamāṇaiḥ śātitaḥ śata dūṣaṇyām śaṅkara ādi mudhā grahaḥ śarīraka śarīram tu vyaktam atra pradarśyate iti śrutaprakāśikā bhūmau yena ādau parirakṣitā pravartitā ca pātreṣu tasmai śreṣṭhāya maṅgalam iti kumāra vedānta ācārya kṛta maṅgala āśāsana parāmarśane śruta prakāśikā pravacana tatpara tvam ācāryāṇām tattvaṭīkā pūraṇa vighātāya jātam syāt iti ca apātaram aṇīyam śru prakāśika ācāryasya himleccha bala upamarda lagnasya nija guru sabrahmacāriṇaḥ  mumūrṣataḥ prārthanayā tad grantha rakṣaṇa pravacanayoḥ aṅgīkārepi na etāvatā svakīyam mahīyāṃsam prabandha praṇayana prayatnam ācāryaḥ  vitathīkariṣyati na hmatratyam apūrvam artha jātam grantha antareṇa caritārtham bhavati tad idam ācārya granthe kṛta śramāṇām svata eva su vyaktam idānīm upalabhyamāna paryantepi tattvaṭī kā grantha khaṇḍe ye viṣayāḥ pratipādyantu na ete śruta prakāśikāyām anyatra vā grantha antare pratipattum sulabhāḥ kiñca su ācāryaiḥ vādi haṃsa ambu vāha āryaiḥ praṇīte vidyamāna eva hi nyāya kuliśa ākhye nyāya nibandha ratne nyāya pariśuddhim ācāryaḥ svayam nibabandha avaśya vaktavyeṣu ca artheṣu joṣaṃbhāvaḥ kathañcid api śāsra ācārya tāyāḥ sadṛśaḥ  na bhavati na ca nava nava artha āviṣkaraṇam arvācām prācīnācārya paribhavāya api ca nikhila nigama śreṇī cūḍā pariṣkṛti rūpiṇī nipuṇa manasām āśā saudha sthalīṣu nibadhyate iti prabandha upakrama pratijñānam eva pradarśayati grantha antaraiḥ acarita arthasya sarva vedānta artha saṃskārasya mahāmatibhiḥ api sarvajña sakāśāt śuśrūṣitasya pratipādana artham apūrvāyāḥ kṛteḥ samārambha iti sa katham na paripūryeta kiñca nija nibandhasya śruta prakāśikā rakṣaṇa aṅgīkāra samaya eva labdha prasara tām anusmṛtya parakīya grantha pravacanam aṅgīkṛtam ācāryaiḥ iti śakyam abhyūhitum tathā ca sati tattvaṭī kā grantha lopanidāna m arvācām ācāryāṇām tatra apariśīlanam eva na tu grantha apari samāptiḥ yathā hi nyāya siddha añjanam api jaḍa dravya paricche dena eva paryavasitam sāṃpratam paridṛśyate adravya paricchedaḥ tu patita eva aśakyam ca tad pūraṇam anyaiḥ ittham amum artham śrīraṅga rāma anujaguruḥ eva nyāya siddha añjana vyākhyāne na kvāpi atas  parama dṛsyata kośaśeṣa stad śeṣa pūraṇa kṛtiḥ parihāsa hetuḥ jñātavyam anyat api taiḥ niraṇāyi samya ggrantha antareṣu iti na kiñcid iha asti cintyam iti nigamayat nivedayati śatadūṣaṇī api hi na samagrā dṛśyate ṣaṭṣaṣṭiḥ eva vādā loke pracaranti śeṣe tu mithyā eva kim api aitihyam kalpayitvā katipaye prajalpanti yad tāvat dvaita mata khaṇḍana paraḥ śeṣaḥ  granthaḥ madhvamatasthena kenacid yatinā bhikṣāmaṭa tā sa vinayam upasṛtya prārthitoyam ācāryaḥ tam tasya bhikṣā arthe prāyacchid iti tad api na vicāra kṣamam na hi ācārya grantheṣu kvacid api madhvamatam nirasyate tattva viplava abhāvāt avāntareṣu ca artheṣu naiyāyika vaiśeṣika ādi pratipāditasya eva dvaitasya anuvādāt  anatipracura tayā tasya matasya loka viplava prasaṃga abhāvāt cānā sthā eva ācāryāṇām tatra syāt  atas catustriṃśat vādā madhvamata khaṇḍana parā iti kiṃvadantī mātram etad  śatadūṣaṇī ca śaṅkā ādi kṛta sūtra vyākhyāna ādi nirāsa artham eva pravṛttā iti ca tad grantha mukha eva sphuṭībhavati tatra hi prācīm upetya padavīm yati rāja dṛṣṭām tad saṃnikṛṣṭam api vā matam āśrayantaḥ prājñā yathā uditam idam śukavat  paṭhantaḥ pracchanna bauddhavijaye paritas  yatadhvam iti pratiśrutam atra atat saṃnikṛṣṭam api vā matam āśrayantaḥ iti anena dvaitinaḥ sva pakṣīkriyante advaita khaṇḍanam eva ca grantha pravṛtti prayojanam iti ca darśitam tathā cavidyā araṇya akṣobhya muni vivāde nirṇayam bruvadbhiḥ ācāryeḥ asinā tattvam asinā para jīva prabhedinā vidyā araṇya mahā araṇyam akṣobhyam uniḥ acchinat iti uktam aśātitaḥ śata dūṣaṇyām śaṅkara ādi mudhā grahaḥ iti atra tu śaṅkara ādi ityādi padam yādava bhāskarayoḥ saṃgrahāya iti sthitam tasmāt  samagra grantha adarśanamarvācām ācāryāṇām pravacana viccheda nibandhanam prabandha lopahetuḥ iti spaṣṭam etad  atra prasakta anuprasaktam ācāryasya kṛṣṇa miśra samāgama caritam kiñcid upanyasya tekṛṣṇa miśraḥ hi gauḍa deśīyaḥ paṇḍita cūḍāmaṇiḥ sarvāsu vidyāsu kalāsu ca sa viśeṣa kṛta śramaḥ kaviḥ ca brahmādvaitam siddhantam ātiṣṭhamānaḥ  vāda kutūhalitayā sarvā diśaḥ paryaṭan jita kāśī krameṇa dakṣiṇān diśamācakrāma tatra śrī raṅgam divya kṣetram viduṣām āvāsamākarṇya deva sevā apadeśena vāda samaram arthayamānaḥ śrīraṅga rājasya bhava gataḥ prāsāda m āsadāda tadānīm tatra bhāṣā mayīrgāthāḥ sa rāga tālam gīyamānā niśamya tad kartṝṇām ca kavīnām varṇa avarāṇām api pratimāḥ tasmin devālaye deva upacāraiḥ ārādhyamānā viditvā tatra sevā samavetān jñāna vṛddhān śrī vaiṣṇavān āmantrya abhoḥ prājñāḥ bhavatām anena apabhraṃśa pāṭhena varṇa avara pūjanena ca dūra apoḍham veṣṇavam tejaḥ kim anena ārādhanena anthatha akṛtam akṛtam hi bhavati iti sa ākṣepam papraccha yadā taiḥ militaiḥ api na kiñcid ākṣepa sadṛśam uttaram pratipannam tadā tad ātanāya tad deśa adhipataye tam artham āvedya pratiṣṭhā prabhṛti sarva eva ālaya saṃskāraḥ kāryaḥ pratyagra eva iti ca niyamya tam divya ālayam gāḍha ghaṭita argala dvāram parityakta aśeṣa pūjā utsavam ca kārayāmāsa loka ācārya prabhṛtayaḥ ca bahavaḥ tatra darśana guravaḥ tādṛśam vaiśasam acintita upanatam anusmṛtya durante duḥkha sāgare nimagnāḥ tam ca prativādinam sarva vidyā viśāradam vāda āhava navaśūram aprakampyam ākalayantaḥ sabhām abhinavān kām api saṃgamayya tasya anarthasya kiñcid api pratividhānam cintayāmāsuḥ tasmin mahati sadasi viduṣām saṃpradāya ācāryaḥ śrīmān loka ācāryaḥ sarveṣām sabhā sadām vadheya vacanaḥ samarthām abhyarhitām vācam ādade bhoḥ bhāgavata pradhānāḥ balavantam paripanthinam parāṅmukhīkartum upāyaḥ kaścid atra me pratibhāti sa tāvat ucyamānaḥ  bhavadbhiḥ anumanyatām asti kila kāñcyām nagaryām veṅkaṭa nāthāryaḥ  nāma viduṣām prathamaḥ sa hi vṛṣa śaila nāthasya ghaṇṭā aṃśa eva avatīrṇaḥ iti tattva vidām grahaṇam soyam pañca varṣa deśīyaḥ śiśuḥ eva san nija mātulena vādi haṃsa ambu vāhena ātreya rāma anuja ācāryeṇa śārīraka bhāṣya grahaṇāya varada guru sakāśam gacchatā priya bhāgineyena nītaḥ tatra bhāṣya viṣaye prasaktān bahūn saṃdeha śṛṅkhalā granthīn visraṃsayan  tayā tatra samavetayā prajñā vṛddha pariṣadā apūrva prasāda vismaya citrita cittayā sa bahu mānam avalokitaḥ śrīmatā ca varada guruṇā śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya daivāt  saṃprati saṃjātam avalambanam iti baddha āśvāsena apratiṣṭhāpita veda antaḥ pratikṣapta bahis mataḥ bhūyāḥ traividyamānyaḥ tvam bhūri kalyāṇa bhājanam iti āśiṣam prayuñjānena aasya kumārasya svatas  pratibhāta samasta śāstra artha sārasya vidyā saṃskāra mātra phalaḥ  guru upadeśaḥ  bhaviṣyati na tu jñāne kaścid api śakti leśa ādheyaḥ  bhavati bhagavān api hi devakī nandanaḥ vidyā grahaṇāya sāṃdī pineḥ ācāryasya sakāśe guru kula vāsam agrahīt  kim ca asya śaiśava eva ayam prajñā prakarṣaḥ  dāśaratheḥ iva vikramatiśayaḥ  janma siddhaḥ na asau puruṣa antara dṛṣṭi viṣayam prāpayitum yuktam sa abhyasūyāḥ sa vismāyā vā dṛśaḥ  na asmin bāla vayasi patitum arhanti dṛṣṭi doṣaiḥ hi viṣa analaiḥ iva prasaradbhiḥ tarava iva avalāḍhāḥ kati nāma mahā guṇāḥ puruṣāḥ sva guṇaiḥ lokam anupakṛtya eva astam gatāḥ bhavān eva amum sarva śāstreṣu kṛta prajñam kartum arhati śrī bhagavat rāma anuja siddhāntasya eṣa jayadhvajaḥ samucchrīyatām iyā ādiśya śiśuḥ asau nija mātule vādi haṃsa ambuda ācārye nyāsīkṛtaḥ atha asau vayasā viṃśati varṣa deśīya eva san sarvatomukha prasṛta prabodha tayā pareṣām anabhibhavanīyaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ evam akṣayya pratibhā draviṇena sarveṣu api ca tantreṣu nirāmayam panthānam avagantum prasādayitum ca alaṅkarmīṇena ca ācāryeṇa sārdham kadācid  kāñcī nagare devadevasya bhagavataḥ śrī devarājasya vaiśākha māsike yātrā mahā utsave vidvat saṃvāda kutūhalitayā samāgataḥ sarva pathīna vaiduṣī vibhavaḥ prabandha ratna praṇetā ca akhila śāstreṣu vidyā araṇya iti kṛta praśasti nāmadheyaḥ  mādhava ācāryaḥ  nāma veda bhāṣya kṛt vāda āhave lagnaḥ  niraṅkuśa niśita tarka śara āsāra varṣiṇaḥ ācāryasya agratas  pratyavasthātum akṣamaḥ  vismaya bahu māna bharita manā vijaya nagaram prayātaḥ sva śiṣyasya rājñaḥ tam artham yathāvṛttam āvedya tathāvidha vidvat ratna darśana utkaṇṭhā tvaritasya prabhoḥ prārthanayā chatra cāmara prabhṛti samasta rāja paribarha paribṛṃhitam rāja aupavāhya puraḥsaram pradhāna saciva hasta arpita sa bahu mānasamāhvāna lekham ca caturaṅga balam praṇīyaḥ prārthitaḥ  vairāgya pañcakam tasya pratyuttarayā añcakāra tena ca mādhava ācāryeṇa svīye sarva darśana saṃgrahe rāma anuja darśanam upakṣipatā atat uktam veṅkaṭa nāthena tattvam uktāka kalāpe iti upakramya patyuḥ saṃyaminām praṇamya caraṇau tad pāda koṭīrayoḥ saṃbandhena samidhyamāna vibhavān dhanyān  tathā anyān gurūn śuddham saṃśrita bādarāyaṇa tanoḥ nārāyaṇasya uktibhaḥ śrīmān veṅkaṭanāyakaḥ sthiti padam nirmāti nīteḥ śubham vidyā sthāneṣu dharmyeṣu gaṇyate nyāya vistaraḥ sa ca viplau  itaḥ taiḥ taiḥ tatas  atra pariśodhyate gautama sūtra bahiṣkāra pakṣaḥ yadi api kathañcid ākṣa pādam sat pakṣe nikṣeptu śakyam na ca kaṇabhakṣa pakṣa nikṣepavat  kleśaḥ na api tad kartā gautamaḥ tāmaseṣu paripaṭhyate na api ca vipralambhakatva khyātiḥ tathā api brahmasūtra kāra ādi bahiṣkṛta tvāt na atīva vayam ādriyāmahe na khalu ārṣatva ādibhiḥ tad ādaraḥ atiprasaṅgāt  prājñānām prathamena eva guruṇā hi svayam purā lokāyata matam proktam loka viplava kāraṇam athavā pitāmaha eva atra pramāṇam ya indra virocanāyoḥ cārvāka matam upadiṣṭavān tathā gautamaḥ  api saṃbhāvyate atha api kāṇāda śākya pāṣaṇḍaiḥ trayī dharmaḥ  vilopitaḥ tridaṇḍa dhāriṇā pūrvam viṣṇunā rakṣitā trayī iti smṛteḥ bahavaḥ puruṣā rājan sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇaḥ na eta icchanti puruṣam ekam kuru kula udbhava samāsena tu tad vyāsaḥ puruṣa aikātmyam uktavān iti mahābhārata ukteḥ ca yuktam tad tad bahiṣkāraḥ iha tu na tathā iti ced na tulya nyāyatayā vacanasya upalakṣaṇa artha tvāt na khalu tad vā tādṛś vā iti kaścid viśeṣaḥ yadi api kāśa kuśā avalamba nyāyena pakṣa antarāt ādhikyam asya pakṣasya atha api na tad vedānta saṃnidhau na khalu maśakāt baliṣṭhaḥ  api mātaṅgaḥ kaṇṭhīravam uparuṇaddhi yad akṣapādaḥ pravaraḥ  munīnām śamāya śāstram jagataḥ  jagāda ku tārkikā jñāna nivṛtti hetuḥ kāriṣyate tasya mayā nibandhaḥ iti vākyam akṣapāda pakṣa pātena uktam iti anāstheyam uktam ca pūrva ācāryaiḥ kāṇāda mākṣa pādam vā kāpilam tantram eva vā tantrāṇi etāni sarvāṇi na tantrāṇi ātma nirṇarya iti ata eva hi etena śiṣṭā parigrahā api vyākhyātāḥ iti sūtre bhāṣitam etena veda aparigṛhīta sāṃkhya pakṣa kṣapaṇena śiṣṭāḥ ca veda aparigṛhītāḥ kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda kṣa paṇa kabhipakṣāḥ kṣapitā veditavyāḥ iti na ca sūtra nibaddham sarvam vidyā sthānam iti niyamaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na ca eka eva ekasya vidyā sthānasya sūtrakṛt iti api vā ṛṣiḥ iti eva vā rājā ājñā anyaiḥ api ca tad karaṇa darśanāt pramāṇa śabdasya bhāve karaṇe ca vyutpattiḥ evam ca pramā eva pramāṇam iti eke pramākaraṇam eva iti apare tayoḥ anyatarat iti anye yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam pramāṇam yad ajñānāt saṃsāraḥ  yad jñānāt  tad nivṛttiḥ tad  prameyam mumukṣubhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meya tvāt  tad dvividham dravya adravya bhedāt  sāmānyatas  vā pramā viṣayaḥ prameyam āgantuka dharma āśrayaḥ  dravayam atathābhūtam adravyam dravyam dvedhā jaḍam ajaḍam iti jaḍam ca dvedhā prakṛtiḥ kāla iti ajaḍam ca tathā pratyak parāk iti pratyak api dvividham jīvar iśvara iti parāk api tathā dharma bhūta jñānam nitya vibhūtiḥ ca iti athavā dravyam dvividham ātmān ātma bhedāt  tredhā vā bhoktṛ bhogya niyantṛ śruti anusārāt  ṣoḍhā vā triguṇa kāla jīva īśvara śuddha sattvam ati bhedāt asvayaṃprakā aṃśam jaḍam svayaṃprakāśam ajaḍam miśra sattva āśrayaḥ prakṛtiḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇa lava ādi vyavahāra hetuḥ svasmai bhāsamānam pratyak parasmai bhāsamānam parāk  paratantra cetanaḥ  jīvaḥ svatantra r iśvaraḥ artha prakāśaḥ  buddhiḥ prakṛti vyatirikta tve sati sattva āśrayaḥ  nitya vibhūtiḥ adravyam anekadhā sattva śabda ādi vaicitryāt  ekam vā itara viśiṣṭam prādhānyataḥ prameyam param brahma itareṣām sva niṣṭha brahma eka niṣṭhatvāt  tasya eva ca tathā tvena mumukṣubhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meyatva śruteḥ avyavasthita vyavahāra kāraṇam jñānam saṃśayaḥ ayathāvyavahāra kāraṇam jñānam viparyayaḥ saṃskāra mātra jam jñānam smṛtiḥ tad vyatiriktam jñānam anubhavaḥ puruṣa pravṛtti uddeśyam prayojanam vyāpti adhigama sthānam dṛṣṭāntaḥ prāmāṇikatva abhimataiḥ parigṛhītoḥ athaḥ siddhāntaḥ para artha pramāṇa prayoga vākya avāntara vākyāni avayavāḥ vyāpya aṅgīkāreṇa vyāpaka aniṣṭa prasañjanam tarkaḥ tarka anugṛhīta pramāṇa pūrvaka tattva avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ vīta rāga kathā vādaḥ pakṣa dvaya sādhanavatī vijigīṣu kathā jalpaḥ pratipakṣa sthāpana hīnā tu sā vitaṇḍā hetu aṅga eka deśa vikalā hetvābhāsāḥ avivakṣita śabda artha āropeṇa dūṣaṇam chalam sva vyāpi dūṣaṇam jātiḥ kathakā śakti liṅgam nigraha sthānam iti etādṛśāni vākyāni kim na sūtrāṇi syuḥ tad iha saṃkṣiptam lakṣaṇa ādi vākyam sūtram tad udāharaṇa ādi vākyam tu bhāṣya ādikam iti vibhāvya saṃtoṣṭavyam na ca pūrva prābalya vyavasthā tad pūrva saṃbhavāt vārtikasya ca anavatāra prasaṅgāt  vyākaraṇa ādiṣu anyathā karaṇa svīkārāt ca na ca jaimineḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇa ādiṣu audāsīnya mātreṇa gautama ukteṣu kāśyapa ukteṣu vā niḥśeṣa anumati siddhiḥ iti mantavyam anya para tayā loka prasiddha upajīvanāt para kalpita taṭāka upajīvanavat  karma kāṇḍa vṛtti kārādayaḥ  api hi losiddhām pramāṇa ādi vyavasthām yathāyatham anyathā saṃjagṛhuḥ atas  yāvat iha yukti yuktam tāvat upajīvyate na khalu taṭāka sthaḥ paṅkaḥ  api apaṅkila buddhibhiḥ ta tad avagāhibhiḥ upajīvyate atas  siṃha vana gupti nyāyena yathā avasthita nyāya anugṛhītam vedam veda anumatam ca nyāyam anusarāmaḥ na punar nyāya mātram yad tu jñāta saṃbandhasya ityādi grantham upādāya anantara m uktam śrī viṣṇu citteḥ vyāpti dhīgarbha anubhavaḥ  anumānam iti arthaḥ nyāya śāstre tu tad viśeṣa nirṇayaḥ iti tad api tad nirūpaṇa adhikṛta vidyā sthāna khyāpana param pramāṇa ādi sūtram upādāya vyācakṣāṇaiḥ tad pakṣa niṣṭhaiḥ api pūrvaiḥ kvacid  sūtrāṇi nirākṛtāni tad nyāyasya na asmāsu sarpamāraḥ na api daṇḍa nivāraṇam tatas ca yathālokam yathāvedam laukike vaidike api ca yaḥ  vaktā sa parigrāhyaḥ prāktanaḥ  adyatanaḥ  api vā vivakṣita artha avaiśadyam vyākula tvam apūrṇa tā ullokatā iti amī doṣā guṇa koṭau jaḍaiḥ kṛtāḥ bhagavat na artha munibhiḥ nyāya tattva samāhvayā avadhīrya akṣa pāda ādi nyabandhi nyāya paddhatiḥ tad arvāgbhiḥ tathā ācāyaiḥ yatheṣṭam matam āsthitaiḥ praṇinye bahudhā taiḥ taiḥ pramāṇa ādi vicāraṇā tad ayam bhāṣya svaḥsa siddhaḥ  bahiṣkāra pakṣaḥ gautama sūtra svīkāra pakṣaḥ aṅgīkāra kāṅkṣiṇām akṣapādīyam api asmad ukta ekānta tayā sthāsyati tathā eva sthāpayiṣyāmaḥ atas  vayam api mahatām ayukta artha tātparya kalpanena na aparādhyema nyūna adhika viruddha vyapadeśa ādīnām alakṣaṇa lakṣaṇa uktīnām ca adhyāhāra ani aparyāmyām tad bhakteḥ api nirvāhāt  tathā asmin yatra sphuṭaḥ śruti smṛti śārīraka virodhaḥ sa uddeśataḥ  niruhyate yad tāvat sūtritam prathama adhyāye ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ iti atra jñāna indriya pañka upādānam na indriya antara pratikṣepa artham manasaḥ pṛthak prameya tayā uddeśāt  anantaram eva ca yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti lakṣaṇa karaṇāt  abhyupagama siddhānta nyāyena ca tad indriyatva parīkṣaṇāt  atas ca uktena samāna yogakṣema yukti pramāṇakaḥ karmendriya varga upalakṣaṇīyaḥ pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ iti sūtre vācaḥ kaṇṭha ukteḥ pāṇi ādi catuṣṭayasya śārīra vyāpāra karaṇa tayā sūcanāt iti śarīrake tu sapta gateḥ viśeṣita tvāt ca iti pūrva pakṣam upakṣipya asādhayat ca hasta ādīnām api indriya tvam bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ hasta ādayaḥ tu sthite atas  na evam iti bhūtebhyaḥ iti ca na upādāna abhiprāyam ahaṅkāra upāttānām āpyāyaka bhūta vivakṣayā api tad upapatteḥ tathā ca veda artha saṃgrahe evam āhaṅkārikāṇām indriyāṇām bhūtaiḥ ca āpyāyanam mahābhārata ucyate iti samādhānam ṛṣi antara vākyasya api samāna nyāyasya nirvāha artham paraspara viruddha pramāṇa vākyeṣu tātparya viśeṣa parikalpanayā parihāra eva hi paṇḍita kṛtyam anitya manaḥ vādibhiḥ api hi anna mayam hi somya manaḥ iti śrutiḥ āpyāyana para tayā eva yojyā tulyam idam anyatra api iti yad tu bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham tad atyanta vimokṣaḥ  apavargaḥ iti tatra duḥkha atyanta nivṛtteḥ apavarga tvam sarva aṅgīkṛtam na ca tatra ānandaḥ śrautaḥ kaṇṭha uktyāḥ pratiṣidhyate tad abhiprāye ca ananyathā siddham kim api na liṅgam paśyāmaḥ ata eva hi bhūṣaṇa mate nitya sukha saṃvedana saṃbandha siddhiḥ apavarge sādhitā etena tasmāt sarva duḥkha vimākṣaḥ  apavargaḥ iti caturtha adhyāya vākyam api nirvyūḍham tatra api ānanda niṣedha abhāvāt yad ca śārīraka dvitīya adhyāya viruddham iha dvitīya adhyāye avayavi samarthanam iva ābhāti tad api tad eka artham yojayitum śakyam tathā hi na ca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt sādhya tvāt avayavini saṃdehaḥ sarva agrahaṇam avayavi siddheḥ dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ ca senā vanavat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti etāni hi tad sūtrāṇi na tāni virudhyante senā vana ādi vyāvṛtta avaya vyārambhaka tayā tad asamavāyi kāraṇatva abhimata avasthā viśeṣa āpannaḥ saṃghāta viśeṣa eva avayavi śabdena nirdiṃśyata iti avirodhāt  tāvatā eva upalambha vyavahāra viśeṣa ādeḥ carita artha tvāt atīndriya aṇu vacanam api pradīpa avayavānām iva aindriyikāṇām eva avasthā viśeṣeṇa atīndriyatva abhyupagamāt aviruddham avyaktam eva hi triguṇa dravyam avasthā viśeṣādravyaktam bhavati iti āgamikāḥ pratyekam upalambha ayogyānām api saṃhati viśeṣa rūpa avasthā bhedāt aindriyikatva tad tāratamya ādikam himānī cūrṇa puñja ādiṣu anārabdha  ayaviṣu loka siddham upamāna ākhya pramāṇa antara samarthanam tu nyāya eka deśibhiḥ eva upamānasya anumāna antarbhāva pratikṣepa mātra para tayā nirvyūḍham yad ca pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca saṃbandha abhāvaḥ iti śabda artha saṃbandha abhāvam upakṣipya pariharatā śabda artha vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhḥ na sāmayika tvāt śabdāt arthe pratyayasya ityādinā sāmayika tvam uktam tad api saṃpratipannasāmayikatva dvārā anumāna ādi vilakṣaṇa saṃbandha viśeṣa khyāpana artham iti yojyam anādi nidhana avicchinna saṃpradāya veda vartinām padānām manu ādi vacana viruddha sāṃketikatva upapādana kḷpti asaṃbhavāt yad ca mantra āyurveda prāmāṇyavat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt  iti etad api anādi nidhanasya eva vedasya pratikalpam īśvareṇa āptatamena yathāpūrvam pravartanam abhisaṃdhāya iti sugamam varṇa anityatva varṇanam tu na śruti ādi viruddham pratyuta anukūlam eva śārīraka devata adhikaraṇe varṇa anitya tvam abhyupagamya eva hi ata eka ca nitya tvam samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca āvṛttau  api avirodhaḥ  darśanāt  smṛteḥ ca iti veda nitya tvam sādhitam yad tu jaiminīye śabda adhikaraṇe varṇa nityatva samarthanam vyācakhyuḥ sa tu vyākhyātṝṇām eva aparādhaḥ asāṃketika vācaka ākāra nityatva paratvena anya paratvāt tasya adhikaraṇasya yad ca dvitīya adhyāya ante vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ iti uktam tatra api na vaiśeṣika abhyupagata jāti svīkāre liṅgam paśyāmaḥ na hi atra dravya guṇa ādi padārtha parisaṃkhyānam kriyate te vibhakti antāḥ padam iti pratipādita pada vācya pradarśana para tvāt anantaram catisṛṇām eva lakṣaṇam āha vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ  mūrtiḥ ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅga ākhyā samāna prasava ātmikā jātiḥ iti iha tu vastu svarūpa nirūpita svarūpa viśeṣaka dharma svarūpa nirūpaka dharma viṣaya tayā yathāsaṃbhavam yojyam atas  na dvitīya adhyāye api vedānta virodhaḥ tṛtīye darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt iti ādikam bāhya antar indriya ādinirūpaṇa ādikam ca atyanta upayuktam na ca manaḥ nityatva ādikam tatra sūtritam yena tad utpatti ādi śruti kopaḥ yad ca atra uktam gandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam śruti prāmāṇyāt ca iti etad eva yathāśrutam siddhānta tayā svīkāryam yad api gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrva pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ iti guṇa vyavasthāpanam tatra tu tathā eva abhyupagame api na vastu antara virodhaḥ tathā api ākāśa ādiṣu śabda ādeḥ eka dvi tri catuṣpañca krameṇa purāṇeṣu pāṭhāt  ākāśa anupraveśāt anyatra śabda iti nirvāhe vārūvādi anupraveśāt uttarottareṣu sparśa ādiḥ iti nirvoḍhum śakya tvāt  upalambha anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyavasthāpanasya api sama tvāt  gandha ādi sūtram pṛthivyāḥ te santi eva iti ayoga vyavacchedena nirvāhyam ākāśasya uttaraḥ iti atra tu tasya sa eva iti anya yoga vyavacchedena kati kati ca evam sūtrāṇi kliṣṭāni paraiḥ api niruhyante yad ca sva guṇān na upalabhanta indriyāṇi kasmāt iticed  sa guṇānam indriya bhāvāt iti atra na śabda guṇa upalabdheḥ iti uktam tatra api śrotra indriyasya ākāśa āpyāyitā tvāt āpyāyaka guṇasya tad guṇa tām paṭanailya pānīya saurabha ādivat  prakalpa uktam uttaram athavā yathā āgamamāhaṅkārika tvam indriyāṇām ajānataḥ ca udye bhūta āpyāyita indriya pakṣe sthitvā eva idam uttaram gūḍha abhiprāyeṇa dadīya iti etad uktam bhavati bhavatā kim indriya guṇa upalambha abhāva ucyate kim vā tad āpyāyaka guṇa upalambha abhāvaḥ pūrvatra aṅgīkāra eva uttaram śabda ādīnām anindriya guṇa tvāt  uttaratra vyabhicāra iti atas  na vedānta virodha prasaṅgaḥ caturthe adhyāyepravṛtti rāga dveṣa ādi nirūpaṇam ātma nityatva ādinā pretyabhāva ādi pratipādanam animitta bhāva utpatti sarva anityatva sarva nityatva ādi nirūpaṇam ca atyanta anuguṇam avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca prāc ukta nyāyena netavyaḥ pañcamaḥ tu jāti nigraha sthāna mātra upakṣīṇaḥ  na kvacid tattva upakaroti vyavahāra aṅga vimarśa saundaryā saundarya ādikam tu vāstava lakṣya lakṣaṇa yukti ādi parāmarśa vaijñānikaiḥ artha sthiti mātra anusārāt anādaraṇīyam yad  punar arvāgbhiḥ akṣa caraṇa pañcādhyāyyām kuśa kāśa avalambena kaṇa caraṇa kathām niveśya naigamikyaḥ padavyaḥ  nirudhyante tatra tu nūnam sa eva gautamaḥ svayam antar  prahasati iti svīkāra pakṣaḥ yad vā na atīva ca bahiṣkāraḥ  na atīva ca parigrahaḥ sāṃkhya ādivat iha api syāt  samādhiḥ tauṣataṃṇḍulaḥ upajīvya bahutvena vidyā sthāna niveśanam viruddha aṃśa eka viṣayā sūtra ādiṣu bahiṣkriyā adhikāri vivecanam niyata adhikāraḥ ca ayam nyāya vistaraḥ adhikārāt ca niyataḥ syāt ayam nyāya vistaraḥ apratyavāyaḥ  māhātmyāt dayāluḥ śāstram abravīt  sarva adhikāram iti etad asamīkṣita bhāṣitam katham āgama vṛttāntam anadhīta āgamā viduḥ niṣiddhe prerayan  tān vā katham kāruṇikaḥ  bhavet  na ca śakyā nara śiraḥ pāvitrya ādi anumākṣatiḥ vihāya āgamam akṣa ādyaiḥ dvidhā tatra api viplavaḥ śrutyām hi anadhikāri tvāt tad anyatra avyavasthiteḥ dharma kṣobhām umā bhaṅge katham śūdra ādayaḥ kṣamāḥ atha traivarṇikaiḥ ukte tu anyaḥ  viśvasitī iti api svayam nyāya vicāre asya phalati anadhikāritām pratyakṣa anumayoḥ yatra nityam veda anapekhatā tatra apaśūdra bhāṣya uktā śūdra ādeḥ api adhikriyā caturdaśā api sthānāni bhagavān dharma vidyayoḥ na spraṣṭavyāni śūdraiḥ iti abravīt āśvamedhike aṅgāni vedāḥ catvāraḥ  mīmāṃsā nyāya vistaraḥ purāṇam dharma śāstram ca vidyā hi etāḥ caturdaśa yāni uktāni mayā samyak vidyā sthānāni bhārata utpannāni pavitrāṇi pāvana artham tathā eva ca tasmāt tāni na śūdrasya spraṣṭavyāni kathañcana iti tasmāt etāni traivarṇikaiḥ adhyetavyāni tatra brāhmaṇena vidyā prāptaye dharma anuṣṭhānāya ca adhigantavyāni kṣatriya vaiśyābhyām dharma anuṣṭhānāya eva tathā śaṅkhena vidyā sthānāni anukramya uktam etāni brāhmaṇaḥ  adhikurute sa ca vṛttim darśayati itareṣām iti evam eva dharma śāstra saṃgrāhakaiḥ samarthitam tatas ca yeṣām karma brahma mīmāṃsa avaseya tattva hita rūpa prameya cintā adhikāraḥ teṣām eva tātparya paryavasāyitayā dharma vidyā sthāna abhimata nyāyaṃvistara andhikārapa iti siddham prayojana nirūpaṇam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇena śuddhiḥ pada tad arthayoḥ māna meya ādi niyatiḥ nirdeṣa ukteḥ ca mānatā grāva plavana vākyāḥ dāvāni paryam virodhataḥ citrā paśu phala tvāda avabādha dvāra saṃgrahaḥ anuvāda vidhāna ādi cintā prāpti ādi pūrvikā pratyakṣa ādiṣu asiddheṣu na kalpeta kathañcana evamādi upayogena munibhiḥ nyāya vistaraḥ veda anugrahaṇāt dharma vidyā sthāna tayā uditaḥ āgama ākhya pramāṇe tu saṃśuddhe nyāya vistarāt  tad viśeṣasya mīmāṃsā sādhayet dharmam āna tām prameyasya api saṃśuddhiḥ antatas  brahma cintanāt  iha tasya niveśaḥ tu tādarthyādi prasiddhaye pramāṇam eva asya śāstrasya prādhānyataḥ  viṣayaḥ tatra prekṣāvat adhi cikīrṣā siddhi artham prameya tattva jñānam hāna upādāna dvārā niḥśreyasa hetuḥ tad ca sa parikarāt  pramāṇāt iti paramparayā prayojana jñāpanāya pradarśana mātram iha abhimatam atas  pradhāna viṣaya tayā prameya ādi sādhaka tayā ca pramāṇam prameyāt api pūrvam ucyate tatra vyavacchedyatva aṅgatva ādi mukhena saṃśayāt ayaḥ  api caturdaśa yathāyatham nirūpyante na ca ṣoḍaśa tve nirbandhaḥ atathātva viparyayatva ādi upādhi antara adhīna saṃgraha vibhajanābhyām nyūna adhika uddeśasya api śakya tvāt  upayoga anupayoga aviśeṣāt ca etāvat eva gautamasya api hṛdayam iti pramāṇa apramāṇa vyavasthāpanam asti tāvat idam pramāṇam idam apramāṇam iti prasiddhaḥ  laukika parīkṣaka vyavahāra ghaṇṭā pathaḥ tad anādare tu nirāśraya tayā parīkṣaṇasya api anudayaḥ vyavahāraḥ  hi jagataḥ  bhavati ālambane kvacid  na tad sāmānyataḥ na asti kathantā tu parīkṣyate sāmānya niścita arthena viśeṣe tu bubhutsite parīkṣā hi ucitā sva iṣṭa pramāṇa utpādana ātmikā na sarvasya apramāṇa tvam sva pakṣasya svatas  kṣateḥ na sarvasya pramāṇa tvam sva pakṣasya anyatas  kṣateḥ siddhi asiddhyaḥ  sva pakṣasya siddhā loka vyavasthitiḥ tad siddhi asiddhyoḥ tvad pakṣaḥ  na kathañcana sidhyati pramāṇena pramāṇasya bādhaḥ sva vyāhateḥ hataḥ apramāṇena tad bādhe sādhanam ca tatas  na kim apramāṇāt  pramāṇāt vā māna siddhiḥ na ced na tad  yatas  pramāṇataḥ tasya siddhiḥ sva para rakṣiṇī bādhā bādha vyavasthā api mānataḥ syāt ravi avasthitāt  anyathā tu avyavasthāyā na vyavasthā iti avasthiteḥ sarvatra anirṇaye na staḥ saṃśaya utpatti nirṇayau yathā tad koṭi tad siddhiḥ tathā anyatra api yujyate dharmi sādhāraṇa ākāra koṭīnām pūrva niścaye asau  ayamayam vā iti hi āvirbhavati saṃśayaḥ sarvatra saṃśayaḥ tāvat na sarvasya api dṛśyate sarvam saṃdigdham iti te nipuṇasya asti niścayaḥ saṃśayaḥ ca na saṃdigdhaḥ saṃdigdha advaitavādinaḥ dūram gatvā api durvāraḥ saṃśaye nirṇayaḥ tava māna āmāna vibhāge atas  sāmānyena vyavasthite kvācid ka saṃśaya ucchittyai lakṣaṇam saṃpracakṣate tatra vyutpatti vivakṣā bhedāt  pramitim tad karaṇam ca yathā iccham pramāṇam āhuḥ iti avocāma āśraya prāmāṇyasya anādeśika tvāt  āpta prāmāṇyāt  āpta uktatva hetoḥ prāmāṇyāt iti arthaḥ na hi vaktṛ prāmāṇyam vākya prāmāṇya upayujyate laukika vākyeṣu kintu kāraṇa doṣa abhāvaḥ dvidhā api pramitiḥ eva śodhyā pramā lakṣaṇa parīkṣaṇam tatra asmadīyā eva kecid anyathā ākhyātim icchantaḥ smṛteḥ prāmāṇyam anicchantaḥ samyak anubhavaḥ pramā iti lakṣayanti ubhayam icchantaḥ yathārtha jñānam pramā iti ubhayam anicchantaḥ anubhūtiḥ pramā iti evaṃprāyāṇi ca vādi antara uktāni lakṣaṇāni vayam tu brūmaḥ yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam pramā iti yathārtha khyātim akhyātim anyathā ākhyātim eva vā icchadbhiḥ na vimantavyam idam loka anusārataḥ smṛti mātrāṃ pramāṇa tvam na yuktam iti vakṣyate abādhita smṛteḥ loke pramāṇatva parigrahāt  buddha āgama ādi tyāge ca na hetuḥ smṛti mūla tā viśuddha smṛti mūle api mānavādau prasaṅgataḥ bhrāntim pramātaḥ  bhindantaḥ  na ca āhuḥ smṛti mānatām smṛti tvam eva hi vyaktam aprāmāṇyam bhavat mate pīta śaṅkha bhrama ādau ca na hi etad upapadyate cakṣuṣā eva hi śaṅkha ādeḥ pītim ādeḥ ca tatra dhīḥ tatas ca pratipattau vā vyavahāra udaye api vā tathā abhāvānyathā tvābhyām pramā bhra antita vyavasthitiḥ viparyaya ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ evam eva hi sidhyati yad kiñcid anyathātvam hi vaiparītyam iti iṣyate ātma khyāti ādi vādeṣu api anyathātvam avāritam bhrama pravṛtti bādha ādeḥ anyathā na hi saṃbhavaḥ evam sati anyathā adhīḥ tad sāmagrī vā api lāghavāt  ayathāvyavahārasya hetuḥ iti avaśiṣyate sarvaiḥ api anyathā khyātiḥ dustyaja tvāt laghīyasī tad vādinā api avarjya tvāt tatas  api akhyāti lāghavam svārasyam anyathā ākhyāta avakhyātau lāghavam sthitam iti darśayitum bhāṣye dvitayam tad anujjhitam yad nātha muni miśra ādyaiḥ yathārtha khyāti sādhanam tad loka buddhi anārohāt vaibhavam kecid ūcire mānāt rūpi ādi sattve api tayoḥ anyatarat dhruvam kārya akṣamatva agrahaṇāt tad kṣamatva graheṇa vā khyāti antarāṇām doṣāḥ tu tad tad siddhānta śīlane svayam eva unmiṣanti eva saṃgrahāt  kiñcid ucyate tatra ātma khyātau tāvat  anyat vijñānam asti iti dhīḥ anya viṣayā na vā ādyer athasya api tadvat dhīra nyatra ekā eva dhīḥ bhavet  saṃtāna antara vijñānam sva saṃtāne kṣaṇa antaram yā dhīḥ sādhayate sā hi svatas  bāhyam vigāhate saha upalambha niyamaḥ saṃvidaḥ  grāhya lakṣma ca bodhe api artha iva iti evam jñāna artha aikyam na tad bhavet doṣa ādi hetu jālasya mithyāve api yathā iṣyate adhiṣṭhānasya mithyāve api anivāryaḥ tathā bhramaḥ tatas  mādhyamikasya eva pakṣaḥ tatra avaśiṣyate na ca tatra api nistāraḥ sarvathā anupapattitaḥ asattvam laukikam brūṣe lokottaram atha api vā na niṣedhaḥ  nirupadhiḥ pūrvatra anyat na dhī padam catuṣkoṭi vimuktam ca tattvam prāmāṇikam na vā pūrvatra tāvatī sattā na ced  tad dhīra sanmatiḥ anyeṣām ca niradhiṣṭhāna khyātau atra asat eva bhavatām atra iti khyāyate na vā ādye siddham adhiṣṭhānam dvitīye khyāti apahnavaḥ kim ca sva netra niṣṭhyūtam timiram timira arditaiḥ keśa stabaka sādṛśyāt tathā bhāti evam īdṛśāḥ yadi api avidyamānor athaḥ vidyamāna tayā sphuret  tathā api asau  adhiṣṭhānam sva deśa ādau mitaḥ  hi saḥ idantvena pratīter athe tad āropam pare viduḥ tasmin nidantu āropaḥ te phalataḥ tulya tā dvayoḥ anirvacanīya khyātau anirvācya tayā vastu nirucyeta na vā tvayā ādye virodhaḥ  vividhaḥ  dvitīye asmad mata sthitiḥ sat asat vyatirekaḥ  api viruddhaḥ  yadi gṛhyate sat asat rūpa tā kim nu pratītā tu na gṛhyate anuṣṇa aśītavat  tucchāt brahmaṇaḥ ca atireki tā sādhyeta khyāti bādha ādeḥ yadi siddham tad atra naḥ na ca viśvasya bādhaḥ  api svarasāt upajāyate apratiṣṭhita yuktyā tu bādhaḥ  brahmā api saṃspṛśet  nāśāt saditara tvam ca nāśa kāle yadi iṣyate sva kāle yadi bādhaḥ syāt na aśasya api anirūpaṇam nitya tvena śrutānām ca keṣāṃ cit na hi nāśitā bhāga asiddhaḥ tatas  hetuḥ na ca aikyam nāśa bādhayoḥ nirviṣaya khyātau viṣaya alīka bhāva ādau khyāti antara parigrahaḥ anullekhaḥ tu rūpya ādi dhīḥ iti uktyā nibarhitaḥ nigamanam tatas ca atra anyathā adhīḥ vā tad hetumatiḥ eva vā bhrāntiḥ vastu virūpasya vyavahārasya kāraṇam tad iha anyathā ākhyāti pakṣe viparyayasya saṃśayasya ca vyavaccheda artham yathā avasthita vyavahāra anuguṇam jñānam iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇe yathā avasthita ādi viśeṣaṇam akhyāti pakṣe api tad sāmagrī anupraviṣṭam jñānam taca chabdena vyapadiśyate tad ca tatra apramāṇam iti loka siddha tvāt vyavacchedyam eva tatra api pratyeka aṃśe yāthārthyam na vihanyate viparyaya nirūpaṇam tatra ādye pakṣe anyasya anyathā adhyavasāyaḥ  viparyayaḥ dvitīye tu pakṣe sāmānyatas  dharmi sphuraṇe sati apratipanna tad virodha viruddha viśeṣa adhyavasāya iti sa ca ayam anekavidhaḥ eka aneka viruddha viśeṣa sphuraṇāt  tatra eka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā pītaḥ śaṅkha ityādi aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā aekam eva bhinnam abhinnam ca ityādi anekānta vādinām prapañcaḥ sat vilakṣaṇaḥ  asat vilakṣaṇaḥ ca ityādya dvaita vādinām paraspara viruddha aneka viśeṣavata r idṛśasya viparyayasya saṃśayāt bhedaḥ  mithas virodha abhimāna viraheṇa samuccita adhyavasāyaḥ dharma virodhe paraspara aviruddha aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam yathā vipulatva ekatva viśiṣṭe candre alpatva dvitva ādi grahaḥ viparyayam eva dharma antara dharmī antara bhedāt anyathā khyāti viparīta khyāti bhedena kvacid vyavaharanti yathā pīta śaṅkha rajju sarpa bhramau tayoḥ ca rajaḥ tamasī mūlam iti gīyate yayā dharmam adharmam ca kāryam ca akāryam eva ca ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasī adharmam dharmam iti yā manyate tamasā vṛtā sarva arthān viparītān  ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī iti yadi api rajju sarpa ādi bhrame rajjutva ādi dharma viparīta sarpatva ādi dharma adhyāsa eva tathā api svarūpa nirūpaka dharma tvena antaraṅga tayā dharmi vaiparīti avyapadeśaḥ śvaitya ādeḥ tu nirūpita svarūpa viśeṣaka tvam eva vivaraṇe tu evam uktam trividham ajñānam svarūpa ajñānam anyathājñānam viparīta jñānam iti svarūpa ajñānam nāma vastunaḥ  apratipattiḥ anyathājñānam vastunaḥ  vastu antaratayā bhānam yathāśukteḥ rūpya tayā viparīta jñānam tu yathāvat  vastuni bhāsamāne yuktibhiḥ tasya anyathā upapādanam yathā ājñātṛtayā ahantvena ātmani bhāsamāne api kuyuktibhiḥ asyabhrānti ta upa pādanam kudṛśām iti adharma indriya doṣa dustarka abhyāsa durvyāpti anusaṃdhāna vipralambhaka vākya śravaṇa ādibhiḥ tattva āgraha sahakṛtaiḥ viparyayasya yathāsaṃbhavam udbhavaḥ saṃśaya nirūpaṇam sāmānya dharmi sphuraṇe sati apratipanna tad virodha pratipanna mithas virodha aneka viśeṣa sphuraṇam saṃśayaḥ yathā ūrdhva vastu mātra grahaṇe sati tad virodhitayā ananusaṃdhīyamānayoḥ mithas sphuṭa virodhayoḥ sthāṇutva puruṣa tvayoḥ sphuraṇa mayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ  vā iti mithas  virodha agrahaṇe tayoḥ vikalpaḥ  na syāt  tatas  eva ḍolā vegavat atra sphuraṇa kramaḥ iti eke ekasmin yugapad anyonya pratikṣepasya dhī viruddha tvāt  atra caitanyasya viṣayeṇa dṛḍha saṃyogaḥ  hi niścayaḥ tasya eva bahubhiḥ yuga pada dṛḍha saṃyogaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti ātma siddhi granthaḥ  api na viruddhaḥ itarathā jñāna arthayoḥ dṛḍha adṛḍha saṃśleṣa nirūpaṇa anupapatteḥ yugapad iti tu śaighṣa mātra param yaugapadya abhyupagame api adṛḍha tvam paraspara pratikṣepa prakāra viśeṣa eva anyathā ayam ūrdhva u vā sthāṇuḥ vā ityādi saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ yadi api aviruddheṣu api keṣucid adharma ādi mūlaka virodha grahaṇāt keṣāñcid īdṛśaḥ  api saṃśayaḥ saṃbhavati yathā ātmā jñānam vā jñātā vā iti jñānam dharmaḥ  dharmi vā ityādi tathā api ābhimānikam paraspara pratikṣepi tvam tatra api asti eva asya ca samāna dharma vipratipattibhyām eva asādhāraṇa kāraṇābhyām adharma ādi sahitābhyām yathāsaṃbhavam udbhavaḥ tad uktam tattva ratna ākare kaḥ ca eṣa saṃśayaḥ katividhaḥ ca ekasmin dharmiṇi viruddha aneka viśeṣa avabhāsaḥ saṃśayaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ ityādinā tatra samāna dharmaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ  dharmaḥ tad janitaḥ yathā ūrdhvatva aviśeṣāt sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ  vā iti agṛhyamāṇa bala tāratamya viruddha aneka jñāpaka upasthāpanam iha vipratipattiḥ sā ca sajātīya vijātīya ābhāsa rūpa dvi tri catur ādi jñāpaka bhedāt bahu prakārā pratyakṣa tad ābhāsa vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ  yathā cakṣuṣā samukham pratibhāti darpaṇa talam sparśanena tu anyathā kim idam samukham nirmukham vā iti anumāna tad ābhāsa vipratipatteḥ yathā dhūmavat tvāt  parvataḥ  agnimān nirāloka tvāt anagniḥ iti atra sa agniḥ anagniḥ vā iti śruti vipratipatteḥ yathā bheda abheda vyapadeśābhyām jīvaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā ityādi vādi vipratipatteḥ yathā vaiśeṣika aupaniṣada vākya dvaya śrāviṇaḥ  madhyastha buddheḥ kim indriyāṇi bhautikāni āhaṅkārikāṇi vā iti evam pāmara ādi vākya vipratipatteḥ api nadyāḥ tīre phalāni santi na santi vā ityādi pratyakṣa anumāna vipratipatteḥ yathā cakṣuṣā pīta śaṅkha bhrame śaṅkha tvāt ca sitatva anumāne kim ayam śaṅkhaḥ pītaḥ sitaḥ  vā iti pratyakṣa āgama vipratipatteḥ yathākim aham arthaḥ sthūlaḥ  aṇurve ati anumāna āgama vipratipatteḥ yathā kim paramāṇu upādānam jagat  uta brahma upādānam iti eṣā diś  kecid tu vipratipatti śabda mātre muhyantaḥ  vādi vipratipattim eva vipratipattim manyante tad ayuktam viśeṣa abhāvāt yad uktam prajñā paritrāṇe sādhāraṇa ākṛteḥ dṛṣṭyā aneka ākāra grahāt tathā vipaścitām vivādāt ca tridhā saṃśaya iṣyate iti tad api nūnam para anukāra mātram dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ akaiḥ āśyāt  grāhaka ava antara bhedasya atiprasaṅgi tvāt aprayojaka tvāt ca atra ca aneka ākāra grahaḥ  nānā ākāra grahaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ na tu aneka vyāvṛtta asādhāraṇa ākāra grahaḥ anantaram artheṣu eṣu aviśeṣeṇa dvi ākāra grāhidhī dvayam ityādinā tasya eva udāharaṇāt asādhāraṇa dharmāt api kecid  saṃśayam āhuḥ yathāgandhavat tvāt  pṛthivī nityā anityā vā ityādi atra gandhavat tvasya nitya ātma ādi vyāvṛtteḥ kṛtakatva ādivat anityatva smāraka tvam anitya ābādi vyāvṛtteḥ niravayavatva ādivat nityatva smāraka tvam iti viruddha viśeṣa dvaya anvita samāna dharmasya iva tad ubhaya vyāvṛtta asādhāraṇa dharmasya api saṃśaya hetu tvam upapannam iti tad ayuktam na hi tatra gandhavattva ādinā saṃśaya utpattiḥ api tu vyatireka nirūpaṇa vilambā prāk eva gandha ādi viśiṣṭa dravyasya nitya anitya sādhāraṇa tayā bhāsamānaiḥ dravyatva ādibhiḥ eva tatra anyatara śiraḥ nirṇinīṣayā viśeṣaka dharma cintāyām tu gandhavat tvam ubhayān anvita tvāt ubhayoḥ api aniṣkarṣam iti etāvat eva cintyate kevala vyatireki bhaṅge ca etad viśadam bhaviṣyati gandhavat tvāt  pṛthivī nityā vā anityā vā iti tu yadā kaścid vyavaharet tatra api gandhavat tvam nityatva anitya tvayoḥ anyatarasya prayojakam na vā iti eva saṃdehaḥ saḥ  api dharmatva ādi lakṣaṇa samāna dharmāt eva atha nitya vyāvṛtta dharmavat tvāt anitya tvam anitya vyāvṛtta dharmavat tvāt ca nitya tvam puraskṛtya nityā anityā vā iti saṃśate tadā api hetu bhūta dharma dvaya nimittaḥ  ayam saṃśayaḥ na hi eka eva atra hetuḥ gandhaḥ tu tatra sāmānya rūpaḥ taṭa sthaḥ na tu hetuḥ vipratipattim api kecid  samāna dharma eva antar bhāvayanti yathā hi ūrdhva tvam ubhaya sādhāraṇam tathā vādi parigṛhītatva ādeḥ api sādhāraṇa tvāt  vimati viṣayasya dharmiṇaḥ  vā sāmānya veṣasya tad ubhaya sādhāraṇyāt iti tathā api sādhāraṇa dharmasya saha anubhūta stha aṇutva puruṣatva smārakatvavat  vipratipatteḥ apisamāna dharma unnīti nirapekṣāyā eva tad upajīvyatayā tad pūrva bhāvinyāḥ sākṣāt tad viśeṣa smārakatva siddheḥ dvaidham uktam asmābhiḥ punar ca ayam dvi tri catur ādi śirodhi karaṇa bhedāt bahuvidhaḥ yathā ayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ  vā iti ghaṭaḥ satyaḥ  asatyaḥ  nirvacanīyaḥ anirvacanīyaḥ vā ityādi tathā imau sthāṇū vā puruṣau vā ete padārthāḥ satyā asatyā nirvacanīyā anirvacanīyā vā ityādi yaḥ tu dvayoḥ anyatarasya cora tve siddhe ayam coraḥ ayam vā cora iti saṃdehaḥ sa tu ayam coraḥ  na vā iti evaṃrūpa saṃśaya dvaya samāhāraḥ yad vā yaḥ ca uraḥ saḥ ayam ayam vā iti eka eva atha vā cora tvam etad niṣṭham etad niṣṭham vā iti yadi api ubhaya vyatirikta puruṣa coratva abhāva u tayoḥ anyatarasya cora tve vā tātparyāt nirṇaya garbha tvam tathā api ubhayoḥ anyatara viśeṣa nirṇaya abhāvāt tasmin  aṃśe saṃśaya eva na ca ekasya api jñānasya saṃśaya nirṇaya ātma tā virodhaḥ sarvasmin  api saṃśaye dharmya śādau nirṇayasya dustyaja tvāt  punar dvividhaḥ  ayam anyatara koṭi pariśeṣa yogyatva tada yogyatva bhedāt pūrvaḥ yathā sthāṇu ātmake vastuni sthāṇuḥ puruṣaḥ  vā iti uttaraḥ tu palālakūṭe dviradaḥ  giri śikharam vā iti tatra nirūpakāṇām prāyaśas  pūrva eva bhavati tena eva ca pravṛttasya pākṣikor athalābhaḥ yad vā nirīhasya eva kadācid  dvitīyena saṃśayena viparyayeṇa ca pravṛttasya daivāt  tad ātana artha saṃnipātena abhimata lābha iti punar api imau saṃśaya viparyayau sāmānya dharmiṇaḥ  viśeṣāṇām ca anubhūyamānatva smaryamāṇatva ādi bhedāt bahuvidha āvūhanīyau  iti kiṃsa jña kaḥ  ayam vṛkṣa iti evamādi rūpaḥ  anadhyavasāyaḥ  nāmānyaḥ  jñāna viśeṣa iti kecid  tad asāram tasya saṃjñā ādi viśeṣa saṃdeha samanantara bhāvita dviśeṣa bubhutsa ātmaka tvāt  athavā avacchedaka adarśanāt anavacchinna koṭi viśeṣaḥ saṃśaya eva ūhaḥ tu prāyas  puruṣeṇa anena bhavitavyam ityādi rūpa eka koṭi sahacarita bhūyodharma darśanāt anutkaṭa ani akoṭikaḥ sa eva prāyas  puruṣeṇa bhavitavyam iti puruṣa eva iti abhiprāyaḥ ced  yathocitam pratyakṣa anumāna ādiṣu anupraveśaḥ tarka rūpam ūham tu anumāne vakṣyāmaḥ trividham pramāṇam pratyakṣa anumāna śabda bhedāt  bhagavatā m anunā api uktam pratyakṣam anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam trayam su viditam kāryam dharma siddhim abhīpsatā iti āha ca bhagavān śaunakaḥ dṛṣṭa anumāna āgama jam dhyānasya ālambanam tridhā iti bhāṣya kāreṇa ca pratyakṣa ādi trayam sva śabdena upādāya pramāṇa saṃkhyā vivāde api sarva abhyupagata pramāṇa anām ayam eva viṣaya iti na kena api pramāṇena nirviśeṣa vastu siddhiḥ iti anyeṣām anādaraḥ kṛtaḥ sarva abhyupagata pramāṇānām iti ca para abhyupagama mātram dyotayati tatra prativādinaḥ ṣaṣ pramāṇa abhyupagamāt pratyakṣa anumāna āgamānām eva ca mithas  bhedaḥ  veda artha saṃgrahe viśadam upapāditaḥ yad tu mattaḥ smṛti jñārnam apohanam ca iti atra bhāṣyam jñānam indriya liṅga āgama yoga jaḥ  vastu niścayaḥ iti tatra api yoga jasya pratyakṣasya prādhānyāt  pṛthak vyapadeśaḥ antarbhāvam ca vakṣyāmaḥ uktam ca śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ prameya saṃgrahe pramāṇa saṃkhyā vivāde api iti atra tri pramāṇa tvam bhāṣya uktam iti bhāṣye ca keṣucid  kośeṣu yathārtha khyāti samarthanadaśāyām athavā kim anena bahunā upapādana prakāreṇa pratyakṣa anumāna āgama ākhyam pramāṇa jātam āgama gamyam ca nirasta nikhila doṣa gandha mana vadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇam sarvajñam satya saṃkalpam param brahma abhyupagacchatām kim na setsyati kim na upapadyate ityādiḥ pāṭhaḥ  dṛśyate yadi api smṛtiḥ api yathārthā pramāṇam iti vakṣyate tathā api pratyakṣa ādi mūla tayā tad aviśeṣāt pṛthak anuktiḥ uktam ca tattva ratna ākare pratyakṣa ādi mūlānām smṛtīnām sva sva mūle antarbhāva vivakṣayā pramāṇa tritva avirodhaḥ catuṣṭve ca vaidika anuvādaḥ  darśitaḥ iti sa cācam anuvādaḥ pūrva upāttaḥ smṛtiḥ pratyakṣam aitihyam anumānam catuṣṭayam iti pratyakṣa ādi aviśeṣeṇa veda anuvādāt ca eti prajñā paritrāṇe tu smṛti prāmāṇya anabhyupagame api jñānasya tāvat  karaṇa bhedāt cāturvidhyam eva uktam tatra indriya artha saṃbandhaḥ  liṅga śabda grahau tathā saṃskāra unmeṣa iti ete saṃvidām janma hetavaḥ iti yad tu tatra eva svayaṃsiddhiḥ tathā divyam pratyakṣam anum āgamaḥ pañca santi pramāṇāni jaimini vyāsayoḥ hṛdi ityādinā svayaṃsiddhi divyayoḥ pṛthak nirūpaṇam kṛtam tad  pratyakṣa avāntara vairūpya bodhana abhiprāyam yathā uktam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ bhagavat prasāda labdha yogi pratyakṣam divyam iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam tatra sākṣātkāri pramā pratyakṣam sākṣāt tvam ca jāti rūpa upādhi rūpaḥ  vā kaścid  jñāna svabhāva viśeṣaḥ sva ātma sākṣikaḥ jñāta kāraṇa ja jñāna smṛtitva rahitā matiḥ aparokṣa iti niṣkarṣe na avyāpya ādi prasañjanam prameya saṃgrahe tu evam uktam sākṣāt anubhavaḥ pratyakṣam sākṣāt tvam jātiḥ ityādi tattva ratna ākare api evam uktam aparokṣa pramādhi kṣamā aparokṣyam ca saṃvidaḥ vyavahārya artha saṃbandhi jñāna jatva vivarjanam iti pārokṣyam ca evam uktam pārokṣyam vyavahārya anantargata vastu vedanā apekṣā tad anantargata liṅga ādi apekṣā pārokṣyam anumādau iti vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ mānaya artha ātmi anirṇaye tu evam uktam aparokṣa pramā pratyakṣam pramāyā āparokṣyam nāma viśada avabhāsa tvam iti brūmaḥ kim idam vaiśadyam nāma asādhāraṇa ākāreṇa vastu avabhāsaka tvam ityādi sākṣāt tvam dvidhā anityam ca anityam car iśvara nitya jñāna ādi niṣṭham nityam asmad ādi jñāna niṣṭham tu anityam asmad ādi pratyakṣam dvidhā yogi pratyakṣam ayogi pratyakṣam ca iti tatra yogi pratyakṣam prakṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa viśeṣa jam tad  yukta avasthāyām manaḥ mātra janyam viyukta avasthāyām tu bāhya indriya janyam api tad ca bubhutsā ādi pratiniyatam āgama eka siddham ca bhāvanā balaja mātram jagatkartari pratyakṣam pratikṣiptam śāstra yoni adhikaraṇe anyatra bhāṣya kāraiḥ eva sākṣāt yogi pratyakṣasya kaṇṭha ukteḥ tasya saṃbhavataḥ  api āgamikeśvara jñāna mūlasya āgama anuvādatva āpādanā śaktyā tatra audāsīnyāt dharma ādayaḥ kasyacid indriya grāhyāḥ prameya tvāt  ghaṭavat  mīmāṃsakānām apratyakṣa tvāt vā asmad sukha ādivat iti ādi anumānānām vipakṣe bādhaka viraha ādibhiḥ ābhāsa tvāt  āgama bādha prasaṅgasya eva puraskāre tu āgamena eva caritārtha tvāt anyathā dharma ādayaḥ kasyacid cakṣuḥ grāhyā iti vadataḥ  bauddhasya kim prativakṣyasi yaḥ ca anuvyavasāye sa viṣaya vyavasāya pratyakṣatām icchati tasya asmad ādiṣu api dharma ādi vyavasāya anuvyavasāye dharma ādi pratyakṣatva siddhau katham tad atirikta yogi pratyakṣa anumā siddhiḥ tad vyavacchedena prayoge api saugata ukta cākṣuṣatva ādi sādhana prasaṅga syāt iti sa ca adṛṣṭa viśeṣaḥ  yoga abhyāsa tapaḥ cārya ādibhiḥ jāyate tasmāt ārṣa abhimatam api prakṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa jatvā viśeṣāt tatra eva antarbhūtam yathā uktam prajñā paritrāṇe atra indriya anapekṣam yad jñānam artha avabhāsakam divyam pramāṇam iti etad  pramāṇa jñāḥ pracakṣate parameśvara vijñānam muktānām ca dhiyaḥ tathā saṃjaya arjuna vālmīki prabhṛti ārṣadhi yaḥ  api tad  iti indriya anapekṣam itia divyenḥ diyā anapekṣam iti arthaḥ ata eva hi gīyate divyam dadāmi te cakṣuḥ ityādi yadvā aparameśvara ādi vijñāna saha pāṭhā ādibhiḥ tathā eva mantavyam anantaram ca evam uktam svābhāvikasya jñānasya svatas  sarva avabhāsinaḥ avidyā pratibandhasya pratibandhaḥ  akṣa yogataḥ avidyā hānitaḥ  mukta puruṣāṇām hi saṃvidām svābhāvika svarūpeṇa nikhila artha avabhāsitā pratibandhaka bhāvasya pratyuttambhaka bhāvinā pareṇa anugṛhītā dhīḥ ṛṣīṇām sarva bhāsikā iti mānasa pratyakṣam api asmad ādīnām na asti eva iti vṛddha saṃpradāyaḥ ātma svarūpasya tad dharma bhūta jñānasya ca svayaṃprakāśa tvāt  sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnānām tad tad hetu tayā abhimata jñāna viśeṣānatiḥ ekasya veda artha saṃgrahe samarthita tvāt  nityatva ādi viśiṣṭa asmad ādi anubhavasya śāstra ādi prasiddha tvāt pūrva anubhava ādi jñānasya smṛti rūpa tvāt  ātma sukha ādi vyatirikta bahis viṣayeṣu tasya bāhya indriya anapekṣa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ iti śāstra yoni adhikaraṇa bhāṣyasya anvāroheṇa api upapatteḥ iti tatas ca ādivya bāhya indriya prasūtam jñānam ayogi pratyakṣam tad  sāmānya adṛṣṭa āloka viśeṣa ādi saha kṛta indriya janyam dṛṣṭa sāmagrī viśeṣāt pratiniyata aviṣayam tad  śrotra ādi indriyāsādhāraṇa kāraṇa bhedāt  pañcadhā viṣaya indriya saṃbandhaḥ ca dravyeṣu saṃyogaḥ dravya āśriteṣu rūpa ādiṣu tu saṃyukta āśrayaṇam yathā uktam tattva ratna ākare atra vṛddhā vidāmāsuḥ saṃyogaḥ saṃnikarṣaṇam saṃyukta āśrayaṇam ca iti yathāsaṃbhavam ūhyatām iti punar  pratyakṣam dvidhā sa vikalpakam nirvikalpakam ca iti sa pratyavamarśam pratayakṣam sa vikalpakam tad rahitam pratyakṣam nirvikalpakam naiyāyika nirvikalpaka nirākaraṇam ubhayavidham api etad viśiṣṭa viṣayam eva aviśiṣṭa vastu grāhiṇaḥ  jñānasya anupalambhāt  anupapatteḥ ca bāla mūka tiryak ādi vijñānam api hi saṃjñā vikalpa rahitam api viśiṣṭa vastu viṣayam eva anyathā teṣām heya upādeya vibhāga pūrvaka pravṛtti śeṣa anupapatteḥ vipratipannam viśiṣṭa jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna pūrvakam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt  surabhi candanam ityādi viśiṣṭa jñānavat iti ced na eka sāmagrī vedya viśeṣaṇeṣu tad nirapekṣa tvāt  svarūpa saṃbandha pakṣe svarūpa graheṇa eva saṃbandhasya api grahaṇāt  tāvatā eva viśiṣṭa grahaṇa siddheḥ samavāya vāde api tasya eva gṛhyamāṇasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva rūpa tvāt samavāya viśiṣṭa pratyaye tathā eva abhyupagamāt tad vaiśiṣṭya grahe ca guṇa vaiśiṣṭya grahasya āvarjanīya tvāt  na ca samavāyasya sa vikalpaka eka viṣaya tā iti vācyam nirvikalpake dharmavat harmivat ca tad saṃbandhasya api aindriyikatva aviśeṣeṇa grahaṇa saṃbhavāt  yogyasya saṃnikṛṣṭa gṛhyamāṇa saṃbandhinaḥ saṃbandhasya agrahaṇa anupapatteḥ anyathā nityam tad agraha āpātāt  prathama akṣa saṃnipāta jā buddhiḥ viśiṣṭa viṣayā buddhi tvāt  saṃpratipannavat  ityādi api cintyam sa vikalpaka nirūpaṇam na ca sa vikalpakam na pratyakṣam iti vācyam sākṣātkāra ābādhādya viśeṣāt sahakāri viśeṣeṇa na vaijātyam prasajyate tad jātīye tu yad kiñcid vaiṣamyam saṃbhavet api yatra dṛśyeta vaijātyam tathā tatra abhyupeyate tāvatā na eva sarvatra bhavet etasya kalpanam kevala indriya jam ca api na kiñcid jñānam iṣyate sahakāri viśeṣām hi vibhidyante pratīndriyam atas  saṃskāra saṃbhede api aparokṣatva yogataḥ pratyakṣa tvam vikalpasya na kvacid vinivartate nirvikalpakam eka jātīyeṣu dravyeṣu prathama piṇḍa grahaṇam ityādi bhāṣyam tu udāharaṇa param yojyam ata eva hi śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ uktam saṃskāra udbodha saha kṛta indriya janyam jñānam sa vikalpakam eka jātīyeṣu prathama piṇḍa grahaṇam dvitīya ādi piṇḍa grahaṇeṣu prathama akṣa saṃnipāta jam ca jñānam nirvikalpakam iti anyatra ca uktam kevala cakṣuḥ ādi indriya janyam nirvikalpakam ityādi yad tu uktam tattva ratna ākare viśeṣaṇānām svāyoga vyāvṛttiḥ avikalpake sa vikalpe anya yogasya vyāvṛttiḥ saṃjñitā tathā iti tatra api saṃskāra nirapekṣatva sāpekṣa tvayoḥ pradarśana para tvam grāhyam pratyakṣasya ca evam vibhāgaḥ  abhihitaḥ dvividham ca etad  pratyakṣam arvācīnam anarvācīnam ca yugapad aśeṣa viṣaya sākṣātkāra kṣamama narvācīnam tad  yogi mukteśvarāṇām prabhāva viśeṣa adhīnam upapādayiṣyate ityādi ata eva kudṛṣṭīnām sat mātra grāhi pratyakṣam iti avilakṣa jalpitam nirastam krama yaugapadya ādi dūṣaṇam tu bhrānti vikalpe api samānam bhrānti rūpaḥ  api hi vikalpaḥ kṣaṇika tvāt na viramya vyāpartu malam na ca pūrva jñāna vārtām jānāti na ca svayam dharmi pratiyogi grahaṇa abhāve bheda grahaṇam manyase tathā api yadi kalpanā bheda viśiṣṭam yugapad gṛhṇāti kā pratyakṣe sarpa mṛtiḥ atas  dharmivat yogya tvāt jātya ādi rūpa bhedaḥ  api yugapad grāhyeḥ abheda iva bhedaḥ  api svarūpataḥ pratītau na pratiyogi sākāṅkṣaḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ tu abheda vyavahāravat tad sākāṅkṣa atas  prathamam eva bheda dhīḥ yuktā ata eva dharma dharmiṇoḥ dharmi pratiyoginoḥ anyeṣām ca pratītau  anyonya āśrayaḥ  nirastaḥ tatas ca vyupatteḥ tad vyavahāre api na tad prasaṅgaḥ bheda śabdena vyavahārasya tu pratisaṃbandhi nirūpita ākāre vyutpanna tvāt  tad apekṣā bheda tvam hi bhedānām pratiyoginā nirūpyam na tu jāti ādi lakṣaṇam svarūpam yad grahaḥ  yatra yadārā upavirodhī sa hi tasya tasmāt bhedaḥ gaḥtva ādi ca gṛhyamāṇam svasmin sva āśraye ca aśvatva ādi āropam nirūṇaddhi iti svasya sva āśrayasya ca svayam eva tasmāt bhedaḥ api ca pratiyogi sāpekṣatva nirapekṣatva lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsena bhedāt  svarūpa bheda grahaṇa aikyām na saṃbhavati iti vadan bheda t uṣaṇa artham eva bhedam sādhayati iti sva vacana virodha iti śābda aparokṣa nirāsaḥ śabda janyam api pratyakṣam asti iti ta eva varṇayanti tad api ayuktam vyāghātāt  na hi parokṣa janana svabhāva tayā siddhā sāmagrī viśeṣa abhāve kvacid  svabhāvam atipatet na ca eka jātīya sāmagrītaḥ prasūtam kāryam vicitram syāt  ekayā evava sāmagryā sarva jātīya utpatti prasaṅgāt  ekasya kāryasya viruddha jāti yoga prasaṅgāt ca daśamaḥ tvam asi ityādi dṛṣṭānte api tvam artha mātram pratyakṣam adaśamaḥ  aham iti pratyayaḥ hi na indriya svātantryeṇa udeti kintu puruṣa vacana anurodhena tad mūle api ced  pratyakṣatā evam adharmavān  tvamasi iti kārtāntika upadeśa ādau atādṛśaḥ  aham asmi iti bodhe dharma ādeḥ api pratyakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca apratyakṣam iti jagati kiñcid na syāt  pratyakṣa bhūtam yad kiñcid uddiśya viśeṣaṇa tayā eva sarvasya pratyakṣatva upapatteḥ pūrva avagata daśama bhāvam tu puruṣam pratyupadeśe bhāṣara āśi praviṣṭa maṣī nyāyena pūrva apara aparokṣaṇī nairantaryeṇa madhya varti śabda janya dhiyaḥ aparokṣatva vyavahāraḥ kasyacid  syāt vā na vā ata eva tad tvam asya ādi śabdaḥ sva viṣaya gocara pratyakṣa jñāna janakaḥ svatas  aparokṣa artha gocara tvāt daśamaḥ tvam asi saṃvid  sva prakāśā ityādi vākyavat  ityādi anumānāni nirastāni daśamatva svaprakāśatva ādi viśiṣṭa ākāreṇa dṛṣṭānteṣu aparokṣa jñāna janana asiddheḥ tathā vigītaḥ śabdaḥ  na sva vācya gocara pratyakṣadhījanakaḥ śabda tvāt  saṃpratipannavat  iti ādi apipratiprayoktavyam upalambha virodha śābda pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa saṃkara ādi prasaṅgaḥ  atra vipakṣe bādhakaḥ na evam pūrvasya śabda janya pratyakṣam antareṇa api yoga ja adṛṣṭa janita sākṣātkārāt praṇidhāna viśeṣa prasādita paramātma saṃkalpāt vā niḥśreyasa siddheḥ iti pratyakṣam cit acit mayam jagat idam yasya iti anuśrūyate yaḥ ca ananya dhiyām ananta vibhavaḥ pratyakṣatām aśnute yaḥ ca ekaḥ yugapad sadā svata idam viśvam darī dṛśyate prājñam tam pratipanna mokṣaṇa vidhāt akṣam didṛkṣemahi iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedānta ācāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau pratyakṣa adhyāye dvitīyam āhnikam atha anumodayam smṛtyā hetu tvena api saṃsthitm madhye tayoḥ ihetadānīm mānam śabdam pracakṣmahe anāpta anukta vākya janitam tad artha vijñānam tad  pramāṇam kāraṇa doṣa bādhaka adarśanāt  naca an āpta ukta vākyam pramāṇam kāraṇa doṣa bādhaka darśanāt na ca vākyatva ādibhiḥ bādhaḥ sva vacana virodhāt  yadi bādhaka upanyāsa vākyam ayathārtham tadā katham bādhaḥ atha yathārtham tasya api pakṣīkāre tad bādhaḥ bahiṣkāre tena eva anaikāntyam na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ bhrānta ādi vākyānām doṣa mūla tvasya durapahnava tvāt  atra tu tad abhāvāt utsvapnāyita ghuṇa kṣata akṣara ādīnām tu viśiṣṭa tātparya viraheṇa bodhaka tvepi anāśvasanīya tvāt vyabhicāra darśanāt ca nityepi vede nityeśvara śāsana ātmani tad tad artha tātparyānapāyāt tasya ca atra abhāvāt  kvācid ka doṣa darśanasya ca pratyakṣa ādau  api asamatvāt  svatas  paratas  vā prāmāṇye ca tatas  viśeṣa abhāvāt tad ca vedya aṃśe pratyakṣa atiriktam asākṣātkāri tvāt  anumānavat  anumāna atiriktam pakṣa liṅga parāmarśa ādi adṛṣṭeḥ pada vākya tad saṃbandha ādīnām ca viśiṣṭa vākya artham pratyasiddha vyāptika tvena āliṅga tvāt dṛṣṭānta abhyupagame sarvatra aviśeṣāt vyutpattau ca svatantra tayā eva bodhakatva siddheḥ ata eva vaktṛ jñāna anumāna abhyupagamepi śabda prāmāṇyam siddham āgamika buddhiḥ anumā pratyakṣa itara pramiti tvāt  saṃpratipannavat iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt  anyathā śabda rasa gandha ādi buddhiḥ anumā acākṣuṣa pramiti tvāt  saṃpratipannavat  iti api prasaṅgāt  pratyakṣam anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam dṛṣṭa anumāna āgama jam iti manu ādi mahā ṛṣi saṃmateḥ ca śabda anumānayoḥ bheda udṛśyate na ca atra gaḥ balī vardanayaḥ antarbhāva adarśanāt  āgāmonumānam saṃbandha grahaṇe sati eva bodhaka tvāt iti ced na bodhya bodhaka bhāva atirikta saṃbandha grahaṇa apekṣiṇī anumānatva niyamāt na ca atra tad atiriktaḥ saṃbandhaḥ yad grahaṇam niyamena apekṣyeta anyathā saṃbandha sāpekṣa tayā tayoḥ pratyakṣa tvasya api su sādha tvāt iti na ca smṛtiḥ apūrva viṣaya tvāt  pada saṃdoha viśeṣaḥ  vākyam prāmāṇika pada vyavahāra viṣayaḥ padam tasya suptiṅantatva ādi kalpanayā api vyaktiḥ kriyate ata eva hi anyathā anyathā prakṛti pratyaya ādikam vyākaraṇa antareṣu kalpyate tad ca na sāṃketikam saṃketayitṛ puruṣa asaṃbhavāt ata eva na bhāṣā antaravat tad klaptiḥ nitya veda gata tvāt ca yāni vaidikāni padāni tāni eva laukikanī iti veda śabdebhyaḥ  eva ādau ityādi vacanāt api siddham bhāṣāt chandasoḥ tu katipaya śabdānām lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ tad tad ānupūrvī pratiniyama apekṣaḥ bhāṣā prayuktaḥ sarva upi vede kvāpi prayogavān veda eka niyataḥ śabdaḥ  na anyatra iti vyavasthitiḥ uktam ca etad veda artha saṃgrahepi vaidikā eva sarve vācakāḥ śabdāḥ ca ityādinā vākyam dvidhā pauruṣeya apauruṣeya bhedāt  puruṣa svātantrya adhīna racanā viśeṣa viśiṣṭam pauruṣeyam tad dvidhā anvita artham ananvita artham ca ādyam yathāagniḥ uṣṇaḥ āpaḥ  dravāḥ iti dvitīyam yathāagniḥ anuṣṇaḥ āpaḥ kaṭhināḥ iti atra eka deśinaḥ  vadantiananvaya āgrahāt anvita vyavahāraḥ kvacid jāyata iti ata eva laukika vākye dṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya na jhaṭati vākyāt vākya artha adhyavasāyaḥ yogya tā vimarśa sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt  sāmānya yogya tā grahaṇepi vyakti yogyatāyāḥ vaktṛ jñāna anumāna m anteraṇa asiddheḥ iti prameya saṃgraha ādiṣu samarthitam tathā asat mātra grāhi pratyakṣa nirākaraṇāya śāstrasya anuvādakatva prasaṅge vivaraṇa kāraiḥ uktam abuddha bodhana svarasasya śabdasya ātathātvam doṣa iti abhisandhiḥ athavā anuvādaka tvam eva syāt  na hi māna antara pratīterthe śabdaḥ pramāṇam tathā eva hi tasya vyutpattiḥ iti uktvā nanu anuvādaka tayā eva vyutpattiḥ puṃvākyeṣu ityādinā vaktṛ jñāna anumānam upapādya satyam daivāt  tad anuvādakatvam iti na abuddha bodhana svārasya bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ yathā smṛti anumita vedasya anuvādakatva ipi arthāt iti na mānatā bhaṅgaḥ ityādi uktam ca prajñā paritrāṇe pauruṣeya giraḥ śaṅkā grastā na sahasā mitim janayanti na yāvat  tad mūla mānānavagrahaḥ anumāya ca vaktuḥ tad mūla yogya pramā antaram tad ukta vākya liṅgena vākya artham anujānate anvita artha abhidhānāya yogyam vākyam idam sadā asau ca na anṛtam vakti saṃjñātva artham tad abravīt vaktṛ jñāna anumānena jñāta ajñāta sva vākyataḥ anvita artha abhidhāyitva yogya tā mātra dhīrgirām parāmarśa iti prāptaḥ  na artha saṃsarga gocaraḥ māna antara avirodhi tvam yogyatā iti abhidhīyate nanu evam laukikam vākyam liṅgam ced liṅgavat  tatas  śabdaḥ  gṛhīta saṃbandhāt  tadvat asya api liṅga tā vyutpatti kāle vyutpitsoḥ liṅga dhīḥ na asti asaṃśayāt yathāvyutpatti śabdāḥ tu bodhakā iti ced atas svata eva artha bodhaḥ syāt iti na eva asya liṅga tā ityādi bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ tu āgama pramāṇye vaktṛ jñāna anumānam dūṣitam nigamitam ca tasmāt asti nadī tīre phalam iti evamādiṣu yā siddha viṣayā buddhiḥ sā śabdī na anumānukī iti ayam eva pakṣonusṛtaḥ  vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ tattva ratna ākarepya āgama prāmāṇya grantha upādāna pūrvakam prapañcitam etad  apauruṣeyam tu sarvam anvita artham eva akintu ādityaḥ  yūpaḥ iti ādiṣu upacārataḥ  nirvāhaḥ ākāṅkṣā satti vogya tāvanti hi padāni anvitam abhidadhati anvaye vā viśrāmyanti āditya yūpa padayoḥ pratyakṣa siddha sva artha bhedayoḥ ayogya tayā mukhya vṛtti parityāgaḥ vṛttiḥ dvidhāabhidhā upacāra bhedāt  vyutpatti siddhārtha  eva vṛttiḥ abhidhā yathā siṃha śabdaspaya mṛgendre sā jāti guṇa ādi viṣaya bhedāt  yoga rūḍhi tad samuccaya bhedāt ca bahuvidhā mukhya artha bādhe sati tad āsanne vṛttiḥ upacāraḥ āsattiḥ ca dvividhā mukhya artha saṃbandhaḥ tad guṇa saṃbandhaḥ ca iti tatra pūrveṇa pravṛttiḥ lakṣaṇā yathāgaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ prativasati iti atra gaṅga śabdasya pravāha viśeṣa rūpa vācya saṃbandhini tīre evam lakṣita lakṣaṇā grāhyā dvitīyena pravṛttiḥ gauṇī yathā siṃhaḥ  devadatta iti atra siṃhma śabdasya śaurya ādi gūṇaṇyogini devadatte tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam abhidhāna abhidheya tvam atas  śabda arthayoḥ sthitam saṃbandhotra abhidhā dvedhā bodhyā mukhya jaghanyatas  abhidhā artha  agatya ātmā śabdam vyāpārayiṣyataḥ śabda śakti nimittā sā sva arthe mukhya abhidhīyate sva artha abhidhāna dvārā syāt jaghanya artha antare matā iti tad vistaraḥ tatra eva dgaṣṭavyaḥ na ca gauṇalākṣaṇika prayogayoḥ avācya viṣaya tvāt avācya tvam saṃbandha sādṛśya mātra pravṛttepi ana ādi tvāt tatas  eva vivakṣita sthale yathā aucityam prayoga upapatteḥ etāḥ sarvā api vṛttayaḥ anvita abhidhāna vṛtti antarbhūtāḥ pṛthak padānām smāraka tvam eva abhihita anvaye hi padānām padārthe padārthānām vāvayārthe padānām ca tatra iti śakti traya kalpanāgāra evam syāt  vākya arthasya āśābdatva prasaṅgaḥ  vā padārthe lakṣaṇa samāpteḥ pramāṇa prasaṅgaḥ ca naca anvitā abhidhānenyonya āśrayaṇam mithas  smaraṇa mātra upajīvanāt yathā āhuḥ pada jātam śrutam sarvam smāritān anvita arthakam nyāya saṃpādita vyakti paścāt vākya artha bodhakam iti na api paunarukti ādi doṣaḥ tad tad aṃśa pratiniyata śakti tvāt na api vākya bhedaḥ eka pradhāna tayā sva artha abhidhānāt  padārtha eva vākya arthaḥ saṃsṛṣṭaḥ  hi abhidhīyate iti uktam tathā nānā śabda ādi bhedāt  iti ādhikaraṇe yadi api aveda aupāsīta ityādayaḥ śabdāḥ pratyaya āvṛtti abhidhāyinaḥ pratyayāḥ ca brahma eka viṣayāḥ tathā api tad tad prakaraṇa udita jagat eka kāraṇatva apahata pāpmatva ādi viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa brahma viṣaya pratyaya āvṛtti avabodhinaḥ pratyaya āvṛtti rūpā vidyā bhindanti iti veda artha saṃgrahepi śodhakeṣu api asatyam jñānam anantam brahma aānandaḥ  brahma ityādiṣu sāmānādhikaraṇya vyutpatti siddha an eka guṇa viśiṣṭhā eka artha abhidhānam aviruddham iti sarva viśiṣṭam brahma eva abhidhīyate iti atra eva pūrva bhāge samabhivyāhṛta pada antara vācyā anvaya yogyam eva itara pada pratipādyam iti anvita abhidhāyi pada saṃghāta rūpa vākya śravaṇa samanantaram eva pratīyate tad ca svarga sādhanatva rūpam atas  kriyāvat ananyā artha tā virodhāt eva parityaktā iti eṣām svārasyam anvita abhidhāne na ca atra para abhyupagamena uktam iti jñāpakam asti vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ api satya jñāna ādi padānām akhaṇḍa ekarasa artha tve anvita abhidhāna anupapatteḥ ca ityādiṣu bahuṣu pradeśeṣu anvita abhidhānam eva māyā vādinam pratyuktam uktam ca āgama prāmāṇye anya anvitā abhidhānepi vyavahāra upapattitaḥ avaśya āśrayaṇīyā iyam anvita artha abhidhāyitā iti ārabhya tasmāt ākāṅkṣita āsanna yogya artha antara saṅgate sva arthe padānām vyutpattiḥ āstheyā sarva vādibhiḥ iti tattva ratnākarepi avaśya āśrayaṇīyā iyam anvita artha abhidhāyitā iti āhuḥ yāmunā ācāryāḥ padaiḥ eva anvitā abhidhām iti ārabhya prapañcena upapādya upasaṃhṛtam ṣaḍbhiḥ pratīti pramukha upapattibhi rnirdhūta codyābhiḥ iha anvitā abhidhā siddhā padaiḥ na abhihita anvaya sthiti rvi paryayāt iti akhilam samañjasam iti prajñā paritrāṇa nyāya su darśanayoḥ ca bahuśa uktam anvita artha abhidhāyi tvam śabda śakti nibandhanam vyutpatti avagatam pundhī doṣa tosya viparyayaḥ ityādinā nanu abhihita anvaya t yotakāni api vākyāni vidyante veda artha saṃgrahe tāvat  evam bodhakānām pada saṃghātānām saṃsarga viśeṣa bodhanena vākya śabda abhidheyānām uccāraṇa kramaḥ  yatra puruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ iti ādi uktam tathā tatra eva prakṛti pratyaya rūpeṇa padasya eva aneka viśeṣaṇa garbha tvāt  aneka padārtha saṃsarga bodhaka tvāt ca vākyasya iti bhāṣyepi śabdasya tu viśeṣeṇa sa viśeṣa eva vastuni abhidhāna sāmarthyam pada vākya rūpeṇa pravṛtteḥ prakṛti pratyaya yogena hi padatvam prakṛti pratyayoḥ artha bhedena padasya eva viśiṣṭa artha pratipādanam avarjanīyam pada bhedaḥ ca artha bheda nibandhanaḥ pada saṃghāta rūpasya vākyasya aneka padārtha saṃsarga aviśeṣa abhidhāyi tvena iti ādi uktam evam vyutpatti nirūpaṇe veda artha saṃgrahe siddha vastuṣu śabdasya bodhakatva śakti grahaṇam atyanta sukaram iti upakramya apavarake daṇḍaḥ sthitaḥ iti vākye yādṛcchika vyutpatti prakāram upapādya tathā bālaḥ atātoyam anbaiṣā ityādinā buddhi pūrva vyutpādanena tad tad padānām tad tad padārtheṣu eva bodhakatva śakti grahaṇam upapādya punar api asya śabdasya ayam artha iti pūrva vṛddhaiḥ śikṣitaḥ ityādi ca uktvā evam eva sarva padānām sva artha abhidhāyi tvam saṃghāta viśeṣāṇām ca yathā avasthita saṃsarga viśeṣa vāci tvam ca jānāti iti ādi uktam bhāṣyepi prathama sūtra pūrva pakṣa nirākaraṇe evam kila laukikāḥ śabda artha saṃbandham avadhāra yanti mātā pitṛ prabhṛtibhiḥ ambā tāta mātula ādīn ityādinā pada vyutpattiḥ pūrvam upapāditā tatra ca teṣu teṣu artheṣu teṣām śabdānām prayogaḥ  bodhakatva nibandhanaḥ iti niścinvanti iti ādi uktam punar ca vyutpanna itara śabdeṣu asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ iti pūrva vṛddhaiḥ śikṣitāḥ ityādi yadi nāma anvita abhidhānam abhimatam tadā katham iva pada mātre vyutpattiḥ syāt  yadi ca sā syāt  katham anvitam abhidheyam vyutpatti vaiparītya prasaṅgāt  tasmāt na anvitā abhidhānam eva siddhānta iti nirṇetum śakyam iti kecid  anye tu bodhakānām ityādi vākyam anvite saṃsarga viśeṣa siddheḥ upapadyate pada vākya bheda abhidhānam api tad tad viśeṣa vaiśiṣṭya pradarśana mātra artham para abhyupagamat yotana artham vā pratyeka pada vyutpatti abhidhānam api anvita artha bodhana upayukta asādhāraṇa dvāra prakāśana mātram padārtham smārayitvā eva hi padāni vakya artham bodhayanti iti uktan smṛteḥ ca sva anubhūti mūla tvāt na śakti antara kḷptiḥ vyākhyātam ca bhāṣya ādikam anvita para tayā vivaraṇe śrī rāma miśraiḥ tathā ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepepi śabdaḥ ca svatas  śakyam anvita tayā bodhayati asaṃbhghavertha antaram iti hi vyutpattiḥ iti ādi uktam atas nvita abhidhānam siddhāntaḥ iti evam anvita abhidhāna sāmarthyāt viśiṣṭa pratipatti anyathā anupapatteḥ ca padānām api viśiṣṭa abhidhāyi tvam siddham ata eva viśiṣṭa artha abhidhāyitvepi viśeṣaṇam atre śaktiḥ iti api nirastam abhidhāyitvā atirikta śakti antara abhāvāt aparyavasāna vacanam api viśiṣṭa bodhana śaktasya viśeṣaṇa mātre sthātum aśakta tvāt  viśiṣṭa anupraviṣṭam hi viśeṣaṇam pareparañjaka veṣam eva iti tādṛś ākāraḥ  viśeṣya grahaṇam antareṇa durgrahaḥ tāvatā ca tad artham viśeṣya grahaṇam iti vyartham vacaḥ yathāprati iti vyavasthāpanasya eva yukta tvāt  kim ca gavā ādi śabda abhihita gaḥtva ādi artha svabhāvataḥ vyakti dhīrya di tadvat  syāt  niṣkarṣaka padeṣu api gavā ādi śabdā jāti ādīn paratantrān pracakṣate tena āśraya pratītiḥ ced  tad naḥ siddhaḥ samīhitam param katham avijñāpya pāratantryasya bodhanam vijñāpya yadi śabdasya tatra śaktiḥ na kim bhavet  parasya paratantreṇa tathā buddhena bodhanam tad buddhyā paratantrasya bodhanenyonya saṃśrayaḥ para dhīniḥ apekṣam ced  pāratantryam pratīyate na tena para buddhiḥ syāt niṣkṛṣṭa pratipattivat  pāratantryam svarūpam ced  tulyam niṣkarṣa kepi tad  adhikam dharmi niṣṭha tvāt anyat na upalabhāmahe pada antara parāmarśa nirapekṣa pratītike nirūḍha lakṣaṇauvādāḥ paryāya avṛtti gocarāḥ vyakteḥ gauritya niṣkarṣāt niṣkarṣe tvādi apekṣaṇāt niṣkarṣakeṣu adṛṣṭeḥ ca na jātyā vyakti lakṣaṇā ākṛtau  eva yaḥ śaktim śabdānām abhimanyate sattāyām eva kim tena sarveṣām na abhyupeyate atas  gavā ādi śabdebhyaḥ  viśiṣṭa viṣayā matiḥ śabda śakti prasūtā iti balāt abhyupagamyatām yad tu na loka vyutpatti haniḥ tatra eva śakteḥ iti ṣaṣ artha saṃkṣepe śrī rāma miśraiḥ uktam tad api tatra śakti abhāva pratikṣepa param asamāpta dhīḥ tu vedānta aśruteḥ bhramaḥ āpāta vyutpattyā śruteḥ tad pūrtiḥ iti anantaram abhidhānāt  yad ca ātma siddhau yathā gavā ādi pada śaktiḥ ekabuddhi siddhepi sāmānya viśeṣa ātmake vastuni sāmānya aṃśena saṃbadhyate iti tad api para abhyupagata udāharaṇam anya artham yathā iti para saṃpratipanna nidarśanāt  guṇa vācini api pade jāti śabda ukta nītitaḥ apṛthak siddha vāci tvāt na yuktā guṇi lakṣaṇā svara liṅga viśeṣa uttha mantra lope na saṃskriyā viśiṣṭa vācaka tvam tu tadāthattam na manmahe atas  niṣkarṣaka śabda atiriktānām apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa vācinām viśeṣya paryavasāna vyutpatteḥ śarīra vācinām deva ādi śabdānām api yathā prayogam śarīri paryavasānam siddham ata eva ca ātma pṛthivī ādi śabdānām īśvara paryanta tā tena sarvaṃsvatu idam brahma jyotīṃṣi viṣṇuḥ ayam ātmā abrahya tad tvam asi ityādi sāmānādhikaraṇyam tad tad prakāraka brahma param nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam ca tad anupraveśāt ata eva ca tasya sarva śabda vācya tvam api śrūyateth tad eva ca vyajyate tad anupraviśya sat ca tyat ca abhavat iti smaryate ca sarvam samāpnoṣi tatosi sarvaḥ iti sūtritam ca carācara vyapāśrayaḥ tu syāt  tad vyapadeśaḥ  bhāktaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt iti uktam ca vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ svarga kāma śabdena kāmyamāna svargaḥ puruṣobhidhīyate na hi īśvara uvāpta samasta kāmaḥ svargam kāmayate tasya ati alpa sukha tvāt atas  vācya eka deśe jīve lakṣaṇā gaṅgā śabdasya tīra  iva iti yad vā svarga kāma ādi śabdānām api jīvādi mātrepi mukhya tvam eva pravṛtti nimitta aparityāgāt  ata eva hi bhākta padasya bhaktyā vyapadeśa artha tvam api bhāṣya kāraiḥ uktam viśiṣṭa veṣasya śakti viṣaya tvāt  tad tyoge katham na lakṣaṇa iti ced  aparityakta pravṛtti nimittasya vyutpatti anupraviṣṭa mātra bodhanam mukhya tā tad abhāva kṛta upacāra iti vyavasthānāt  nanu tad tvam asi iti atra tvam iti śvetaketu mātra nirdeśe tad asi iti sāmānādhikaraṇyā yogaḥ śvetaketu śarīrakeśvara nirdeśe tad ā abhimukhyena upadeśa ayogaḥ tad uddeśena tvam artha vidhānam ca asi śabdān anvaya ādinā dūra nirastam prāpta artha tayā nigamana rūpa tvepi pava viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhedaḥ  niṣkarṣaṇīyaḥ evam aham brahmā asmi ityādi vyapadeśa upi durnirvahaḥ jīvena ātmanā iti atra api ātma śabdena jīva ātma ādi abhidhānam ṣāṣyakāra vacana viruddham jīvena mayā ityādi vyapadeśāt paramātma abhidhāne tu tṛtīyā anupapattiḥ vyākaravāṇi iti abhihita tvāt  kriyā abhedepi kṛtvā ādeḥ uttara kriyā eka rasyāt kartṛ antara āyuktiḥ samāna kartṛkatva virodhāt karaṇatva vivakṣayā kartari tṛtīyāyām mukhyatva hāniḥ atas cāreṇa anupraviśya para balam saṃkalayānītivat jīvasya vai praviśati kartṛ tvam paraḥ tu vyākaraṇa mātra kartā tāvatā tu śabdānām na tad paryantatva siddhiḥ iti atra ucyate saṃbuddhiḥ tāvat atra ātma vidyā upadeśena śvetaketu mātra paryavasitā iti na asaṃbodhya saṃbodhanam vacana vyaktiḥ ca tad asi iti eva tatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvena śarīra ātma bhāvena vā sāmānādhikaraṇya nirvāhaḥ ubhayatra tvaṃśabdasya api tad śabda abhihita dravya paryavasānam siddham dharma antara viśeṣyasya dharma antara viśeṣyataḥ svasmāt abhedaḥ tādātmyam syāt upādāna dehinoḥ atas tvad śarīrakam brahma iti vivakṣāyām satyām tvam tad iti nirdeśa mātram upapannam madhyama puruṣaḥ ca tvaṃśabda prayoga nibandhanaḥ yuṣmadi upapade samāna adhikaraṇe sthāninī api madhyamaḥ iti vidhānāt  atas  sā upi tvaṃśabda paryavasāna viṣaya paryavasitaḥ yad vā tad  tvam asi iti eva anvayoḥ tu na ca uddeśya anuguṇā tiṅvibhaktiḥ iti niyamaḥ upādeya anuguṇa liṅga vacana ādi nirdeśavat atra api virodha abhāvāt prayuñjate ca patañjali prabhṛtaya upādeya anuguṇām api tiṅvibhaktim sa punarāvṛttaḥ suvarṇa piṇḍaḥ khadira aṅgāra savarṇe kuṇḍale bhavataḥ ityādiṣu etena aham brahmā asmi iti ādikam api nirvyūḍham jīvena ātmānā iti atra api anena nyāyena sva śabda paryāyeṇa ātma śabdena jīva śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam tāvat  siddham tṛtīyā anupapattiḥ tu svarūpa tādātmya pakṣe pṛthaktva pakṣe ca samānā atha aṃśa bheda ādinā vibhajya karaṇatva ādi vivakṣayā kathañcid nirvāhaḥ tathā viśiṣṭa ākāra ādi bheda vivakṣayā vibhajya atra api nirvāham anumanyethāḥ atas  śruti ādi vākyeṣu viruddha artha anubandhinaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya na svarūpa aikya niṣṭhatā kārya tvāt apṛthak siddheḥ āviśāt anukārataḥ asti sṛṣṭi upakāra ādeḥ sāmānādhikaraṇya dhīḥ na ca tvad dṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ sthāṇuḥ itivat  puruṣa eva idam sarvam tad tvam asi iti ādau bādha artham sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti vācyam mukhya vṛtti saṃbhave tad ayogāt  prapañca satyatva ādeḥ ca ābādhita pratyakṣa ādi bala siddha tvāt cit aṃśa sāmānādhikaraṇyam tu na bādha saham tvayā api tad satyatva abhyupagamāt svarūpa aikya vidhāne ca viruddha dharma pratirodhāt  tad parityāge padayoḥ anatirikta artha tayā paryāya pada sā mānādhikaraṇya prasaṅgāt  dvāra abhāvena mukhya vṛtti bādha āpatteḥ gati antare ca saṃbhavati tad ayogāt  sva rūpa mātra nirdeśe ca pada antara vaiyarthyāt  svarūpa bhedasya ca bahu pramāṇa siddha tvāt satyam jñānam ityādi lakṣaṇa vākyam api satyatva ādi viśiṣṭa eka viṣayam tathā eva sāmānādhikaraṇya vyutpatteḥ na ca atra viśeṣaṇa bhedāt viviśeṣya bheda aprasaṅgaḥ viruddha viśeṣaṇa abhāvāt na hi ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu iva virodhaḥ yathā ca pratyakṣe nīlatva utpalatva ādeḥ avirodhaḥ  darśana balāt  tathā atra api na ca satyatva jñānatva ādeḥ vaiyadhikaraṇya niyamaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ yena virodhaḥ syāt  viśeṣya aikya pare tu sāmānādhikaraṇye viśeṣaṇānām viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ ca mithas  bhedaḥ  guṇa eva na ca viśeṣī aikyavat viśeṣaṇa viśeṣī aikya prasaktiḥ viśeṣaṇānām aikya prasaktiḥ vā lakṣaṇa avirodha ādi doṣāt atatha avyutpatteḥ ca na api viśiṣṭe viśiṣṭa antara vidhānāt viśeṣaṇānām mithas  samavāya ādi doṣaḥ yugapad aneka viśiṣṭa eka abhidhānāt anūdya vidhāneṣu api yathā vyutpatti dharma pradhāna tvāt ca na ca viśeṣaṇam sarvam viśeṣaṇa antara asaham virodhi mātra virodhi tvāt anyathā pratyakṣa virodhāt  sādhya sādhaka dharma ādi viśiṣṭa viṣaya anumāna ādi anudaya prasaṅgāt  evantvāt idam viśiṣṭa bodhakam na bhavati ityādi vyavahārasya api vilopaḥ syāt  na ca śabdane pratipādane tathā aviśeṣāt  pratyakṣa ādivat śabdena api yathāvastu bodhanīya tvāt  viśeṣaṇa mātra para tvam tu na abhyupagatam eva yena viśiṣṭa aikya asiddhiḥ syāt  yasya tu viśeṣya mātra para tvam tasya paryāya tulya tvāt  pada antara vaiyarthya lakṣaṇa bhaṅga lakṣaṇa ādi doṣaḥ pravṛtti nimittānām viśeṣaṇānām tyāgāt  viśeṣya mātrasya ca dvāra rahitasya alakṣya tvāt  itara vyāvṛttīnām tu upalakṣaṇa tve svarūpa tve ca pada antara vaiyarthya ādi doṣaḥ sa eva evam tāsām viśeṣaṇa tve pakṣa antaravat viśiṣṭa bheda ādi doṣaḥ tvad ukta āpatet  na ced na anyatra api tyakta pravṛtti nimittasya tad virodhi vyāvṛtti abhilāṣaḥ tu ālokam apahāya timira nirākaraṇa vāñchā vipratipannam vākyam akhaṇḍa param samāna adhikaraṇa vākya tvāt soyam devadattaḥ iti vākyavat  yad vā lakṣaṇa vākya tvāt  prakṛṣṭa prakāśaḥ candraḥ ityādivat  iti ced na dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ tad tedantā viśiṣṭasya eva devadattasya soyam iti pratīteḥ yugapad  tayoḥ vyāghāta iti ced na yaugapadyasya anabhidhānāt anākṣepāt ca yugapad  pratipattiḥ tu na doṣaḥ anyathā pratyabhijñā bhaṅge kṣaṇa bhaṅga nairātmya apalāpa ādi vādā vijayeran tathā api atītatva vartamāna tve katham ekasya iti ced  sva pradhvaṃsa kāle hi svayam atītaḥ syāt  na ca asau pradhvastaḥ vartamānatva upalaṃbhāt atīta upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhi tayā
