prāmāṇyam grāhyam na ca etad  tuṣa taṇḍula vibhāgavat alpa jñaiḥ śakyam atas  hi śārīrake trayāṇām nirāsaḥ pañca rātram tu kṛtsnam śrutivat  smṛtivat vā pramāṇam pratyakṣa śruti ādi virodha abhāvāt mahābhārate ca āptatama mānava dharma śāstrasya api tad mūlatva ukteḥ ati ādareṇa vyāsa diparigraha viśeṣāt īśvara dayā mūla tvena ca kāraṇa doṣa prasaṅga abhāvāt vedānteṣu yathāsāram saṃgṛhya bhagavān hariḥ bhakta anukampayā vidvān saṃcikṣepa yathāsukham iti ca tatra eva vyakteḥ veda prāmāṇya aṅgīkāratad artha ukti bhūyaḥ tvatad vaiśadya hetutva vacana sādhu paritrāṇa arthatva sattva uttara nārada ādi śrotṛkatva ādi nibandhana spaṣṭa pr na ca vipralambha artham tathā nibandhaḥ anyatra api prasaṅgāt  adhītā bhagavan vedāḥ iti ādeḥ durgrahatva mātra tātparyeṇa veda nindā ādi rūpatva abhāvāt nindā rūpatva īpi udita homa nindā vannindita itara praśaṃsana pravṛtteḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ  nāma jīvaḥ  jāyata iti ādeḥ tu avatāra ādi gocara tvasya tatra eva siddheḥ śarīrake ca utpatti asaṃbhavāt  na ca kartuḥ karaṇam iti sūtra dvayena pūrva pakṣam kṛtvā vijñāna ādi bhāve vā tad apratiṣedhaḥ vipratiṣedhāt ca iti tad prāmāṇya pratiṣedhaḥ parihṛtaḥ tathā nirmūlatva asat parigraha sat parigraha abhāva vaudika saṃskāra varjana avaidika saṃskāra vidhāna vidyā sthāna parigaṇana abhāva kṣudra vidyā bāhulya ādi mand bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ parihāraḥ prapañcitaḥ iti na iha pratanyate evam sākṣāt īśvara dayā mūla tvāt manu ādi nibandhanebhyosyā atirekaḥ teṣām śruti virodhe sati bādhya tvam api saṃbhavet  guṇatraya vaśya tayā kādācid ka bhrama ādi saṃbhavāt  smṛti ādīnām hi śruti mūla tayā eva prāmāṇyam iti bhāṣyepi uktam tad upari api iti adhikaraṇe saṅkīrṇa brāhmaṇa mantra artha vāda mūleṣu dharmaṃśāḥ tra itihāsa purāṇeṣu iti tatas  eva ca eṣām viprakīrṇa śākhā mūla tvam siddhāntaḥ iti api sūcitam kvacid  kadācid  keṣāñcid śākhā viśeṣāṇām ucchedaḥ te ca punar vyāsa ādibhiḥ kvacid  kadācid  pravartyante iti etāvatā ucchinna śākhā mūla tvam astu uktam ca bhagavatā āpastambena teṣām utsannāḥ pāṭhāḥ prayogāt anumīyante iti manu ādi vacana prāmāṇyam nyāyam antareṇa api śrutyā eva siddham yad vai kiñca manuḥ avadat  tad bheṣajam ityādibhiḥ evam śiṣṭa ācārasya api yathā te tatra varteran tathā tratra vartarthoḥ yāni asmākam su caritāni tāni tvayā upāsyāni ityādibhiḥ smṛtiḥ ca smṛti śīle ca tad vidām ācāraḥ ca eva sādhūnām ityādi śrutyā eva dharma nirṇaye saṃbhavati kim dharma śāstreṇa iti āśaṅkya āha marīciḥ durbodhā vaudikāḥ śabdāḥ prakīrṇa tvāt ca ye khilāḥ tad jñaiḥ ta eva spaṣṭa arthāḥ smṛtitantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ iti sati api dharma śāstre gṛhya apekṣām darśayati devalaḥ manu ādayaḥ prayoktāraḥ  dharma śāstrasya kīrtitāḥ tad prayukta prayoktāraḥ  gṛhya kārāḥ sva mantrataḥ iti atas  dharma śāstra gṛhya ādi sāpekṣa tvam veda artha nirṇayasya virodhe ca yathāyogam bala abala vyavasthā siddhā bhagavat dharma śāstrasya tu pañca rātrasya śruti ādi virodhe ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa ādeḥ iva deśa kāla adhikārī avasthā viśeṣa viṣaya tayā vikalpa eva śruteḥ iva asya api doṣa saṃbhāvanā viraha ādi siddheḥ āhuḥ ca evam abhiyuktāḥ vede kartṛ ādi abhāvāt iti ārabhya tasmāt  sāṃkhyam sa yogam sa paśupati matam kutracid  pañca rātram sarvatra eva pramāṇam tad idam avagatam pañcamāt eva vedāt  iti anyatra ca upaniṣadi tu bahvyām vyāvaghoṣya ām adoṣa pratihata guṇa rāśiḥ ghuṣyate tārkṣyaketuḥ śrutiḥ api tad upajñaiḥ pañca rātraiḥ vikalpam na labhata iti sūktam bhāṣya kṛt yā munā āryaiḥ iti tad etad yāmunā ācāryaiḥ āgama prāmāṇye saṃbhāvita samasta pūrva pakṣa yukti nirākaraṇena prapañcitam tad anusāreṇa eva bhāṣya kāraiḥ śrī pāñcarātra adhikaraṇam vyākhyātam śruti mūlam idam tantram pramāṇam kalpa sūtravat  ityādi vacanam tu trayī anta mūla tayā ekāyana śruti mūla tayā ca yojyam na ca atra veda tve sandegdhavyam yam vākeṣu anuvākeṣu niṣad su upaniṣatsu ca mahataḥ  vedavṛkṣasya mūla bhūtaḥ  mahān ayam skandha bhūtā ṛc ādi āḥ te śākhābhūtāḥ tathā mune ityādi vacanāt  tathā ṛgveda pāṭhe paṭhitam vratam etad  su duścaram iti saṃvāda pradarśanāt  veda śākhā vyāsa daśāyām nirukta śākhāyā api gaṇita tvāt  bhagavat śāstra sāra bhūta sāttvata pauṣkara ādiṣu rahasi āmnāya vidhāne ekāyanīya śākhā uktaiḥ mantraiḥ parama pāvanaiḥ ityādibhiḥ tad śrutitpratipādanāt  atra bhagavat yāmuna munibhiḥ eva uktaḥ  granthaḥ  likhyate yad api uktam agarbhādhāna ādi dāha anta saṃskāra antara sevanāt bhāgavatānām brāhmaṇyam iti tatra api ajñānam eva aparādhyati na punar āyuṣmataḥ  doṣaḥ yata ete vaṃśa paramparayā vājasaneya śākhām adhīyānāḥ kātyāyana ādi gṛhya ukta mārgeṇa garbhādhāna ādi saṃskārān kurvate ye punar  sāvitrī anuvacana prabhṛti trayī dharmā tyāgena ekāyana śruti vihitān eva catvāriṃśat saṃskārān kurvate tepi sva śākhā gṛhya ukta dharmam yathāvat anutiṣṭhamānā na śākhā antarīya karma ananuṣṭhānāt brāhmaṇyāt  pracyavante anyeṣām api paraspara śākhā vihita karma ananuṣṭhāna nimitta abra āhmaṇya prasaṅgāt  sarvatra hi jāti caraṇa gotra adhikāra ādi vyavasthitā eva samaya ācārā upalabhyante yadi api sarva śākhā pratyayam ekam karma tathā api na paraspara vilakṣaṇa adhikāri sambaddhā dharmāḥ kvacid  samuccīyante vilakṣaṇāḥ trayī vihita svarga putra ādi viṣaya upabhoga sādhana aindra āgneya ādi karma adhikāribhyaḥ  dvijebhyaḥ trayī anta ekāyana śruti vihita vijñāna abhigamana upādāna ijyā prabhṛti bhagavat prāpti eka upāya karma adhikāriṇaḥ  mumukṣavaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ iti na ubhayeṣām api anyonya śākhā vihita karma ananuṣṭhānam abrāhmaṇyam āpādayati yathā ca ekāyana śākhāyāḥ  apauruṣeya tvam tathā kāśmīrāgama prāmaṇyam eva prapañcitam iti na iha prastūyate prakṛtānām tu bhāgavatānām sāvitrī anuvacana ādi trayī sambandhasya sphuṭataram u palabdhiḥ na tad tyāga nimitta vrātyatva ādi sandeham sahate iti caturvidham ca idam pañca rātram āgama siddhāntaḥ divya siddhāntaḥ tantra siddhāntaḥ tatra antara siddhāntaḥ ca iti caturvidham ca idam veda mūla bhūta aṃśasya upabṛṃhaṇam tad abhiprāyeṇa hi uktam mahābhārate mahataḥ  vedavṛkṣasya mūla bhūtaḥ  mahān ayam ityādi caturṇām ca eṣām lakṣaṇa ādikam śrī pauṣkara ādiṣu bhagavatā eva darśitam yad ca teṣu caturṣu sādhāraṇya asādha araṇya arca upasaṃhārya anupasaṃhārya ādikam vaktavyam tad  sarvam śrī pāñcarātra rakṣā siddhānta vyavasthāyām sarva parāmarśena sādhitam asmābhiḥ iti tatra eva tad vistaraḥ sāttvata dharma goptuḥ ananyaiḥ anusandheya iti na atra prabrūmaḥ evam sthite kecid  bāhlīka prāyāḥ āgama bāhyāḥ śrīmat vaikhānasa prāmāṇye viśerate tatra tāvat  kalpasūtram na apramāṇam itaravat eva kalpasūtra tvāt  tad kartuḥ ca kalpasūtra kāratva prasiddheḥ veda aviruddha tvāt  vaidika mantraiḥ eva sakala dharma vidhānāt sūtra antarāṇām api kuṇḍa sanniveśa lakṣaṇa ādiṣu kvacid  kvacid  tad upajīvanāt varṇa āśrama dharmāṇām anukūlam nārāyaṇa paratva pratipādana ādeḥ api sattva mūla tvena prāmāṇya eka hetu tvāt  harim eva smaret nityam karma pūrva apareṣu api dhyāyet nārāyaṇam devam snāna ādiṣu ca karmasu ityādinā śaunaka ādibhiḥ api tathā eva vidhānāt  vaṃśa paramparayā ca vaikhānasaiḥ adhīyamāna tayā viplavasyā api anavakāśa tvāt astu kim api tad  idam tad iti kim niyākamam iti ced  itara anupalamaḥ tad upalambhaḥ ca anyathā sarvatra śruti smṛti ādīnām tathā tathā saṃśaya prasaṅgāt  astu idam eva tad  pramāṇam ca tathā api bhārgava ādi catuṣkasya katham prāmāṇyam iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt  mahā ṛṣi praṇītatva veda aviruddhatva ādeḥ sama tvāt  pañcarātra virodha usti iti ced na tattve tad abhāvāt kartavya kriyā ādi bhedasya api pratiniyata adhikāri viṣaya tvena eva upapatteḥ kalpasūtra prakriyā bhedavat  āgama divya tantra tantra antara rūpa pañcarātra avāntara catuṣka kriyā ādi vibhāgavat ca āśvamodhike śrī vaiṣṇava dharma śāstre dvitayam api sama prāmāṇyatayā upāttam dvayoḥ api paraspara prāmāṇyam viṣṇoḥ tantram dvidhā proktam ityādiṣu vyañjitam paraspara ākṣepa vacanāni tu ikṣu bhakṣa kṛti cikīrṣubhiḥ asa hiṣṇubhiḥ upakṣiptāni vā sva śāstra praśaṃsā artha vāda rūpāṇi vā iti na tatas  virodhaḥ nanu bhārgava ādīni na tāvat  kalpasūtrāṇi tathā anabhyupagamāt  aprasiddheḥ ayukteḥ ca na smṛti antarāṇi manu ādiṣu apāṭhāt  tadvat  tad prasiddhi abhāvāt ca ana ca svatantra tantra antarāṇi sāṃkhya yoga ādi saha pāṭhā darśanāt vaikhānasa anuvartanāt ca tad  katamām vidhāma valambyāmīṣām prāmāṇyam ucyate manu atri bhārgava ādivat  nāradīya ādivat ca dharma śāstra tayā eva teṣām api prāmāṇyam aṣṭādaśa ādi parigaṇanasya upalakṣaṇa tāyāḥ prāmāṇikaiḥ abhyupagamāt  smṛti antareṣu deva utsava ādi prapañcanam na asti iti ced  mā bhūt  prapañcanam svarūpam tāvat anujñātam tad prapañca parāṇām tathā api jīvānām anta tonyonya vaiṣamya mātrasya ca sārvatrika tvāt nikṛṣṭa ādhikārikāṇi tāni iti ced na teṣu anyeṣu ca brāhmaṇya eka pradhānatva vacatāt tathā upalabdheḥ ca katham teṣām brāhmaṇyam iti ced  śāntam pāpam śravasī pidadhīmahi tathā api vaktavyam dṛśyante hi ete vaṃśa paramparayā vedam adhīyānā vekhānasa sūtra ukta vaidika sakala saṃskāra śālinaḥ  varṇa āśrama dharma karmaṭhā bhagavat ekāntā brāhmaṇāḥ nūnam amīṣām brāhmaṇya eka kāraṇena bhāgavata tvena eva viparītam bambhrami iti brāhmaṇa gardabhaḥ anyathā vaikhānasa kalpasya api niradhikāri tvena aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ astu tad prāmāṇyam santu ca deśa antare kāla antare vā tad adhikāriṇaḥ amī tu katame iti ced  deśa antara ādau  api evam vaktum śakya tvāt  viparītam vā kasmāt na syāt  evam ca sati sūtra antara ādiṣu api kaḥ samāśvāsaḥ vaikhānasānām nikṛṣṭa jātitva vacana vivādābhyām sandeha viṣaya tvam iticed  āpta grantha stha tā dṛśa vacana abhāvāt  bhāvepyeteṣām nikṛṣṭa jāti tve pramāṇa abhāvāt  āgama prāmāṇya ukta sātvata ādi samākhyā nirvāha sama tvāt na hi aneka arthaḥ śabdaḥ  na asti na ca śabda aikyāt artha aikyam śabda bhedena artha bhedaḥ  vā anyathā vilīnam tṛtīya āśrameṇa api vivādasya tubhavādṛśa jihvā spanda mātra adhīnasya sūtra gotra ādau  api suśaka tvāt  itas  pūrvam tāvat na asti iti ced na asya api vivādasya anādi tvā yogāt tatas  pūrvam abhāvāta tathā ca bhavataḥ  bhaviṣyataḥ  vā vivādasya vivādatva aviśeṣāt  tatas  param teṣām anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt  asmākam tāvat  teṣu saṃśayaḥ  na asti iti ced  asmākam vā kim asti amīṣu kva tarhi nikṛṣṭa jāti antaram kim asmāsu tad nyāsīkṛtam yena asmābhiḥ pradarśanīyam na ca asmābhiḥ anantā deśā draṣṭum śākyāḥ sambhavati ca ucchedaḥ idānīm kṣatriya vaiśya māhiṣya ādivat  teṣām keṣāṃ cit nāma sāmya mātrāt atra anupraveśaḥ saṃbhavati iti ced na kasyā api śaṅkāyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt  asti ca varṇitu abhikṣutva ādīnām sāmyam anyatra api yaḥ ca evam atiśaṅkayā dūyate sa tu sva mātā pitṛ carita an avadhāraṇena sva brāhmaṇyam api yathārham atiśaṅketa iti jitam lokāyatena uktam ca bhagavatā ajñaḥ ca aśraddhadhānaḥ ca saṃśaya ātmā vinaśyati na ayam lokosti na paraḥ  na sukha saṃśaya ātmanaḥ iti tad  siddham viśiṣṭa ādhikārikam veda aviruddham vaikhānasa ādi smaraṇam pramāṇam iti yad ca dharma śāstra ādiṣu aṣṭādaśa ādi parisaṃkhyānam na tad adhika saṃkhyā vyavaccheda param anyeṣām api śiṣṭa parigraha ādeḥ aviśiṣṭa tvāt  anukta aṃśa darśana ādinā upajīvya tvāt ca iti evam sa parikaraḥ  vedaḥ pramāṇam iti siddham chandaḥ pādau śabda śāstram na vaktram kalpaḥ pāṇī jyautiṣam cakṣuṣī ca śikṣā ghrāṇam śrotram uktam niruktam vedasya aṅgāni āhuḥ etāni ṣaḍ  ca evam sa parikara veda artha tattva nirṇaya viṣayā atha atas  dharma jijñāsā iti ārabhya anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt anāvṛttiḥ śabdāt  iti evam antā viṃśati lakṣaṇī mīmāṃsā tatra ca saṃhitam etad śarīrakam jaiminīyena ṣoḍaśa lakṣaṇena iti śāstra ekatva siddhiḥ iti bhāṣya upāttaḥ vṛtti granthaḥ tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam karma devatā brahma gocarā sā tridhā udbhabhau sūtrakārataḥ jaimineḥ muneḥ kāśa kṛtsnataḥ  bādārayaṇāt ityataḥ kramāt  iti anayoḥ devatā kāṇḍasya jaiminīya tvakāśa kṛt snīyatva uktī tādadhīni ādi vivakṣaya samāna arthe gamayitavye tatra karma kāṇḍa artham evam saṃjagṛhuḥ dharma dhīḥ mānabheda aṅga prayukti krama kartṛbhiḥ sa ati deśa viśeṣaḥ ha bādha tantra prasaktibhiḥ iti veda arthe nyāya cintye prathamam avasitam karma tad devatā ca thātas  śārīraka aṃśe niravadhika phala brahma cintā tu asūtri tatra adhyāye parasmin svayam upaniṣadām anvayosya avirodhaḥ  mokṣa upāyotha muktiḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇau siddha sādhyau dvikā arthau tatra adya iti anta gūḍha āviśada viśada ta  chāyajīva ādi vācaḥ paścāt smṛti ādikaiḥ akṣati rahita hatiḥ kārya tā abhra indriya ādeḥ doṣa adoṣau tṛtīyepya vara para gatau bhaktiḥ aṅgāni ca athaḥ pāsa anuṣṭhā prabhāva utkrama saraṇi phalāni antime cintitāni vicārāt  pūrvam eva atra prāptam adhyayanam vidheḥ atas nadhīta vedasya vicāraḥ śāstra bādhitaḥ kramaḥ  viṃśati lakṣaṇyā na vaidhaḥ kintu yauktikaḥ atas  vyutkrama cintāyām anaucityam praśiṣyate evam viṃśati lakṣaṇī śravaṇa m ananābhyām su pratiṣṭhita samasta śāstra arthasya mokṣa sādhana tayā vidheyam nididhi āsanam na vākya artha jñāna mātram tasya rāga prāpta śravaṇa ādi siddha tvāt ata eva ca tasmin viśeṣe vedanā ādi sāmānya śabda paryavasānam na ca nididhi āsana ādikam niṣiddham varaṇīya tvam eva vihitam iti vācyam svatantra anya kartṛka varaṇa karmībhāvasya āpuruṣa tantretu enā vidheya tvāt  atas tad hetunā prīti rūpa tvena upāsanam eva viśiṣyate tathā sati bhaktyā tu ananyayā iti smṛti avirodhaḥ ca tad eva ca nididhi āsanam prīti rūpam prakaraṇa viśeṣāt  samādhiḥ ca ca aṣṭa aṅgaḥ śāstreṣu śiṣyate tāvati ca pātañjala prāmāṇyam api āgama śīlanam ca āphalāt mātrayā anuvartanīyam smaranti ca svādhyāyāt yogam āsīta yogāt  svādhyāyam āviśet  svādhyāya yoga saṃpattyā paramātmā prakāśate iti yad  punar  śrūyate grantham abhyasya medhāvī jñāna vijñāna tatparaḥ palālam ima dhānya arthī tyajet  grantham aśeṣatas  iti tad  kośa tyāga abhiprāyam na ca sa ādara paṭu saṃskāra pracaya saṃsiddha medhā saṃpadaḥ puruṣasya kośena kiñcid  sāddhyam medhāvi iti ca viśeṣvate dhīḥ dhāraṇāvatī medhā iti ca naighaṇṭukāḥ adhīmahe ca medhā manīṣe mā viśatām samīcīna bhūtasya bhavyasya avaruddhyai iti yaddhā mukta prāya atyanta niṣpanna yoga puruṣa viṣayam etad  na hi tasya śāstreṇa jñātavyam tadānīm asti sākṣātkṛta samasta tattva artha tvāt yad tu smaryate śāstra jñānam bahu kleśam buddheḥ calana kāraṇam upadeśāt hariṃ buddhvā viramet  sarva karmasu iti idam tu tīvra saṃvegināmalasāstikānām ca grāhmam buddhi calana hetūnām asat śāstrāṇām tyāga artham vā tadā viśeṣaṇa sāphalyam dharma vidyā sthāneṣu api hi bahis daleṣu ati saṃrambhaḥ  mumukṣoḥ apa udyate na śabda śāstra abhiratasya mokṣaḥ  na ca eva ramya āvasatha priyasya na bhojana ācchādana tatparasya na loka citta grahaṇe ratasya iti tad  śābdam prameya tattvam adhijigamiṣatām pramāṇeṣu sāram tad abhāve puṃsaḥ paśubhiḥ samatva prasaṅgāt  iti yasya ājñā nigama eka harmya valabhī vāstavya pārāvatī yad bhrū lāsi avaśaṃvadā vidhi śiva sva sthāna susthāsikā yaḥ sarvatra yathāpuram vitanute nāmāni viśva ākṛti rnityam naḥ pratibhātu sarva vacasām niṣṭhā sa nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedāntān acāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau śabda adhyāye dvitīyam āhnikam atha smṛtiḥ nirūpyate saṃskāra mātra jam jñānam smṛtiḥ iti tad lakṣaṇam nanu smṛtiḥ na pramāṇam avidyamāna viṣaya tvāt  ananubhūti tvāt  bhrama sambhava ucca iti ced na smṛti mātrā prāmāṇyasya prathama ahnikre pratikṣipta tvāt  avādhita bāhya artha darśanāt  atīta anāgata viṣaya anumāna ādi bādha prasaṅgāt  sarva loka virodhāt ananubhūte artha antarepi smṛti prasaṅgāt  smṛteḥ api sva prakāśa tvepi vedya ākāre saṃskāra ādi sāpekṣa tvāt na ca pūrva anubhava puraskāreṇa eva grahaṇāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na smṛti pramoṣe tad abhāvāt pramāṇa tayā saṃmatāyām pratyabhijñāyām bhāvāt ca paratantra tvāt apramāṇyam iti ced na sva hetu pāratantrya mātrasya sārvatrika tvāt  anubhava mūla tvasya pramāṇa mūla tvasya ca sa vikalpaka ādibhiḥ anaikāntika tvāt  saṃskāra mātra janya tvasya asādhāraṇa tvāt sva viṣaya prakāśa vyavahārayoḥ tu smṛteḥ api svatantra tvāt icchā ādivat viṣaya niyamepi pāratantryam asti iti ced na tadvat eva ajñānatva prasaṅgāt  jñānam eva hi svatas  viṣaya pravaṇam icchasi ata eva hi nityayoḥ api riśvara cikīrṣā prayatnayoḥ viṣaya niyamāya jñāna apekṣām brūṣe icchā ādīnām api svatas  viṣaya prāvaṇyam jñāna tvam ca asmābhiḥ svīkṛtam nanu saṃskāravat iti ced na tasya api sva hetu samāna viṣaya jñāna utpādana śakta svabhāva tvāt atas  hetu niyata viṣaya tvam eva phalitam tad ca anubhavepi samam tathā ca samāna viṣaya anubhava janyatva tad abhāvābhyām smṛti anubhavayoḥ pāratantrya svātantrya vyavahāraḥ  mandānām sva prāmāṇya nirṇaya ādau  api na anubhava apekṣatva nirbandhaḥ sva viṣaya prakāśana bādha viraha ādibhi satad siddheḥ gṛhīta mātra grāhi tvasya asādhāraṇa tvāt prābhākarāṇām anumāna ādau naiyāyika ādīnām dhārāvāhika ādau yoga siddha sarvajña vādinām dvitīya yoga pratyakṣa ādau keṣāñcid īśvara vādinām anitya īśvara jñāne ca vyabhicārāt ca niṣprayojana tvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na tṛṇa ādi viṣaya pratna yakṣa ādinānaikāntyāt  asiddheḥ ca smṛtyā eva hi jagatām kṛta akṛta pratyavekṣaṇa ādi siddhiḥ smṛtyā eva hi śabda anumānayoḥ pravṛtiḥ para bhakti ādi niṣpattiḥ ca pūrva anubhuvasya eva tāni prayojana āni iticet sarva jagat ādi kāraṇasya brahma saṃkalpasya eva kim na syuḥ evam ca anubhavasya api na tad siddhiḥ tad kāraṇasya iti vaktum śakya tvāt  yad uktam prajñā paritrāṇe jñāta ātma jñāna rūpa tvāt sva prameya prahāṇataḥ viṣaya avyabhicāri tvepya prāmāṇyam smṛteḥ matam ityādi tad api anena parihṛtam pramāṇa vyavahāra abhāvāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced na pāmara vyavadvāra abhāvasya anaikāntika tvāt  evam parīkṣaka vyavahāra bhāvasya api vigīta tvāt ca sarva parīkṣaka vyavahāra abhāvasya ca asiddheḥ māna manohara ādau vāc īśvara ādibhiḥ ta prāmāṇi asya ukta tvāt katipaya parīkṣa kavyahāra abhāvasya ca ati prasañjaka tvāt akṣapāda ādi vyahāra avi avahārayoḥ bṛhaspati ādi vyavahāravat asmābhiḥ na atīva ādaraṇāt indra pāṇini ādīnām tu sarva saṃpratipatteḥ abādhāt ca ādarāt  pārāśarya ādīnām pramāṇa parigaṇana anadhikṛta tvena tad anuktera prayojaka tvāt  āgamaḥ pramāṇam iti api vyavahāra abhāvāt  pratyakṣam ca anumānam ca śāstram ca vividha āgamam ityādiṣu ca pratyakṣa ādi mūla smṛteḥ pratyakṣa ādi samāna carca tvena pṛthak vyavahāra abhāva upapatteḥ pramāṇa hetukā smṛtiḥ pramāṇam eva avisaṃvādāt  iti uktam ca nyāya tattve smṛti udāsīna bhedake caturthedhi karaṇe apramāṇa mūla tvam tu ubhayoḥ api na asti vyabhicāra abhāvena anadhigata artham pramāṇam iti viśeṣaṇasya ayukta tvāt  pramite pramiti anupapattiḥ kva dṛṣṭā smṛtau ced  pratijñā eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ syāt  jñāna antare ced na nujānāmi ityādi tattva ratna ākare ca yathārtha niścayaḥ  mānam tad hetuḥ ca iti sūrayaḥ na ati vyāptiḥ smṛtau vyāptiḥ yathā arthena hi sā pramā iti uktvā asya uttara ardha vivaraṇepi uktam anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ yathāsa ghaṭa ati nanu tām api vyāpnoti lakṣaṇamya satyam tad vyāptau na ati vyāptiḥ tasya api lakṣya pakṣe nikṣepāt  lakṣya alakṣye anālakṣya kṣipyate lakṣaṇam katham loka dhī vī avahāram hi lakṣya alakṣya avadhi viduḥ ityādi yad tu anubhavaḥ pramāṇam smṛti vyatiriktam jñānam anubhavaḥ ityādinā smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam iva śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ tad nūnam para ma tā anvāroheṇa ata eva hi taiḥ svatas  prāmāṇya nirṇaya daśāyām anyathā vyavahṛtam tathā hi tasmāt  siddham etad  pramāṇānām yathārthatva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam guṇa jñāna anapekṣāt sva pramāṇāt eva avasīyate svakīyāt  kāraṇāt eva jñāyata iti ca iti tathā artha tathā tvam guṇa saṃvāda jñāna anapekṣa jñapti tad abhāvepi jñāyamāna tvāt  iti ādau na ca hetoḥ asiddha tvam tathā hi rajata jñānasya artha tathā tvam nāma rajata viṣaya tvam tad ca asati bādhake rajata grāhiṇā eva jñānena avagamyate ityādi atas  yathā avasthita vastu niścaya ātmaka tvam eva prāmāṇyam pramāṇa jñānānām ātmīyāt  kāraṇāt jñāyate na guṇa saṃvāda jñānam apekṣate iti tathā pramāṇānām yathā avasthita vastu niścaya ātmaka tvam eva prāmāṇyam tad ābhāsa yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣiṇa ucyante siddhāntepi viveka pradarśanam eva iti yadi ca anubhava eva pramāṇam tad na yuktam upayuktam vā na ca sarvam anubhavam pramāṇa tayā vyavaharanti pīta śaṅkha bhrama ādiṣu adarśanāt  na api sarvām smṛtim apramāṇa tayā pramāṇa mūla smṛtiṣu tad abhāvāt agṛhīta grahaṇa śaktam pramāṇam iti vara da viṣṇu miśra uktiḥ api para ma tā anvāroheṇa netavyā yad tu āgama prāmāṇye proktam pramāṇa antara dṛṣṭa artha viṣaya vyāpiśemuṣī pramāṇam eva tad pūrvam na ced  sva artham vigāhate iti idam api anuvāda vākyasya anya para tayā sva artha prāmāṇya vyavaccheda artham anyathā smṛti pramoṣe pramuṣita tad aṃśe pūrva anubhava puraskāreṇa sva artha avagāhana asiddheḥ katham tatra smṛtitva nibandha nam aprāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati yad tu bhāṣye sat mātra grāhi pratyakṣa nirākaraṇa daśāyām uktam aśve hastini ca saṃvedanayoḥ eka viṣaya tvena uparitanasya gṛhīta grāhi tvād viśeṣa abhāvāt ca smṛti vailakṣaṇyam na syāt  iti na tatra smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyam sūcitam prakāra antareṇa api vailakṣaṇya siddheḥ tad apekṣayā ca prasaṅga upapatteḥ yad ca aparam bhāṣyam indriya janmanaḥ pratyakṣasya hi eṣa svabhāva niyamaḥ yad  sva sama kāla vartinaḥ padārthasya grāhaka tvam na tu sarveṣām jñānānām pramāṇānām ca smaraṇa anumāna āgama yogi pratyakṣa ādiṣu kāla antara vartinā upi grahaṇa darśanāt  ityādi tatra api parasya aniṣṭa prasaṅgāya tad abhiprāya anudhāvanena vibhajya udāharaṇam yuktam yad ca śāstra yoni adhikaraṇe bhāṣitam bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta janmanaḥ tasya viśada avabhāsa tvepi pūrva anubhūta viṣaya smṛti mātra tvāt na prāmāṇyam iti kutas  pratyakṣatā iti idam api na sākṣāt  siddhānta stham na ca yāthārthyam tatra pratikṣiptam evam anyat api bhāvyam smṛtyaprāmāṇya vādinā upi vaiśeṣikāḥ tām yathā arthyāt vidyā koṭau paṭhanti tatas  eva ca tad eka deśibhiḥ api tad prāmāṇyam svīkṛtam iti iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedānta ācāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau smṛti adhyāye prathamam āhnikam evam tāvat vivecitam pramāṇam cārvākāḥ tu pratyakṣam ekam pramāṇam iti āhuḥ teṣu eva kecid  anumānasya pratyakṣentarbhāvam icchanti kecid tu aprāmāṇyam pratyakṣam anumānam ca kāṇādāḥ saugatāḥ ca tatra pūrve śabdasya anumāna intarbhāvam āhuḥ pare tu kecid  antarbhāvam kecid aprāmāṇyam te ca āgamam ca sāṃkhyāḥ bhūṣaṇa mata anuvartinaḥ ca tatra vedasya anādi tvam pūrve parijagṛhuḥ uttare tu īśvara sṛṣṭa tām tāni ca smṛtim ca vaiśeṣika eka deśina usmad siddhānta eka deśinaḥ ca tāni eva sārtha āpattikāni prābhākarāḥ anupalabdhi ṣaṣṭhāni tāni eva tauta atitāḥ tad pralobhana rucayaḥ  māyā vādinaḥ ca tāni eva saṃbhavati hya yuktāni purāṇa śaraṇāḥ adyatana pramāṇa parigraha upalambha prakriyā iyam anante pūrva apara kāle kaḥ kim aṅgīkuryāt  kim vā bahiṣkuryāt  iti kaḥ  jānāti anyatra kalpa sākṣāt kāriṇaḥ tasmāt ekasmāt devāt  iha ca nyūna vādinaḥ tad avasare nirastāḥ adhika tayā para abhimatānām tu arnta bhāvaḥ  vaktavyaḥ tatra yathā pratyabhijñā ādīnām pratyakṣa ādiṣu eva niveśa iṣyate evam anyeṣām api pratyabhijñā tāvat  grahaṇa ātmikā eva iti eke tathā hi pratyabhijñāyām api smṛtiḥ anubhava iti aṃśa bheda usti ced  iti āśaṅkya pratyuktam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ yadi viṣaya bhedaḥ tadā aṃśa bhedaḥ saṃbhavet  aikyam eva hi niraṃśam pratyabhijñā pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ katham saṃskāraḥaparokṣadhī janakaḥ iti ced  na cakṣuḥ ādi indriya sahakṛtasya saṃskārasya jñātuḥ aikyāt  tad idam iti aparokṣadhī hetutva upapatteḥ aparokṣa artha aikya sādhikā sā pratyabhijñā soyam vai pumān iti evam ātmikā saṃskāra mātra janya tvāt na smṛtiḥ mānam eva tad  iti dīpe ca aanusmṛteḥ ca iti sūtre bhāṣitam pratyabhijñānāt ca na paṭa ādeḥ kṣaṇika tvam tad eva idam iti pratyabhijñāyate pratyabhijñā hi nāma atīta vartamāna kāla varti eka vastu viṣayam ekam pratyakṣa jñānam tasya kāla dvaya sambandha aviśiṣṭam ekam eva vastu viṣayaḥ na ca tad iti aṃśaḥ smaraṇam idam aṃśaḥ ca grahaṇam atīta sambandhini indriya saṃprayoga abhāvāt iti vācyam tad idam iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena grahaṇasya ekatva sphuraṇāt  pūrva anubhava janita saṃskāra saciva indriya saṃprayoga yuktasya puruṣasya tathā grahaṇam upapadyata eva anvaya vyatireka adhīnam hi sarvatra sāmagrī parikalpanam iti anye tu atra dhī bheda bāddhya parihārau matvā tad idam aṃśayoḥ tad aṃśe saṃskāra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt parokṣa rūpa tayā idam aṃśe ca pati akṣa rūpa tayā ca ubhaya ātmaka tvam āhuḥ tad mate saṃskāra adhīna prakāśā smṛtiḥ iti lakṣaṇam aparokṣa jñānam pratyakṣam ubhaya lakṣaṇa yogāt  pratyabhijñāyām ubhaya ātmaka tvam iti abhyupagantavyam ca asmad siddhāntibhiḥ sarvaiḥ pratyakṣa itara jñānānām parokṣa aparokṣa rūpa tvam svayaṃprakāśa tvāt  sarva jñānānām vedya itara aṃśa apekṣayā ca pratyakṣa tvāt  uktam ca idam śrī viṣṇu cittaiḥ api sva prakāśakam viṣaya prakāśakam ca ekam eva jñānam tatra smṛtriḥ anubhūtiḥ iti kutaḥ bhedaḥ iti paricodya prakāśa māna bhedāt  iti brūmaḥ yathā gauḥ ayam iti ekasmin  eva jñāne prakāri prakāra viṣaya bhedena jñāna aṃśa bhedaḥ yathā gauḥ ayam iti ekasmin  eva jñāne prakāri prakāra viṣaya bhedena jñāna aṃśa bhedaḥ yathā ca ghaṭa paṭau  iti ekasmin  eva jñāneṃśa bhedaḥ yathā vā para abhyupagata bhrama jñāneṣu adhiṣṭhāna aṃśe prāmāṇyam itaratra aprāmāṇyam ca iti parihārāt  tathā smṛteḥ sva prakāśa aṃśa upi saṃskāra mātraja eva indriya ādi pratiniyata kāraṇa antara abhāvāt  iti paricodya na evam jñānānām prakāśamānatvasya svābhāvika tvāt iti parihārāt ca tasmāt  sarvatra viṣaya apekṣayā eva aparokṣatva anumititva smṛtitva ādi vibhāgaḥ jāti saṃkara asaṃkara ādi tu darśana adarśanābhyām vyavasthāpyam aupādhika saṃkara ādivat ca tad evam ubhaya ātmakatva upapatteḥ pratyabhijñā api ubhaya ātmikā iti pratyabhijñā api abhijñāvat tridhā cākṣa ādi bhedataḥ tad tad saṃskāra saṃbheda mūlatva anna vadhā bhavet  pratyakṣa toktiḥ dīpa ādau pradarśana pareṣya tām na hi liṅga ādibhiḥ soyam iti jñānam na jāyate śabda jam pratyabhijñānam upajīvya pravartate śākhā antara adhikaraṇa nyāyaḥ ca kratu vidyayoḥ dīpa ādiṣu iva sarvatra bādhaka ādeḥ asaṃbhavāt vigītam pratyabhijñānam pramāṇam sa vikalpavat  karaṇa akaraṇa ādīnām kāla bheda ādi upādhitaḥ avirodhāt na bīja ādau śakyate bheda kalpanam anyathā deśa bhedena karaṇa akaraṇa ādibhiḥ ekam jagati na eva syāt iti syāt  sarva śūnyatā tasmāt  viruddha saṃspṛṣṭa viṣaya pratyabhijñayā sthira tvam ātmanām siddham bāhyānām api vāstavam pratisandhānam api ātma gocaram pratyabhijñā viśeṣa eva yoham adrākṣam sa eva spṛśāmi iti evamādi rūpa tvāt  pratisandhiḥ artha dvaya viṣaya eka buddhiḥ iti eke tatra api pṛthak anubhūta aneka artha gocara eka kartṛka eka buddhiḥ iti pūraṇīyam iti saṃvādaḥ  nāma jñāna jāti antaram iti kecid  tad ayuktam saṃkhyā antara asaṃbhavāt yad tu vara da viṣṇu miśraiḥ uktam gṛhīta artha viṣayam śabda kāraṇakam jñānam saṃvādaḥ iti tad api śābda avāntara bhede saṃjñā viśeṣa niveśa mātra param na hi gṛhīta artha viṣaya tve śabda śakti prasūta tvam apaiti gṛhīta mātra gocara pramāṇa antarepi tad anyatva prasaṅgāt  bhavati hi parva toyam agnimān iti śabda śravaṇa anantaram dhūmam parāmṛśatā upi tādṛśī buddhiḥ tathā dvitīya yogi pratyakṣa ādau  api draṣṭavyam anapekṣitatva ādikam api śruta viṣaya anumāna ādau samam na ca apekṣā yuktam prāmāṇyam bhedaḥ bhedaḥ  vā tṛṇa ādi pratyakṣasya api tathā prasaṅgāt  iti uktam kimartham tarhi vedānām vedāntānām ca aprāpta viṣaya tvam samarthyate iti ced  atathā prāptau sākṣāt aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  tathā prāptau  api anapekṣita tayā prekṣāvadbhiḥ nirarthaka prayāsa bhīrubhiḥ tyājyatva āpātena phalatā uprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  iti paśya upamānam api yadi gṛhyamāṇa padārtha gata sādṛśya vijñānāt smaryamāṇa padārtha gata sādṛśya vijñānam tadā smṛtiḥ tad tad vastu saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādi atiriktasya sādṛśyasya abhāvāt  tasya ca pūrva dṛṣṭa tvāt  smaryamāṇa tvāt ca vyavahāropyaḥ tu apūrvaḥ tad tad vyavahāravat pratisambandha viśeṣa parāmarśa upādhikaḥ yad vā yaḥ  yad sadṛśaḥ sa tad gata sādṛśya pratiyogī yathāmithas  sva hastau iti vyāpti siddhau gauḥ etad sadṛśaḥ etad gata sādṛśya pratiyogi tvāt iti anumānāt  smaryamāṇa gata sādṛśya asiddhiḥ anyathā gṛhyamāṇa gata vaisādṛśya jñānāt smaryamāṇa gata vaisādṛśya pratītiḥ api māna antaram syāt  sā ced  arthāpattiḥ sādṛśya dhīḥ api tathā kim na syāt  iti athavā yugapad eva tad sadṛśa uyam iti pratyayena eva ubhaya vṛtti sādṛśya sphuraṇāt na tad hetukam anyathā pṛthak anubhūtayoḥ tadānīma pratīta sādṛśyayoḥ parastāt yugapad  smaryamāṇayoḥ yugapad eva pratīyamāna sādṛyayoḥ kaḥ nirvāhaḥ tatra api vā pramāṇa antaram kalpyate yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ govat  dviśaphaḥ  na bhavati aśvaḥ dīrgha grīvaḥ pralamba uṣṭhaḥ  vikaṭa ākṛtiḥ paśuḥ kramelakaḥ iti tu sādharmya vaidharmya dharmya mātra viṣayam trividham api atideśa vākyam āgama eva yad tu śruta atideśa vākyasyagavaya ādau  ati deśa vākya artha pratyabhijñānam upamānam tad ca vyutpatti phalakam iti tad api anupapananam prāk eva vyutpatti siddheḥ yad tu sādṛśyasya nimittattvāt nimittasya apratītitaḥ samayaḥ  durgrahaḥ pūrvam śabdena anumayā api vā iti tatra nimittasya apratītitaḥ iti tu asiddham gavayatva ādeḥ eva jāti viśeṣasya gaḥ sādṛśya ākāra upalakṣitasya prathamam eva vākya artha tayā pratītiḥ gaḥ sādṛśya ākāra upalakṣitasya prathamam eva vākya artha tayā pratītiḥ gaḥ sādṛśya upalakṣitaḥ kaścid  vyakti viśeṣaḥ  gavaya iti hi pratītiḥ paścāt  pratyakṣita gavayasya tad vaiśadya mātram eva uktam ca śrī viṣṇu citteḥ gaḥ sadṛśaḥ  gavayaḥ iti gaḥ sādṛśya eka adhikaraṇam sāmānyam vācyam iti vyutpannam prathamam vākya artha tayā pratīteḥ gaḥ sādṛśya upalakṣitasya anirṇaye paścāt api anirṇayaḥ anyathā anirṇaye tathā paścāt api tatas  vākya śravaṇa velāyām eva nirṇitam iti evam ca anabhyupagame katham inrdā ādi śabda vyutpattiḥ na hi atra nimitta bhūta saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādi dṛṣṭiḥ na ca nityam tatra avyutpattiḥ tad artha viśiṣṭa vākya artha bodha āpātāt  evam nitya atīndriya viṣaya saṃskāra ādi śabdānām api nityam avyutpattiḥ eva syāt  tatra ced  kathañcid nirvāhaḥ tathā atra api tad  siddham na upamānam atiriktam iti arthāpattiḥ tu anumānam eva tathā hi anupapadyamāna darśanāt upapādaka kalpanam nāma vyāpyāt vyāpaka jñānam avyāpyasya tena vinā anupapadyamānatva abhāvāt  avyāpakasya ca tad upapādakatva ayogāt iti pramāṇa dvaya virodhe sati viṣaya vyavasthāpanam arthāpattiḥ iti api na vācyam pramāṇayoḥ satoḥ virodha abhāvāt viruddhayoḥ api prāmāṇya ayogāt nanu devadattasya jīvane kutaścid  pramāṇāt  pramite jīvatā kvacid  sthātavyam iti aviśeṣeṇa deśa sāmānya sambandha avagatau gṛham api āskandantyām satyām pratyakṣe ca gṛhe tad abhāvam pratipādayati spaṣṭaḥ  virodhaḥ atas tad śānyai bahis bhāva kalpanam arthāpattiḥ iti mā evam kvacid iti viditasya jīvanasya niyama abhāvāt  bahis vidyamāna tā saṃdehe niścaya rūpeṇa gṛha abhāva pratyakṣeṇa pratispardhitum asāmarthyāt  na ca viruddha viṣayayoḥ vāstavam kutra api sama bala tvam samasti ubhayā prāmāṇye tu kathañcid  syāt  ābhimānika bala sāmya īpi tathā eva yadā vaiṣamya grahaḥ tadā tatas  eva bala abala siddhau kim artha āpattyā sādhyam atas  kevala niravakāśa virodhi viśeṣa sannidhau sati sa avakāśam sāmānyam saṃkocayitavyam iti vyavasthā syāt  sā api ca tathā eva vyāpteḥ iti anumāna phalam eva anyathā virodhi viṣaya tyāga iva avirodhi viśeṣa paryavasā ana ādau  api māna antara kḷptiḥ kim na syāt  evam anabhyupagame ca dhūma anumāna ādau  api arthāpattitva prasaṅgaḥ agnim vinā anupapadyamānatva svaya liṅga pratyakṣa rūpa pramāṇa dvaya virodhasya ca vaktum śakya tvāt  dhūmaḥ  hi kāraṇa bhūtam vahnim ākṣipati pratikṣipati tu pratyakṣam iti virodhe parvata arvāgbhāge vahniḥ iti vyavasthā kalpanasya arthāpatti tvam syāt  vyāpti nirūpaṇam antareṇa gamakatā gamakasya eva dharma antara yogi tayā gamyate ityādi bhedāḥ tu āśā mātra kalpitāḥ iti uktam ca śrī viṣṇut tittaiḥ arthāpattiḥ anumānam ityādi kecid tu kevala vyatirekiṇi arthāpatti saṃjñām niveśayanti tasya prāk eva nirāsān na pramāṇa varga anupraveśaḥ anupraveśepi vā na pṛthaktvam yad tu āgama prāmāṇye anubhavaḥ ca indriya liṅga śabda sadṛśāni atha anupapadyamāna artha pūrvakaḥ ityādiṣu upamāna artha āpatti parigrahaḥ pratibhāti tad api pūrva pakṣa pradeśa gata tvāt na siddhānta tvāya kalpate abhāvaḥ tu asmad mate bhāva antarātmā sa cākṣa ādibhiḥ yathāsaṃbhavam sidhyati abhāva ātmanā tu grahaṇepi pratiyogi smaraṇa ādi sahakāri sahitāni tāni eva pramāṇani iti na tad atirikta kalpanā vakāśaḥ ata eva hi prāgarta ja abhāva ādi vijñānam api nirvyūḍham dṛṣṭa eva hi deśa kāla ādi saṃsarga ādi viśeṣaḥ paścāt  pratiyogi smaraṇa ādimataḥ puruṣasya tad abhāva ātmanā dhiyam adhirohati smartavyasya smaraṇa abhāvāt vā tatra tad abhāva anumānam evam atirikta abhāva pakṣepi nirmūlā pramāṇa antara kḷptiḥ sa ghaṭam bhū talam itivat  aghaṭam bhū talam iti api hi aparokṣā pratītiḥ na ca adhikaraṇa grahaṇa upakṣīṇam indriyam guṇa ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt  atirekavat anatiḥ ekepī ajñāta karaṇatva ādīni anumānāni ca sulabhāni iti saṃbhava upyanumānam eva sahasre śatam saṃbhavati iti ādeḥ pūrva anubhū sahasra gata vyāpti bodhana tvāt  saṃbhavati kṣatriye śairyam iti ādeḥ saṃdeha ātmaka tvena apramāṇa tvāt avirodha niścaya rūpa tvepi tad avirodha niścāyaka pramāṇa antare viśramaḥ aitihyam tu pramāṇa mūlam ced āgamaḥ tad ābhāsa mūlam ced  tad ābhāsaḥ evam ceṣṭā ālipi akṣara ādikam api abhiprāya varṇa viśeṣa ādi avinābhūtam anumānam eva ceṣṭāyām vara da nārāyaṇa bhaṭṭārakaiḥ evam uktam śabdasya vyavahārasya anukāraḥ ceṣṭayā api hi kriyate śābda vijñāna yoginām sva artha bodhikā anādi vyavahāreṣu ceṣṭā vijñāta śaktikāḥ bodhikāḥ syuḥ yathā adhyakṣam iti ced  bhavataḥ  matam ceṣṭā giraḥ vā svīkāryāḥ para pratyāyanāya hi anādayaḥ  girām eva anāditā jyāyasī tadā ceṣṭā sāmayikī śābda vyavahāra anusāriṇī asya evam bodhikā iti evam bharata ādi āgame sthitā dṛśyatena ādiḥ āmnāyosmaryamāṇa praṇetṛkaḥ ityādi tattva ratna ākare tu evam uktam vyutpanna bodhya bodhaka niyamam ced  ceṣṭitam śābdam aniyatam api saha dṛṣṭyā smārakam iti na pṛthak eṣṭavyam iti lipi akṣareṣu tu ayam gakāraḥ ayam ghakāraḥ iti varṇa ātmanā jñānam apramāṇam eva etena cihnena idam akṣaram jānīhi iti abhiprāyeṇa lipi akṣara saṃbandha grāhakāṇām pravṛttiḥ tatas ca vyāpti siddhiḥ eṣā lipiḥ etad varṇa viśeṣa abhiprāya pūrvikā bhrama ādi rahita varṇa abhiprāyavat puruṣa likhita etad li pi tvā at saṃpratipanna vyutpatti kāla lipivat ityādi rūpaḥ prayogaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ yad tu pratibhāyām uktam tattva ratna ākare nanu ca pratibhā kācid  yathārthā mānam iṣyatām bāhya arthanaiḥ apekṣyeṇa bāhya jñāna kṣamāḥ tu sā viśiṣṭa kāla puruṣa ādi apekṣā utkarṣa saṃbhavā satyam kāla ādi bhedaḥ tu durviveca usmad ādibhiḥ san  api asau vyavahṛtau na upayogī iti upekṣyate pratibhāyāḥ phalam dṛṣṭam yadā prāmāṇya niścayaḥ tad anyatas  kṛtārtha tvāt prekṣyate na parīkṣakaiḥ puṇyeṣu puruṣeṣu eṣā bhūyiṣṭham satya darśinī tasmāt  patañjaliḥ prāha pratibhā ca iti tām pramām iti tad api prāc ukta yogi pratyakṣa viśeṣa viṣayam eva nanu evam tad api pramāṇa tri tvam catuṣṭvam vā anupapannam pratyakṣa parokṣa rūpeṇa dvi tvasya eva yukta tvāt  iti ced na atiprasaṅgāt  tathā hi bahuṣu ekaikam uddhṛtya tad anyeṣu aika rāśyataḥ dvaidha kḷptau ghadādau  api evam eva prasajyate anumāna numānatva śabdā śabda vibhāgataḥ pramāṇa dvi tvam evam te vada kim vāna rocate pratyakṣasya tad anyābhyām vaijātya grahaṇāt yadi tayoḥ api svetarābhyām vaijātyam sphuṭam eva naḥ atokṣaliṅga śabda ākhyāsā dhāraṇa nidānataḥ upalakṣyam pramātri tvam catuṣṭvam vā api saṃsmṛteḥ spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam iti ca jainā yad  dvaidham ūcire tad pratyakṣa parokṣatva vibhāgāt na viśiṣyate atas  na tāvati dvaidhe sādhite vivadāmahe parokṣasya eka māna tvam durvacam bheda sādhanāt  nanu adhyakṣepi bheda usti bāhya antara vibhāgataḥ divya adivyatayā cakṣuḥ śrotra ādi bhidayā api ca tadvat  parokṣasya ekasya pramāṇasya vibhāgataḥ anumāna āgama bhidā katham na abhyupagamyate datta uttaram idam kiñcid  dṛṣṭam etad śrutam tu idam etad tu anumitam ca iti lokoktiḥ iha sākṣiṇī yatas  kutaścid  vaidharmyam sādharmyam api kenacid  sarvatra sulabham kāmam iha api parigṛhyate atas  smṛti anubhūti ākhyā vibhāgāt api na ucitam pramāṇa dvi tvam iti evam prāk uktā eva su paddhatiḥ trividha unubhavaḥ ca eva tad mūlā ca tathā smṛtiḥ iti ṣoḍhā vibhāge tu na vimanyāmahe vayam anubhūti vibhāgena tad mūlāyāḥ smṛteḥ api vibhāgasya gata artha tvāt aikarāśyam udāhṛtam atas  hi tasyāḥ tad mūleṣu antarbhāva vivakṣayā pramāṇa vargam tri tvena prāñcaḥ kecid viviñcate evam anyat api cintyam iti nanu anena na kim pramāṇa cintā kleśena avimṛśya api pramāṇa vargam upalambha anvaya vyatireka ādi vaśāt paśu ādīnām iva manuṣya ādīnām api laukikeṣu artheṣu pravṛtti nivṛtti tad prayojana ādikam nirupadravam sidhyati alaukikeṣu api tad tad vidhāyakaiḥ tad anugrāhakaiḥ ca kalpa sūtra ādibhiḥ carita artha dhiyām kim anena piṣṭa peṣaṇa ādi kalpena vṛthā vimarśena iti ced  mā evam avakāśa uparodhāya tattva upaplavam icchatām aviparyāsa siddhyai ca viśodhyā mānayat hatiḥ pratisaṃdhāya ca phanalam prārambha āhnika darśitam sādhya prameya saṃśuddhyai sa aṅge māne pariśramaḥ pratyakṣita samasta arthaiḥ yogi indra enar api laṅghyate pramāṇa plavam ālambya tattva viplava sāgaraḥ tasmāt ukta rītyā śuddhiḥ kartavyā iti śuddha anyāya niṣevitā śruti śiraḥ śuddhānta siddhāntinī bhadrāṇām pratipādanāya bhajatu pratyakṣa tām akṣatām patyau nitya rase samam karuṇayā pātivratīm bibhratī sarva granthivimocanī bhagavatī sā me samīcī kṛtiḥ iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedānta ācāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau smṛti adhyāye evam sa parikaram pramāṇam viśodhitam atha prameyam pradarśayāmaḥ tatra yad  punar  ṣaṣ sapta ādi rūpeṇa padārthān vibhajya vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ cintayanti tad na sākṣāt apavarga aṅgam iti taiḥ eva abhyupetam api ca vidyamāna parityāgāt asatām ca parigrahāt  vyāmohanā vimarśāḥ te bahiṣkāryā mumukṣubhiḥ sāvāntara vibhāgeṣu tad tad cintā āśrameṣu iha avistarāya diś mātram doṣāṇām abhidadhmahe yad  tatra āhuḥ abhidheyaḥ padārthaḥ sa ca bhāva abhāva bhedena dvidhā iti tad  tāvat  asat vyapadeśāt na iti ced na dharma antareṇa vākya śeṣāt i ukteḥ śabda antarāt ca iti ārambhaṇa adhikaraṇa sūtreṇa abhāvasya para abhyupagata abhāva abhāvasya iva bhāva antaratva samarthanāt  pratikṣiptam yad api ca dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya rūpeṇa bhāva rūpāṇām padārthānām ṣoḍhā parisaṃkhyānam tad api vaiśeṣika adhikaraṇe samavāya abhyupagamāt ca sāmyāt anavasthiteḥ iti sūtrakāraiḥ eva samavāya ākhya padārtha antara dūśaṇena parāḥ tam abhāva tad adhikaraṇayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva saṃnidhi viśeṣa ādi śabda vācya saṃbandha antara anumānam api samavāya dūṣaṇa  chāyayā eva dūṣitam eva yaḥ ca anyonyam atyanta tulyeṣu mukta ātma ādiṣu mithas  vyāvṛtta dhī jananāya dravyatva ādi hetunā viśeṣa ākhyaḥ padārthaḥ kalpyate sā upi tulya nyāyatayā sūtra kāraiḥ dūṣita prāya eva mahat dīrghavat vā hva sva parimaṇḍalābhyām iti anupapanna paramāṇu dvi aṇuka ādi prakriyā nidarśanena anyeṣām api tad abhyupagatānāmunapapannatvasya sūcita tvāt ca api ca anityeṣu dravyeṣu tāvat jāti guṇa pādibhiḥ eva vyāvṛtta dhīḥ sidhyati iti nityeṣu hi viśeṣaḥ nyaḥ kalpyate yathā āhuḥ nitya dravya vṛtta yontyā viśeṣāḥ iti tathā api veda antibhiḥ diś saṃjñaka vibhu padārtha antara anabhyupagamāt ākāśasya ca kāryatva ādi śruteḥ prakṛti vikāra bhūta pṛthivī ādi aṃśa viśeṣa atirikta paramāṇu jāla pratikṣepāt  tathāvidha paramāṇūnām ca avasthā pravāhasya anādi anta tvāt na tatra viśeṣa kḷptiḥ tatas  kāla ātmānau pariśiṣyete tatra api cetanānām na kāla tattvam ātma tayā bhāti kṣaṇa lava ādi avasthā yogitva parāktvā acetanatva ādibhiḥ eva tasmāt  sveṣām svebhyaḥ ca tasya vyāvṛtta dhī saṃbhavāt  anyathā anyena api kalpitena tad asaṃbhava prasaṅgāt  atas  ātma pariśeṣe tatra api jīveśvarayoḥ aṇutva vibhutva niyāmyatva niyantṛtva ādheyatva ādhāratva śeṣatva śeṣitva śarīratva śarīr itvābhiḥ anekavidhaiḥ dharma bhedaiḥ vyāvṛtta dhī siddhau kim anyena viśeṣeṇa tad atyanta sāmyavatsu mukteṣu nityeṣu api hi tad sāmyasya eva saṃrakṣaṇāya dharmi grāhaka siddhā yāvat ātma bhāvinaḥ te te viśeṣā na parityaktāḥ na ca īśvara dvaitam yena īśvarāṇām mithas vyāvṛtta pratītyai viśeṣam kalpayiṣyāmaḥ ekasya eva sarva deśa kāleṣu ekātapatra tayā sarva śruti siddha tvāt asya eva ca sāmānya śabdaiḥ viśeṣa śabdaiḥ ca rūḍhitaḥ  yogataḥ tad tad vasatu viśiṣṭatva ādinā ca tad tad prakaraṇa anuguṇam śarīrake pratipādyatva sthāpanāt  jīveṣu api baddhānām mithas  bhedaḥ tad tad sukha duḥkha dhi icchā vaicitryeṇa vyaktaḥ baddha muktayoḥ ca kiñcijjñatva sarvajñatva ādibhiḥ muktānām nityānām ca viśuddheḥ ādimattva anādimattvābhyām eva vibhakta dhī saṃbhavaḥ mukta daśāyām nityebhyaḥ kim vaiṣmyam iti ced  kim tena prāktanena tad tad ātma varti tayā pratyakṣitena guṇa ādi bhedena tad anya vyāvṛtta dhī siddheḥ siddhaiḥ api tad vyavahāre prāktana upādhi bhedaiḥ eva tad tad pramāṇa pramitaiḥ pratisaṃhitaiḥ sarva nirvāhāt etena muktānām mithas  vibhakta buddhiḥ api nirvyūḍhā na hi teṣām eka rūpaḥ prāktanaḥ saṃsāraḥ viṣama vipāka samaya anādya saṃkhyāta karma pravāha vaicitrya pratiniyata deśa kāla svarūpa sukha duḥkha tad kāraṇa ādi saṃtateḥ eva mithas  vyāvartaka tvāt  tad atad vibhāgaḥ  hi tad kāla vartinā evam dharmeṇa iti na niyamaḥ atad kālavartinā api tad niṣṭhatayā upalabhyamānena tad siddheḥ na hi atītaḥ saṃsāraḥ  mukta ātma svarūpam upalabhamānaiḥ na upalabhyate upalabhyamānaḥ  vā anya niṣṭhaḥ pratibhāti atha nityeṣu mithas  kā vārtrā sā api kuśala eva teṣām api hi satya saṃkalpānām vicitrāḥ saṃkalpa icchādaya riśvarasya iva aniyata deśa kāla viṣaya aparyanuyojya sāmagrīkā anādi ananta saṃtānavantaḥ santi iti kim anyena viśeṣeṇa api ca yad darśane yatra yad āropaḥ  na bhavati sa hi tasya tatas  bhedaḥ sa eva ca viśeṣaḥ sa ced  sva rūpa bhūtaḥ hantvam ādi rūpeṇa bhātaḥ para āropam pratirundhyāt  kaḥ tatonyaḥ tatas  viśeṣaḥ tasya evam anabhyupagame viśeṣa kḷptau  api kā gatiḥ vaiśeṣikasya sva para nirvāhakāḥ te viśeṣāḥ iti ced  kim ta eva api ca pṛthaktve vidyamāne kim taiḥ viśeṣaiḥ pṛthaktu asya eka jāti saṃgṛhīta tvāt na tata upi vyāvṛtta dhīri iti ced  tarhi tatas  na kvacid api syāt  viśeṣeṣu api vā viśeṣatva ākrānteṣu kaḥ te nistāraḥ viśeṣa tvam nāma jātiḥ na asti iti ced  kim tad  upādhiḥ iticed  kim tatas  na saṃgrahaḥ tathā sati kvacid api tad nibandhana anuvṛtta dhī bhaṅga prasaṅgāt  evam anyonya abhāvena api gatārtha tā dustara iti parāstaḥ para abhimata viśeṣaḥ sāmānyam api para uktam sūtrakāraiḥ eva nirasta prāyam tathā hi tad ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ityādibhiḥ sūtraiḥ kārya daśāyām upādānasya avasthā antara āpatti mātram eva na punar  para abhimatam avayavi ākhyam dravyam asti iti samarthanād ghaṭa ādi avayavi abhāve tad āśrita ghaṭatva ādi sāmānyam avayavi samaveta tayā abhyupagata guṇa ādayaḥ tad ubhaya ārambha prakriyā jālam ca nirmūlitam yad ca upādānasya ghaṭatva ādi rūpam avasthā antaram saṃyoga viśeṣa ādi rūpam tad  paraiḥ api kārya tayā abhyupetam upalambha ādibhiḥ ca tathā eva sidhyati iti na tatra api nityatva kalpanā vakāśaḥ tatas  sarveṣām dravyāṇām sva rūpa tona ādi ananta tvāt kārya dravyatva ātmatva ādi mātram eva śiṣyate guṇeṣu nityeṣu avasthā rūpeṣu ca anuvṛtta pratyaya nimittam kim iti cintyam tatra evam bhāṣitam śārīraka ādye saṃsthāna atirekiṇonekeṣu eka ākāra buddhi bodhyasya adarśanāt  tāvatā eva gaḥtva ādi jāti vyavahāra upapatteḥ atireka vādepi saṃsthānasya saṃpratipanna tvāt ca saṃsthānam eva jāti saṃsthānam nāma svāsa ādhāraṇam rūpam iti yathāvastu saṃsthānam anusaṃdheyam iti etad uktam bhavati kim saṃsthāna atiriktam sāmānyam vivikta sphuṭa pratyakṣa adhyavasāya bhedāt aṅgīkriyate uta upapatti balāt iti na ādyaḥ asiddheḥ na antyaḥ anyathā siddheḥ atirikta sāmānyam abhyupagacchata upi hi tad upalakṣaṇam saṃsthānam iṣṭam dṛṣṭam ca prativyakti niyatam saṃsthānam katham anuvṛtta pratyaya kāraṇam iti ced  katham vā tad jātīyasya lakṣaṇam bhavati anuvṛtta jāti antara saṃgṛhīta upādhi rūpatayā iti ced  tāvatā eva gavā ādi vyavahāra siddhau kim anyena tathā api anta tonuvṛttam sāmānyam kvacid abhyupagantavyam yatra ananyathā siddhiḥ anyathā upādhi saṃgrahasya api asaṃbhavāt iti ced  tava api vā tatra sāmānyam upalakṣaṇena saṃgṛhyate na vā pūrvatra anyathā asiddhiḥ anavasthitiḥ ca uttaratra niyāmaka adarśanāt jāteḥ āśraya vyavasthā na syāt  vyāvṛttānām api svabhāvata eva kāsāṃcid  vyaktīnām tad vyañjakatva niyatiḥ iti ced  sa eva svabhāvaḥ kim na vyavahāram niyachet  nirviṣayaḥ katham vyavahāraḥ syāt iti ced  tāsām eva vyaktīnām viṣaya tvāt  vyāvṛttānām anuvṛtta vyavahāra viṣaya tve sarvatra viṣaya vyavasthā bhajyeta iti ced  vyāvṛttānām anuvṛtta vyañjaka tve sarvatra tad vyaktiḥ kim na syāt  saṃbandhā saṃbandhābhyām niyamāt iti ced na saṃbandhasya api samavāya nāmnaḥ sārvatrikatva abhyupagamāt tatra api abhivyakti pratiniyamasya mṛgya tvāt  nānā samavāya vādepi vyakti svabhāva niyamasya dustyaja tvāt  tathā api dṛṣṭa eka gaḥ vyakteḥ vyakti antare soyam iti pratyabhijñānam katham syāt  ayam gauḥ iti eka vyaktau vyutpāditaḥ ca katham vyakti atyantarepi tad śabdavācya tām pratīyāt  iti ced  tava api vā katham eka dharma samavāyāt iti ced  tena eva dharmeṇa svatas  militasya samavāyasya eva nityam sarvatra vṛtti abhyupagamena sarvatra sarva vyavahāra saṃkara prasaṅgāt  kāsāṃcid eva vyaktīnām tad vyañjakatva svābhāvyāt  vyavasthā uktā iti ced  tarhi tāsām eva vyaktīnām pratisaṃdhāna vyavahārayoḥ viṣaya tvam astu tathā sati bhrānta tvam tayoḥ syāt iti ced na tad vyakti tvena pratisaṃdhāna ādeḥ abhāvāt  api tarhi tathā tvena vyakti svarūpa atiriktam tathā tvam nāma antareṇa jātiḥ eva syāt iti ced  tad jāti vyañjakam tad tad eka vyakti svarūpa atiriktam kim na jāti antaram syāt  upādhi viśeṣa eva ayam pratiniyata āśraya iti ced  evam tarhi pratiniyata pratiyogikam svabhāva niyatam paraspara smāraka tvam upajīvya tad jātīya tayā pratisaṃdhāna vyavahāra upapattau kim anya kalpanena tasmāraka taditara vibhāgaḥ kutastya iti ced  tad vyañjaka taditara vibhāgaḥ te kutastyaḥ darśana at arśana āyatta iti ced  tulyam saṃbandha sādṛśyayoḥ abhāve katham smāraka tvam iti ced  tayoḥ vā katham sadṛśa saha anubhūta darśanasya saṃskāra udbodhaka tvāt iti ced  tad api kutas  kārya darśanāt kalpyate iti ced  tulyam anyathā saṃbandham sādṛśyam vā ekam upādāya tad anyasya katham smāraka tvam iti ca udyasya durvāra tvāt  na ca atra sādṛśyam na aṅgīkurmaḥ sausādṛśya rūpatva abhyupagamāt sāmānyasya nāma antareṇa para abhimata jāti svīkāraḥ iti ced  vyāvṛttānām saṃniveśa ādīnām eva pratiniyata pratiyogi smāraka svabhāva tayā sādṛśya rūpa tvāt gavaya ādeḥ api tarhi gaḥ jātīyatva ādi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na sādṛśya sausādṛśya vibhāga svaya sāṃpratyayikasya sarva saṃmata tvāt iti evam sāmānya ādiṣu sūtrakāra ādibhiḥ nirasteṣu pariśiṣṭā dravya guṇa karma rūpāḥ trayaḥ padārthāḥ iti kecid ācāryāḥ anye tu manyanteyathā tad pratīteḥ anyathā siddha tayā te padārthā bhāṣya kāra ādibhiḥ nirasyante tathā karma api iti ye tāvat iha sarvatra sūrya parispanda ādivat apratyakṣam karma phala anumeyam icchanti tatra yayā sāmagryā karmaṇaḥ siddhiḥ abhimatā tayā eva dṛṣṭam karma phalam sādhya tām kim antarā kalpitena karmaṇā tathā api ced  kḷptiḥ anyatra api kāla viprakarṣa ādarśanepi sāmagrī kāryayoḥ madhye anyasya kḷpti prasaṅgaḥ tathā eva ca tratrāpi iti anavasthā syāt  ye ca pratyakṣam karma iti āhuḥ taiḥ api nūnam karma phala tvena abhyupagama saṃyoga vibhāga atiriktam nipuṇa nirīkṣaṇepi na upalabhyata iti manyāmahe calati pratyayopi hi tāvatā eva caritārthaḥ na ca vācyam yāvat saṃyogam calati pratyaya prasaṅga iti pūrva deśa vibhāga pūrvaka deśa antara saṃyoga prathama kṣaṇa viṣaya tvāt tad pratyayasya tatas  eva hi uttara kāle saṃyoge vartamānepya calat iti bhūta anusaṃdhānam upapannam nanu pravāha madhya sthite sthāṇau pūrva salila skandha viyogaḥ uttara salila skandha yogaḥ ca dṛśyate na ca tatra cala tvam icchāmaḥ vyoma ādaya eva sthira deśa tvena vivakṣitāḥ iti ced na pravāhasya tatas  viśeṣa adarśanāt  laulyam viśeṣaḥ iti ced  tarhi saṃyoga vibhāga atiriktam laulya rūpam karma pratyakṣam iti katham tad apahnavaḥ iti tatra āhuḥyā nāma karma sāmagrī tvayā iṣyate sā tad tad karma phala tayā abhimatam saṃyoga viśeṣam utpādayantī niyata svabhāvam eva tam utpādayati ata eva eva saṃyogoneka niṣṭhopi san kvacid calati pratyaṃyam kvacid  saṃyoga mātra pratyayam ca janayati yathā eka eva samavāyaḥ guṇa guṇibhyām aviśeṣeṇa svatas  militopi san kvacid āśraya pratyayam kvacid āśrita pratyayam ca janayati na hi āśraya bhāva āśrita bhāvaḥ  vā samavāya svarūpa atiriktaḥ tadvat iha api iti vayam tu brūmaḥ apratyakṣa karma vādaḥ tāvat  prāc ukta dūṣaṇāt ayuktaḥ pratyakṣam tu karma svarūpataḥ  durapahnavam tatra bhāṣya ādiṣu atireka vidhi niṣedha adarśanāt artha antara virodha abhāvāt ca udāsitavyam iti idam tu manyāmahe atirekepi guṇa vargān na rāśi antaram karma vibhājaka abhāvāt sva icchā kalpita vibhājakasya sarvatra sulabha tvena yathā abhimatam ekam guṇam ubhayam vāṅgīkṛtya rāśi antara kalpana prasaṅgāt  guṇa avāntara vaicitryasya guṇatva virodha abhāvāt atas  dravyam adravyam iti eva vibhāgaḥ iti tatra ca ātma guṇa tayā abhimateṣu sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ pañca tad tad utpādaka tayā abhimata buddhi viśeṣānatiriktā veda artha saṃgrahe samarthitāḥ dharma adharmau vihita niṣiddha kriyā sādhya tayā abhimatau  ājñāvataḥ  rājña iva sarva praśāsituḥ īśvarasya anugraha nigraha ākhya buddhi viśeṣa rūpau bhāṣya ādiṣu bahuṣu pradeśeṣu prapañcitau yaḥ punar  saṃskāraḥ sa tāvat buddhi viśeṣa ātmanā uktaḥ na ca tad prayuktaḥ tatas ciranaṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa ākāre vyāpti adarśanāt vāsanā anuvṛtteḥ ca vācanika tvāt  yadi api indriyasya indriyasya arthe iti ādi gītāślokeṣu bhāṣya kāraiḥ vāsanāyā icchā dvāreṇa eva pravṛtti hetutva vacanāt jñāna vāsanā viśeṣa atiriktā karma vāsanā na asti tathā api jñāna vāsanā durapahnavā tatas ca tad āśraya mātram vicāryam tatra dharma bhūta jñānasya dravya tvaṃnyāya tattva ātma siddhi bhāśi ādi siddham anusara tām tad niṣṭha smṛti ākhya vikāra utpādakaḥ saṃskāraḥ  api tad niṣṭhaḥ prāptaḥ antaraṅga tvāt abādhāt ca ye tu para paribhāṣam anusarantaḥ tad anuguṇam tasya guṇa tvam gṛhṇanti teṣām ātmani eva saṃskāraḥ iti viśeṣaḥ na ca buddhoḥ nitya tvam saṃkoca vikāsa ādi daśā bhedam ca abhyupagacchadbhiḥ adravya tvam tasyāḥ su vacam avasthā antara yogi tvam eva hi upādana tvam tad eva hi dravya lakṣaṇam tathā api naguṇatva hāniḥ apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇatva atirikta guṇatva avadarśanāt  karma vyatirikta jāti mātra āśrayatva ādi rūpa guṇa lakṣaṇa saṃketasya asmābhiḥ anādaraṇāt na ca dravyasya āśrita svabhāvatva lakṣaṇam apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa tvam viruddham avayavini yuṣmābhiḥ api svīkaraṇāt  yathā ca dravyatva viśeṣaṇatva ādibhiḥ na virodha iṣyate evam atra api upalaṃmbha yukti ādeḥ sāmana carca tvāt  atas  jñānam dravyam tad avasthā viśeṣāḥ tu adravyāṇi iti saṃskāra ākhya vikāra āsthitiḥ api tatra eva yuktā vega ākhyaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ tad utpādakatva abhimata karma viśaiṣa atiriktaḥ  na dṛśyate na ca yujyate sthita sthāpakau tu karma nivṛttau  api tad avinābhūta saṃyoga viśeṣa tvam vaktum yuktam ye ca bhagavatā unantā maṅgala guṇāḥ prakīrtyante te sarvepi ṣāṅguṇya vitati rūpāḥ iti saṃmatam yathā āhuḥ tava ananta guṇasya api ṣaṭ eva prathame guṇāḥ yaiḥ tvayā iva jagat  kukṣau  anyepi antar niveśitāḥ iti ṣaṭsu ca guṇeṣu balam dhāraṇa sāmarthyam aiśvaryam niyamana śaktiḥ vikāra hetuṣu api avikṛta tvam vīryam tejaḥ para abhibhavana sāmarthyam anya anapekṣa tā vā iti lakṣitānām caturṇām atimathane jñāna śakti vitati rūpa tvam vyaktam na ca jñāna śaktyoḥ api evam mithas ntarbhāvaḥ śakyaḥ ajñeṣu api dravyeṣu śakti darśanāt  aśakteṣu api jñāna darśanāt  ata eva jñāna viśeṣaḥ śaktiḥ iti api nirastam śakti viśeṣaḥ tu jñānam syāt iti ced  kosau śakti śabda arthaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ  guṇa viśeṣaḥ prabhākara ādi nayena padārtha antaram vā iti ced  na tarhi jñānasya tad viśeṣa tā sidhyet  atha kārya upayukta viśeṣaṇa mātram śaktiḥ iti sarva prayoga anugatam paśyasi tadā na kevalam jñānasya api tu sarvasya eva śakti tvam prāptam sarvasya api pradhāna kāraṇa tayā abhimate kasmiṃścid viśeṣaṇa tvena avasthānāt nanu evam udayana ādīnām iva svarūpa sahakāri vyatirikta śakti abhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ iti ced  ananyathā asiddha yukti vaśāt āgama balāt vā tad siddheḥ tad śabdaḥ tu vivakṣā viśeṣāt  syāt iti brūmaḥ śakti samarthana saṃrambhaḥ ca ācāryāṇām nyāya kuliśe nipuṇam anusaṃdheyaḥ śakti mātra kāraṇa ādi vādāḥ ca bāhyānām upalambha yukti āpta āgama ādi virahāt anādaraṇīyāḥ sā ced upādānam sūkṣmandravyam eva asau syāt iti na vivādaḥ atha ācit dravya viśeṣa guṇān paśyāmaḥ tatra śabda ādayaḥ pañca tad tad bhūta vartinaḥ pratyakṣa ādi balāt abhyupagatāḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi ca śāstra anusāreṇa saṃyogaḥ ca pratyakṣa ādi siddhaḥ nairantarya mātram eva ayam iti ced  tad  kim dravya svarūpam uta āgantuḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ na ādyaḥ nityatva prasaṅgāt  na dvitīyaḥ nāma antareṇa tad abhidhānāt  iti vibhāga pṛthaktve tu abhāva ukta nyāyena dūṣaṇīye paratva aparatve api sukha ādi  chāyayā na hi tad tad upādhi avacchinna deśa kāla viśeṣa saṃbandha atirikte paratva aparatve paśyāmaḥ tad kalpane ca prāktva pratyaktvādayopi hi bahavaḥ  guṇāḥ tulya nyāyāḥ kalpyāḥ syuḥ evam sat asat guṇa pradarśana prakriyayā saṃkhyā parimāṇa gurutva dravatva snehānām tattvam avasātavyam iti adravyeṣu eṣā diś  atha dravyāṇi vimṛśyante tatra tāvat  kaumārila abhimata vibhu śabda ākhya dravya vādaḥ śabdasya acit avasthā viśeṣa tvena śruti ādi siddha tvāt nirākāryaḥ ātma siddhau tu śabdasya dharmī ati vartitva gatimattva vādaḥ tad āśraya bhūta avayava dvāreṇa iti netavyaḥ yad tu tamaḥ khalu calam nīlam para apara vibhāgavat  prasiddha dravya vaidharmyāt navabhyaḥ  bhettum arhati iti āhuḥ tad etad  dravyam tāvat abhyupagacchāmaḥ tathā hi uktam varada gurubhiḥ tattva sāre tamaḥ  nāma dravyam bahula viralam mecaka calam pratīmaḥ kena api kvacid api na bādhaḥ ca dadṛśe atas  kalpyaḥ  hetuḥ pramitiḥ api śābdī vijayate nirālokam cakṣuḥ prathayati hi tad  darśana vaśāt  iti etena viyati vitatānām sūkṣmāṇām pṛthivī avayavānām kṛṣṇaḥ  guṇaḥ tama iti pakṣa upi pratikṣiptaḥ sa āśrayasya eva tasya grahaṇa virodha abhāvāt guṇa mātra tayā ca kasya api anupalambhāt  sparśa rūpa rasānām ca śabda gandhavat  bhrāntau pramitau vā nirādhāra grahaṇa adarśanāt ca eti evam dravya tve siddhe kṛṣṇa varṇasya dravyasya pṛthivī tvam eva abhyupagantum ucitam yad  kṛṣṇam tad annasya iti śruteḥ yadi api pṛthivyām pāka viśeṣa vaśāt  śukla ādi rūpam na anyatra pākāt api bhavati ākāśa ādiṣu nailya upalambha upi hi pañcīkaraṇa mūla pṛthivī saṃsargāt  ākāśe ca aviśeṣāt iti sūtre bhāṣitam aṇḍa antarvartinaḥ ca ākāśasya trivṛt karaṇa upadeśa pradarśinta pañcī karaṇena rūpava tvāt cākṣuṣa tvepya virodhaḥ iti nanu evam ākāśam eva dravya antara saṃsargāt nīlam tama iti upalabhyate iti syāt iti ced  na syāt  ākāśe tama iti pṛthak upalambha svārasyāt dravnaya antara tve tu kalpanā gauravāt antatotrā api pañcīkaraṇena dravya antara saṃsargasya abhyupagata tvāt ca iti sparśa anupalambhaḥ tu indranīla āloka durdina ātapa ādeḥ iva anudbhava ādeḥ api syāt  na ca pārthiva rūpasya sarvasya āloka sāpekṣa cakṣuḥ grāhyatva niyamaḥ kalpyaḥ karaṇa vaicitryāt iva viṣaya vaicitryāt api vyavasthā upapatteḥ divā bhītānām viśiṣṭa añjana rañjita akṣāṇām ca āloka nirapekṣam eva cakṣuṣā eva padārthā gṛhyante āloka abhāva mātre ca tamasi tamaḥ jyotiṣoḥ nivṛtti vacanam cavyāhanyeta pratiniyata nailya āropakalpanā prayāsaḥ ca atas  pṛthivī viśeṣa tvam tamasaḥ  yuktam pṛthivī ādīni pañca bhūtāni manaḥ ca triguṇa dravya pariṇati viśeṣa tayā śruti ādi siddha tvāt na pṛthak dravyāṇi tatra ca avayavi ākhyam bhautika dravyam tad ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ ityādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sūtraiḥ buddhi śabda antara ādeḥ anyathā siddhi ādi upapādanena nirastam mahat dīrghavat vā hva sva parimaṇḍalābhyām ityādibhiḥ ca parām abhimataḥ paramāṇuḥ atas  pariṇāma viśeṣāt upalambha yogyatva ayogyatva ādi daśā viśeṣa yogi prakṛti ādi saṃjñam dravyam vicitra vyavasthita kramasamaṣṭi vyaṣṭi rūpam avatiṣṭhate diś tattvam api tad tad upādhi avacchinnāḥ tad tad deśa viśeṣā eva atirikta kalpakānām parāpara pratyaya viśeṣa ādīnām anyathā siddheḥ diś utpatti śrutiḥ ca tad upādhika tad nirvāhaka sṛṣṭyā upapannā anyathā dyupṛthivī antarikṣa ādivat  triguṇa pariṇati viśeṣa tā eva syāt  na pṛthak dravya tā na ca evam kālepi prasaṅgaḥ nityasya kālasya bhagavat parāśara ādibhiḥ pṛthak prasaṃkhyānāt  tasya prakṛti pariṇati viśeṣatva ādi pakṣāḥ tad pūrva apara kāla avaśyaṃbhāvāt śruti ādi balāt ca pratyastāḥ atas triguṇa kālau  ātmāca iti trīṇi siddhānir iśvarasya tu pṛthak saṃkhyāne catvāri tasya hi cetanatva ādibhiḥ saṃgraha saṃbhavepi avāntara vailakṣaṇya jñāpanāya pṛthak saṃkhyānam prācāmanādi vācām ca anyathā prakriyā antareṇa acetaneṣu api saṃgraha prasaṃgāt  viviktam ca bhagavatā parāśareṇa parama ātma ātmanoḥ yogaḥ parama artha iti iṣyate mithyā etad anya dravyam hi na eti tad dravyatām yatas  iti evam dharma bhūta jñāna ākhyam api dravyam ajaḍatva aviśeṣepi spuṭatara vaidharmya anatara balāt pṛthak gaṇayanti tasya adravyatva vādaḥ keṣāñcit nātha muni yāmuna muni bhāṣya kāra ādi prabandha virodhāt prāyas  para citta rañjana arthaḥ śuddha sattva ākhyasya ca dravya antarasya para vigraha ādi yātha arthya upadeśa pravṛtta nirukta ādi āpta āgama siddha tvāt sūkṣma triguṇa avasthā viśeṣa ādi pakṣā bahiṣkāryāḥ atas  ṣaṭ etāni dravyāṇi bhoktṛ bhogya niyantṝṇām sat ā ātmanā eka dravyatva ādi pakṣā api nirviśeṣa sanmātra pakṣavat  vyāghāta śruti virodha ādibhiḥ bahuśas  bhāṣya ādiṣu nirastāḥ tatra triguṇa śuddha sattve sva niruktyā eva lakṣye kṣaṇa lava ādi ātmā kālaḥ aṇuḥ jñātā jīvaḥ vibhuḥ tu īśvaraḥ jāna ati vyavahārāsa ādhāraṇa kāraṇam vyavahārya viśeṣaḥ  matiḥ evam triguṇa kāla jīva īśvara śuddha sattva m ati rūpeṇa ṣoḍhā dravya vibhāgaḥ evam pramāṇa sārtha ghaṇṭā pathena dravya adravya rūpa prameya grāmam adhijigamiṣatām na kudṛṣṭi bāhya kalpita kūṭa yukti garta nipātaḥ iti iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedānta ācāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau prameya adhyāye prathamam āhnikam atra yadi api pramā viṣayaḥ prameyam iti vyutpattyā āropita ākāra vyavaccheda arthayā anāropita rūpam sarvam prameyam tathā api niḥśreyasa antaraṅga tayā tad arthibhiḥ prakarṣeṇa meyam prameyam iha vivakṣim yad viṣayeṇa bhrameṇa saṃsarāmaḥ yad viṣayeṇa ca tattva jñānena apavarjyemahi tad iha naḥ prakarṣeṇa meyam prameyam tad ca dvādaśavidham ukta mākṣapāde ātma śarīra indriya artha buddhi manaḥ pravṛtti doṣa pretya bhāva phala duḥkha apavargāḥ prameyam iti tatra cetana ātmā sa dvidhā ariśvaronīśvara iti jagatkartār iśvaraḥ jagat vyāpāra rahitaḥ cetanoni īśvaraḥ yad caitanya samāna adhikaraṇam yad apṛthak siddham yad dravyam tad  tasya śarīram tad  dvividham karma jam akarma jam ca iti ādyam asmad ādīnām dvitīyam īśvara ādīnām sāttvika ahaṅkāra upādānakam dravyam indriyam tad ekādaśavidhampañca jñāna indriyāṇi pañcakarmenidrayāṇi manaḥ ca iti indriya gocarā iha arthāḥ te ca śabda ādayaḥ  guṇāḥ tad viśiṣṭāni ca artha prakāśaḥ  buddhiḥ smṛti ādi karaṇam indriyam manaḥ manaḥ vāc kāyānām puṇya apuṇya rūpaḥ  vyāpāra iha pravṛttiḥ tathāvidha pravṛtti hetavaḥ  doṣāḥ te ca saṃgrahāt rāga dveṣa mohāḥ pūrva deham vihāya uttara deha prāptiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ pravṛtti sādhyam phalam tad eva puruṣeṇa pravṛtti phala tayā uddiṣṭam prayojanam pratikūla vedanīyam duḥkham tatra sukha tad sādhana ādikam api viṣa saṃpṛkta madhuvat  prabhūta anartha anuṣaṅgi tvāt  duḥkham eva mumukṣuṇā bhāvyam iti tasya api pratikūla vedanīya tvam duḥkha antara kāraṇa asamāna adhikaraṇā duḥkha nivṛttiḥ apavargaḥ sa ca svābhāvika ātma svarūpa āvirbhāva pūrvaka samasta vibhūti guṇa viśiṣṭa niratiśaya ānanda brahma anubhava garbhaḥ iti parama puruṣa arthaḥ tad pūrva kaḥ vā tādṛśa brahma anubhava upavargaḥ iti etad eva ca prameyam saṃgrahāt caturdhā vibhajya kecid anusaṃdadhate aheyam tasya nivartakam hānam tasya upāyaḥ iti ye tu kaṇa caraṇa ādayaḥ ṣaṣ sapta ādi rūpeṇa sarvān padārthān vibhajya parīkṣante te sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya ādīnām padārtha antaratva pratikṣepeṇa nirastāḥ tatas ca dravya guṇa karmāṇi trīṇi eva avaśiṣyante tatra api karmaṇaḥ saṃpratipanna guṇa atiriktatva pakṣepi saṃskāra ādi guṇa avāntara viśeṣavat  guṇa pakṣa kakṣīkārāt dvau padārthau tatra ca guṇa śabdasya apṛthak siddha viśeṣaṇa mātra vyutpannasya tathāvidheṣu keṣucid  dravyeṣu api vṛtteḥ dravya guṇa rūpeṇa vibhāgān aucityāt  dravyam adravyam iti eva padārtha vibhāgam ādriyāmaheḥ  idṛśasya tu vicārasya apavarge paraṃparayā upayogaḥ mumukṣūṇām pradhānatamam tu prameyam viśiṣṭam brahma ekam eva iti manvānaḥ  bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ atha atas  brahma jijñāsā iti upakramya tad eva sa prakāram nirūpitavān tad prakāra tayā eva anyat prameyam kecid tu deha ātma viveka krama anusāreṇa bhoktā bhogyam preritāram ca matvā iti śruti prakriyayā ca tridhā tattvam vibhajya cintayanti tatra api sa prakāra dravya cintanāda dravya cintā api antar bhavati tad tulya nyāya tayā kāla cintā ca tad abhiprāyeṇa kālasya padārtha viśeṣaṇa tayā eva samasta vastu prati iti antar bhāvāt na pṛthak asti tvāt ayaḥ  vaktavyāḥ na ca parihartavyāḥ kālosti na asti iti vyavahāraḥ  vyavahartṝṇām jāti ādi astitvanāstitva vyavahāra tulyaḥ iti jaina nirākaraṇa samaye bhāṣya kāraiḥ uktam ātatas ca brahma ekam eva tattvam iti vā cit acit īśvara bhedena trīṇi tattvāni iti vā paśyatām na kaśvidviśeṣaḥ svarūpa bhedasya viśiṣṭa aikyasya ca ubhayeṣām abhimata tvāt  ata eva pradhāna puruṣa vyakta kālāḥ tu pravibhāgaśaḥ rūpāṇi sthiti sarga anta vyakti sadbhāva hetavaḥ ityādi anusāreṇa caturdhā pañcadhā vā vibhajya cintayatām kārya viśeṣaiḥ saha pañca ṣaṣ saptaviṃśati ādi saṃkhyām niveśayatām ca pūrva aviśeṣa eva śrūyate ca tam ṣaṅviṃśakam iti āhuḥ saptaviṃśam atha apare puruṣam nirguṇam sāṃravyam atharvaśirasaḥ  viduḥ iti prāpyam prāptā prāpti upāyaḥ nivartyam phalam ca iti kecid  pañcadhā prameyam parisaṃcakṣate saṃbandha viśeṣeṇa saha anye ṣoḍhā iti atha ayam aparaḥ pravṛtti arthaḥ saṃgraha ūnuṣṭhāna parihāra antaraṅgaḥ tathā hi hitam ahitam ca prakarṣeṇa meyam tatra laukika hita ahitayoḥ anvaya vyatireka āyurvedanīti śāstra ādikam pramāṇam tad api yoga sādhana bhūta śarīra rakṣaṇa artham mumukṣuṇā api śruti smṛti ādya virodhena anusaraṇīyam alaukika hita ahitayoḥ tu vedāḥ pramāṇam tad upabṛṃhaṇa tayā smṛti itihāsa purāṇāni ca yad ca śruti vihitam tad akhilam api yathā adhikāram hitam yad ca tad niṣiddham tad akhilam api ahitam nanu abhicāra ādi karmaṇām anartha hetūnām kṣudra puruṣa artha sādhanānām ca kāmyānām karmaṇām katham hita tvam ucyatea dhika ari viśeṣam apekṣya hi sarvaḥ  vidhiḥ niṣedhaḥ ca yathā uktam traiguṇya viṣayā vedāḥ iti yaḥ  hi sukham duḥkha nivṛttim ca icchati tasya tad sādhanam apekṣamāṇasya laukikeṣu sādhaneṣu pravṛttasya teṣām niraya ādi hetu bhūta anartha hetu tvena tad parihārāya anartha hetutva rahitāḥ sukha ādi upāyāḥ pratipādyante evam kāmya karmāṇi pāralaukikāni dṛṣṭa jātīya tad adhika phala artha tayā dṛṣṭa anartha āvaha sukha pravṛtti pratibandha aupayika tvāt  hitāni eva rāgiṇām tathā aihalaukikāni api citra ādīni kārīrya ādīni tu jagat hitāni api abhicāra karmaṇā upi hiṃsā ādi yuktasya api svarūpataḥ  na anartha hetu tvam tad aṅga paśu hiṃsā ādeḥ agnīṣomīya ādivat vidhi prāpta tvāt  api tu sva sādhyena aprāpta viṣaya vadha ādinā tad apekṣayā ca abhicāraḥ  niṣidhyate sā upi hi kvacid avaśya kartavya eva ṣaṭsu anabhicaran patet  ityādi darśanāt  atas ca mumukṣoḥ api rakṣaka kṣatriya ādi abhāve rākṣasa ādi abhibhave ca ātma rakṣaṇa artham abhicāraḥ kartavya eva sarvata eva ātmānam gopāyet  iti śāstrāt  anyathā aharahar anuṣṭheyasya aprayāṇāt anuvartanīyasya karma ādeḥ uccheda prasaṅgena upāya aniṣpatteḥ mokṣā siddhi prasaṅgāt  vṛṣṭi anna ādi dṛṣṭa arthāni ca sarvāṇi upāsana niṣpatti aupayika tayā tad tad apekṣāyām anuṣṭheyāni pāralaukikāni tu tad phala abhisaṃdhi viraheṇa karma yoga anuṣṭhāna daśāyām nitya naimittikaiḥ ekīkṛtya kartavyāni naimittikāni hi sarvāṇi prasakta anartha parihāra artha tayā sarva hitāni eva evam nityāni uttara karma adhikāra artha tvāt akaraṇa nimitta pratyavāya parihāra artha tvāt ca atas  śruti vihitam sva varṇa āśrama ucitam sarvam hitam eva ata eva hi smaranti śāstram hi vatsalataram mātā pitṛ sahasrataḥ iti evam sthite pravāha anādi sāmagrī cakra vaśāt aniyata samaya samāgata sakala saiddha antika samālambanīya sucar ita paripāka nivṛtta pratibandha parama puruṣa kaṭākṣa viśeṣa samunmiṣita sattva sāmarthyena kara tala āmalakavat ālokita heya upādeya vibhāgasya ana ādi ananta bahuvidha durviṣaha duḥkha anuṣaṅga dūṣita alpa asthira sāṃsārika sukha maya viṣa madhu virakt samasta durita varga apavargāyamāṇa nitya niratiśaya ānanda mukunda caraṇa aravinda sevā makaranda lampaṭasya yathāśakti varṇa aśrama ucita nitya naimittika niṣiddha parihāra saha kṛtam darśana samāna ākāra dhruva anusmṛti rūpam bhagavat upāsanam hitatamam vihitam tad ca sat akṣara nyāsa vaiśvānara madhu bhūmat harādi bhedena bahuvidham traivarṇika sarva āśrama sādhyam tasya ca mahānīya viṣaya niratiśaya prīti rūpa tvena bhakti śabda vācya tvam ayam eva ca paramaḥ  yogaḥ trayī anta anuvidhāyiṣu sarveṣu mokṣa śāstreṣu pratipādyate yathā āha bhagavān parāśaraḥ ātma prayatna sāpekṣā viśiṣṭā yā manogatiḥ tasyāḥ  brahmaṇi saṃyogaḥ  yoga iti abhidhīyate iti smarati ca bhagavān śāṇḍilī rḥ idṛśaḥ paramātmā ayam pratyagātmā ava tathā īdṛśaḥ tad saṃbandha anusaṃdhānam iti yogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ iti tatra cit acit viveka ādi mātre sāṃkhyam upakurute yama niyama ādi samādhi parikara śodhane yogaḥ itikartavya tā viśeṣe karma kāṇḍa ādayaḥ sarvatra eva pañca rātram niṣiddha kāmya vargeṣu vyarthān āvaśyakeṣu ca śama ādi vidhiḥ anyatra pravṛttyā na virudhyate soyam evaṃvidhaḥ parama yoga ākhyaḥ  dharmaḥ mayi eva mana ādhatsva iti gīyate tad aśaktasya atha cittam samādhātum na śaknoṣi mayi sthiram abhyāsa yogena gataḥ  mām icchā āptum dhanañjaya abhyāseṣu asamarthosi mad karma paramaḥ  bhava ityādinā pūrva parvāṇi vidhīyante yaḥ prīti pūrva bhagavat asā dhāraṇa karmaṇi api na samarthaḥ tasya viṣaya rasa vaimukhya jananāya samasta vaiṣayika sukha śeṣi tvena cirataram anusaṃhitasya api sva ātmanaḥ sāṃsārika samasta sukha samadhika ānanda svarūpam ālokayitum āntara cakṣuḥ virodhi timira paṭala pāṭanāya jñāna karma yoga ākhye dve bheṣaje tatra ātma cintana rūpaḥ  jñāna yogaḥ tad ālokanentaraṅga bhūtaḥ tatra api asamarthasya tad adhikāra siddhi artham karma yogaḥ tena tatra siddha adhikārasya api śiṣṭa tayā vyapadeśyasya antargata ātma jñānaḥ karma yoga eva kāryaḥ anyathā kṛtsna vidā upyasya jñāna yoga aśakta akṛtsna vedi puruṣa buddhi bheda janana mūla mahattara durita vaśena jñāna yoga upi pratibadhyeta tādṛśena eva ca karma yogena sukaratva ādi guṇavatā cirataram anuṣṭhitena jñāna yoga vyavadhānam antareṇa api ātma avalokanam sidhyati karma yoga īpya samarthaḥ tu vikalam api karma yogam ārabheta na iha abhikramanā aśosti pratyavāyaḥ  na vidyate su alpam api asya dharmasya trāyate mahataḥ  bhayāt  ityādibhiḥ vaiṅkalya viccheda ādi saṃbhavepi phala avinābhā  ādi pratipādanāt  prakrama mātreṇa api prasannaḥ  bhagavān pauṣkalyam āpādayati sarveṣu ca amīṣu parvasu tad tad sāmagrī cakra ghaṭanāya tad tad phala pradānāya ca sa eva hi śaraṇam anusaraṇīyaḥ tathā ca āmananti sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti sa eva parama puruṣaḥ  vaśī kārya kāṣṭhā parama prāpyaḥ ca iti arthaḥ tasya ca vaśīkaraṇam tad śaraṇa āgatiḥ eva iti bhāṣyam evam hitatamasya upāsanasya diś mātram darśitam phalam ca apa varga rūpam prāk eva lakṣitam anyeṣām tu deha viccheda mātra sahasra yuvati saṃbhoga samasta alīka viṣaya vijñāna saṃtāna uccheda vāsanā atyanta virāma viṣaya uparāga vaidhurya nitya ūrdhva gamana sak niḥśreyasa vikalpā deha ādi atirikta ātma sadbhāva bāhya artha pāramārthikatva tad tad āgama aprāmāṇya brahma nirvikāratva nirdeṣatva tad jñāna ānanda nityatva ādi samarthakaiḥ śārīraka paryantaiḥ śāstraiḥ pratikṣepyā iti tatra tatra vistaraḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ iha tu pramāṇa cintāyāḥ parama prayojanam darśayitum prameyasya saṃgraha uktiḥ sa parikara pramāṇa maryādā pratipādana para tvāt nyāya vistara śāstrasya iti svātantryeṇa mitam sukha itara tayā yad bhāti jantoḥ idam sarvam yasya vibhūtiḥ ivī avasitam svādam vyanakti svakam antar sva antam ananta nandathu nidhiḥ medaḥ dṛśām mādṛśā mā āvirbhāvayatu svayam sa bhagavān ātmānam ātma īśvaraḥ yatra udāsata jaimini prabhṛtayaḥ śruti artha cintā parāḥ yasyām kandalayanti manda matayaḥ pāriplavān viplavān viśveṣām iha veṅkaṭeśa viduṣā viśrāntaye vādinām prācī nītiṣu paryaśodhi saraṇiḥ pracchāya niṣkaṇṭakā śuddhim bibhrati mādṛśām bhaṇitayaḥ cūḍa anvaye kevalam prānte miśram abhāṇi nīti nipuṇaiḥ kim teṣu amantavya tā yuktam varga yuge vimṛśya saradhā puṣpa kramam yauktikai raṅgīkartum aśakya nihnava guṇa granthaḥ  nibandhaḥ  mama nirūḍha nigama traye nikhila loka cintāmaṇau prasattim upaseduṣi praṇidadhāna bhāva āspade ratim bhajati bhāvanā layam iva upayāti drutam rama avasu matī saha ācarita dharmaṇi brahmaṇi iti śrī kavi tārkika siṃhasya sarva tantra svatantrasya śrīmat veṅkaṭa nāthasya vedānta ācāryasya kṛtiṣu nyāya pariśuddhau prameya adhyāye dvitīyam āhnikam
